NKA_2.82–2.83	 śarīra saṅkṣobha śrama janita nidrāṇām prāṇinām āyuḥ paripāka krama sampādana eka prayojana śvāsa santāna anuvṛtti vat mahābhūta samplava saṅkṣobha labdha saṃskārāṇām paramāṇūnām manda taratamādi bhāvena kāla avaccheda eka prayojanasya pracaya ākhya saṃyoga paryantasya karma santānasya īśvara niḥśvasitasya anuvṛtteḥ kiyānasau= iti atra avirodhāt āgama prasiddhim anatikramya tāvantam eva kālam iti anumanyate brahmāṇḍa antara vyavahāraḥ vā kāla upādhiḥ tad avacchinne kāle punar sargaḥ yathā khalu alābula tāyām vitatāni phalāni tathā parameśvara śaktau= anusyūtāni sahasraśas aṇḍāni iti śrūyate evam viccheda sambhave kasya kena parigrahaḥ yatas prāmāṇyam syāt jñāpakaḥ ca ayam arthaḥ na kārakaḥ tatas kāraka abhāvāt nivartamānam kāryam jñāpaka abhimataḥ kathaṅkāram āsthāpayet 
NKA_2.84	 syāt etat santi kapila ādayaḥ eva sākṣātkṛta dharmāṇaḥ karma yoga siddhāḥ te evam saṃsāra aṅgāreṣu pacyamānān prāṇinaḥ paśyantaḥ parama kāruṇikāḥ priya hita upadeśena anugrahīṣyanti kṛtam parameśvareṇa anapekṣita kīṭa ādi saṅkhyā parijñānavatā iti ced na tat anyasmin= anāśvāsāt tathā hi atīndriya artha darśana upāyaḥ māvana iti abhyupagame api na asau satyam eva sākṣātkāram utpādayati yatas samāśvasimaḥ pramāṇa antara saṃvādāt iti ced na ahiṃsā ādi hita sādhanam iti atra tad abhāvāt āgamaḥ asti iti ced na bhāvanā mātra mūla tvena tasya api anāśvāsa viṣaya tvāt eka deśa saṃvādena api pravṛttiḥ iti ced na svapna ākhyāna vat anyathā api sambhavāt na ca anupalabdhe bhāvanā api cora sarpa ādayaḥ hi upalabdhāḥ eva bhīrubhiḥ bhāvyante 
NKA_2.85	 na ca karma yogayoḥ hita sādhana tvam kutaścid upalabdham na ca etayoḥ sva rūpeṇa upalambhaḥ kvacid upayujyate bhāvanā sādhyaḥ vā na ca asmin= anvaya vyatirekau sambhavataḥ deha antara yogya tvāt phalasya apratīta tayā tad anuṣṭhāne tad abhāvāt ca na ca kartṛ bhoktṛ rūpa ubhaya deha pratisandhānāt eva tat upapadyate tad abhāvāt na hi etasya pūrva karmaṇaḥ phalam idam anubhavāmi iti kaścid pratisandhatteḥ 
NKA_2.86	 kecid tathā bhaviṣyanti iti sambhāvanā mātre api anāśvāsāt vinigamanāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt pratipad ni śītha nidrāṇa prātar pratibuddha samasta upādhyāya vat anyonya saṃvādāt kapila ādiṣu samāśvāsaḥ iti ced na eka janma pratisandhāna vat janma antara pratisandhāne pramāṇa abhavāt tathā api ca adhikāri viśeṣeṇa brāhmaṇa tva ādi apratisandhāne anuṣṭhāna rūpasya āśvāsasya abhāvāt na hi pūrva janmani mātā pitroḥ brāhmaṇyāt tat uttaratra brāhmaṇyam iti niyamaḥ yena sarga ādau varṇa ādi dharma vyavasthā syāt īśvara vat adṛṣṭa viśeṣa upanibaddha bhūta viśeṣa anupalambhāt atīndriya artha darśi tve ca anāśvāsasya ukta tvāt 
NKA_2.87–2.88	 etena brahmāṇḍa antara sañcāri varṇa vyavasthayā sampradāya pravartanam apāḥ tam sañcāra śakteḥ abhāvāt varṣa antara sañcaraṇam eva hi duṣkaram kutas loka antara sañcāraḥ kutastarām ca brahmāṇḍa antara gamanam  aṇima ādi sampatteḥ evam api syāt iti ced na atra api pramāṇa abhāvāt sambhāvanā mātreṇa samāśvāsa anupapatteḥ atha mahā jana parigrahāni atha anupapattiḥ eva atra pramāṇam iti ced na evambhūta eka kalpanayā eva upapattau bhūyas kalpanāyāḥ gaurava prasaṅgāt videha nirmāṇa śkteḥ aṇima ādi vibhūteḥ ca avaśya abhyupagantavya tvāt astu ekaḥ eva iti ced na tarhi īśvaram antareṇa anyatra samāśvāsaḥ iti kāram kāramalaukikā adbhuta mayam māyā vaśāt saṃharan hāram hāram api indra jālam iva yaḥ kurvan jagat krīḍati tam devam niravagraha sphurat abhidhyāna anubhāvam bhavam viśvāsa eka bhuvam śivam prati naman bhūyāsamantyeṣu api 
NKA_3.1–3.2	 nanu etat api katham tatra bādhaka sadbhāvāt tathā hi yadi syāt upalabhyeta ayogya tvāt san= api na upalabhyate iti ced evam tarhi śaśa śṛṅgam api ayogya tvāt na upalabhyate iti syāt na etat evam śṛṅgasya yogya tayā eva vyāpta tvāt iti ced cetanasya api yogyā upādhimat tayā eva vyāpta tvāt tad bādhe saḥ api bādhitaḥ eva iti tulyam vyāpaka sva artha ādi anupalambhena api anumīyate nīsti iti kaḥ hi prayojanam antareṇa kiñcid kuryāt iti ucyate yogyā dṛṣṭiḥ kutas ayogye pratibandiḥ kutastarām kva ayogyam bādhyate śṛṅgam kva anumānam anāśrayam 
NKA_3.3–3.4	 sva ātmā eva tāvat yogyā anupalabdhyā pratiṣiddhum na śakyate kutas tu ayogyaḥ para ātmā tathā hi suṣupti avasthāyām ātmānam anupalabhamānaḥ na asti iti avadhārayet kasya aparādhenapunar yogyaḥ api ātmā tadānīm na upalabhyate sāmagrī vaiguṇyāt jñāna ādi kṣaṇika guṇa upadhāne hi ātmā gṛhyate iti asya svabhāvaḥ jñānam eva kutas na jāyate iti cintyate paścāt vā katham utpatsyate iti ced manasaḥ anindriya pratyāsanna tayā jananāt tad pratyāsattau ca paścāt jananāt manaḥ vaibhava vādinām idam asaṃmatam tathā hi manaḥ vibhu sarvadā sparśa rahita dravya tvāt viśeṣa guṇa śūnya dravya tvāt nitya tve sati anārambhaka dravya tvāt jñāna asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga ādhāra tvāt ityādeḥ iti ced 
NKA_3.5	 na sarveṣām āpātatas svarūpa asiddha tvāt tathā hi yadi rūpa ādi upalabdhīnām kriyā tvena karaṇa tayā manaḥ anumitiḥ na tadā dravya tva siddhiḥ adravyasya api karaṇa tvāt atha āsām eva sākṣātkāritaya indriya tvena tad anumātavyam tathā api vyāpakasya nirupādheḥ na indriya tvam iti upādhiḥ vaktavyaḥ tatra yadi karṇa śaṣkulī vat nipata śarīra avayavasya upādhi tvam tadā tāvat mātre vṛtti lābhaḥ tad doṣe ca vṛtti nirodhaḥ śrotra vat prasajyeta tatas śarīra mātram upādhiḥ abhidheyaḥ tathā ca tad avacchedena vṛtti lābhe śirasi me vedanā pāde me sukham iti ādya vyāpya vṛtti tva pratīti virodhaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa anurodhena vibhu kāryāṇām prādeśika tva niyamāt śarīra tad avayava ādi paramāṇu paryanta upādhi kalpanāyām kalpanā gaurava prasaṅgaḥ niyama anupapattiḥ ca iti tatas anyat eva ekam sūkṣmam upādhi tvena atīndriyam kalpanīyam tathā ca tasya eva indriya tve svābhāvike adhika kalpanāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt dharmi grāhaka pramāṇa bādhaḥ 
NKA_3.6–3.7	 atha jñāna krameṇa indriya sahakāri tayā tad anumānam tatas sutarām prāc ukta doṣaḥ yadi ca manasaḥ vaibhave api adṛṣṭa vaśāt kramaḥ upapādyeta tadā manasaḥ asiddheḥ āśraya asiddhiḥ eva vaibhava hetūnām iti atha yatra adṛṣṭasya dṛṣṭa kāraṇa upahāreṇa upayogaḥ tatra tad pūrṇa tāyām kāryam utpadyate eva anyathā antya tantu saṃyogebhyaḥ api kadācid paṭaḥ na jāyota jātaḥ api vā kadācid nirguṇaḥ syāt balavat tā kulālena dṛḍha daṇḍa nunnam api cakram na bhrāmyeta yatra tu dṛṣṭa anupahāreṇa adṛṣṭa vyāpāraḥ tatra tad vaiguṇyāt kāryān udayaḥ yathā paramāṇu karmaṇaḥ tat iha api yadi viṣaya indriya ātmanām samavadhānam eva jñāna hetuḥ tadā tad sadbhāve sadā eva kāryam syāt na hi etat atiriktam api adṛṣṭasya upaharaṇīyam asti na ca sadā eva jñāna udayaḥ tatas atiriktam apekṣitavyam tat ca yadi apisarvāṇi eva indriyāṇi vyapnoti tathā api karaṇa dharma tvena kriyā kramaḥ saṅgacchate akalpite tu tasminnāyam nyāyaḥ pratipad tuḥ akaraṇa tvāt cakṣuḥ ādīnām aneka tvāt iti ced 
NKA_3.8–3.9	 nanu evam api yugapad jñānāni mā bhūvan yugapad jñānam tu kena vāryate bhavati eva samūha ālambanam ekam jñānam iti ced na eka indriya grahyeṣu iva nānā indriya grāhyeṣu api prasaṅgāt teṣu api bhavati eva iti ced na vyāsaṅga kāle jñāna krameṇa vivāda viṣaye krama anumānāt bubhutsā viśeṣeṇa vyāsaṅge kriyā kramaḥ iti ced mā evam na hi eṣa bubhutsāyā mahimā yat abubhutsite viṣaye jñāna sāmagryām satyām api na jñānam api tu na tatra saṃskāra atiśaya ādhāyakaḥ pratyayaḥ syāt yadi tu abubhutsite viṣaye sāmagrīm eva sā nirundhyāt ghaṭāya unmīlitam cakṣuḥ paṭam na eva darśayet tasmāt bubhutsāpi indriya antarāt ākṛṣya bubhutsita artha grāhiṇī indriye manaḥ niveśayantī yugapad jñāna anutpattau= upayujyate na tu svarūpataḥ 
NKA_3.10	 vibhunaḥ api manasaḥ vyāpāra kramāt kramaḥ iti ced na tasya saṃyoga atiriktasya karma rūpa tve vaibhava virodhāt guṇa rūpa tve nityasya krama anupapatteḥ anityasya ca nitya eka guṇasya avibhu dravya saṃyoga asamavāyikāraṇaka tvena tad antareṇa anupapatteḥ tat api kalpayiṣyate iti ced tat eva tarhi manaḥ sthāne niveśyatām lāghavāya tasmāt aṇu eva manaḥ iti 
NKA_3.11	 tathā ca tasmin= anindriya pratyāsanne nirupadhāna tvāt ātmanaḥ suṣupti avasthāyām anupalambhaḥ etat eva manasaḥ śīlam iti kutas niścirtam iti ced anvaya vyatirekābhyām na kevalam tasya kim tu sarveṣām eva indriyāṇām na hi viśeṣa guṇam anapekṣya cakṣuḥ ādi apidravye pravartate svapna avasthāyām katham jñānam iti ced tad tad saṃskāra udbodhe viṣaya smaraṇena svapna vibhramāṇām utpatteḥ udbodhaḥ eva katham iti ced mandataratamādi nyāyena bāhyānām eva śabda ādīnām upalambhāt antatas śarīrasya eva ūṣma ādeḥ pratipatteḥ yadā ca manaḥ tvacam api parihṛtya purītati vartate tadā suṣuptiḥ 
NKA_3.12	 syāt etat para ātmā tu katham parasya ayogyaḥ na hi sākṣātkāri jñāna viṣaya tām eva ayam na prāpnoti svayam api adarśana prasaṅgāt na api grahītuḥ eva ayam aparādhaḥ tasya api hi jñāna samavāyi kāraṇa tā eva tad yoga tā na api karaṇasya sādhāraṇa tvāt na hi āsaṃsāram ekam eva manaḥ ekam eva ātmānam gṛhṇāti iti atra niyāmakam asti svabhāvaḥ iti ced tarhi muktau niḥsvabhāvat tva prasaṅgaḥ tad eka artha tāyāḥ apāyāt iti na bhojaka adṛṣṭa upagrahasya niyāmaka tvāt yat hi manaḥ yat śarīram yāni indriyāṇi yasya adṛṣṭena ākṛṣṭāni tāni tasya eva iti niyamaḥ tat uktam prāk pratyātma niyamāt bhukteḥ iti etena para buddhi ādayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ 
NKA_3.13	 tat evam yogyā anupalabdhiḥ para ātma ādau na asti tad itarā tu na bādhikā iti tava api saṃmatam atas kim adhikṛtya pratibandiḥ na hi śaśa śṛṅgam ayogya anupalabdhyā kaścid niṣedhati na ca prakṛte yogyā anupalabdhim kaścid manyate atha ayam āśayaḥ ayogya śaśaśṛṅga ādau= anupalabdhiḥ na bādhikā syāt iti tatas kim tad siddhyet iti ced evam astu yadi pramāṇam asti paśutva ādikam iti ced para sādhane pratibandiḥ tarhi na tad bādhane tatra eva bhaviṣyati iti ced tat kim tatra pratibandiḥ eva dūṣaṇam atha kathañcid tulya nyāya tayā yogyāḥ eva parātma buddhi ādayaḥ te ca bādhitāḥ eva iti apahṛta viṣaya tvam na prathamaḥ avyāpteḥ na hi paśutva ādeḥ śaśaśṛṅga sādhaka tvena kārya tva ādeḥ kartṛ mat tva sādhaka tvam pyāptam yena tasmin= asati tat pratiṣiddhyeta na dvitīyaḥ mithas anupalabhyamāna tvasya vādi prativādi svīkārāt tathā api paśu tva ādau kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced na jīnīmaḥ tāvat tad vicāra avasare cintayiṣyāmaḥ 
NKA_3.14	 syāt etat yad pramāṇa gamyam hi yat tad abhāvaḥ eva tasya abhāvam āvedayati yathā rūpa ādi prati patteḥ abhāvaḥ cakṣuḥ ādeḥ abhāvam kāya vāc vyāpāra eka pramāṇakaśya para ātmā tad abhāvaḥ eva tasya abhāve pramāṇam aṅkura ādiṣu tat na tad eka pramāṇaka tva asiddheḥ anyathā suṣuptaḥ api na syāt śvāsa santānaḥ api tatra pramāṇam iti ced na niruddha pavanaḥ api na syāt kāya saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ api tatra pramāṇam iti ced na viṣa mūrcchitaḥ api na syāt śarīra ūṣma api tatra pramāṇam iti ced na jala avasikta viṣa mūrcchitaḥ api na syāt tasmāt yat yat kāryam upalabhyate tad tad anuguṇaḥ cetanaḥ tatra tatra siddhyati na ca kārya mātrasya kvacid vyāvṛttiḥ iti na ca tvad abhyupagatena eva pramāṇena bhavitavyam na anyena iti niyamaḥ asti 
NKA_3.15–3.16	 na ca prameyasya pramāṇena vyāptiḥ sā hi kārtsnyena vā syāt eka deśena vā syāt na prathamaḥ pratyakṣa ādi anyatama asadbhāve api tat prameya avasthiteḥ na dvitīyaḥ puruṣa niyamena sarva pramāṇa vyāvṛttau= api prameya avasthiteḥ aniyamena asiddheḥ na hi sarvasya sarvadā sarvathā atra pramāṇam na asti iti niścayaḥ śakyaḥ iti katham tarhi cakṣuḥ ādeḥ abhāvaḥ niścayaḥ vyāpaka anulabdheḥ carama sāmagrī niveśinaḥ hi kāryam eva vyāpakam tad nivṛttau tathābhūta anyāpi nivṛttiḥ yogya tā mātrasya kadācid kāryam tad nivṛttau tathābhūtasya api nivṛttiḥ anyathā tatra api sandehaḥ 
NKA_3.17	 prakṛte api vyāpaka an upalabdhyā tat pratiṣedhaḥ astu na āśraya asiddha tvāt na hi īśvaraḥ tat jñānam vā kvacid siddham ābhāsa pratipannam iti ced na tasya āśraya tva anupapattaḥ pratiṣedhya tva anupapatteḥ ca vyāvartya abhāva vat tā eva bhāvikī hi viśeṣyatā abhāva viraha ātma tvam vastunaḥ pratiyogitā na ca etad ābhāsa pratipannasya asti iti kutas tasya niṣedha adhikaraṇa tvam niṣedhyatā ca iti 
NKA_3.18	 katham tarhi śaśaśṛṅgasya niṣedhaḥ na kathañcid sa hi abhāva pratyayaḥ eva na ca ayam apāramārthika pratiyogikaḥ paramārtha abhāvaḥ nāma tathā pāramārthika viṣayam pramāṇam nāma iti api ca duṣṭa upalambha sāmagrī śaśaśṛṅga ādi yogya tā na tasyām na upalambhaḥ asti na asti sa anupalambhane kena ca śaśa śaṅgam pratiṣiddhyate sarvathā anupalabdhasya yogya tva asiddheḥ tad itara sāmagrī sākalyam hi tat nanu uktam ābhāsa upalabdham hi tat atas eva aśakya niṣedham iti uktam anupalambha kāle ābhāsa upalambha sāmagryāḥ abhāvāt tad kāle ca anupalambha abhāvāt iti kaḥ tarhi śaśaśṛṅgam na asti iti asya arthaḥ śaśe adhikaraṇe viṣāṇa abhāvaḥ asti iti 
NKA_3.19	 syāt etat yadi api īśvaraḥ na avagataḥ yadi api ca na ābhāsa siddhena pramāṇa vyavahāraḥ śakya sampādanaḥ tathā api ātmanaḥ siddhāḥ teṣām sārvajñyam niṣiddhyate kṣiti ādi kartṛ tvam ca iti tathā hi mad itare na sarvajñāḥ cena tvāt aham iva na ca te kṣiti ādi kartāraḥ puruṣa tvāt aham iva evam vastu tva ādeḥ api iti tat etat api prāk eva parihṛtam tathā hi 
NKA_3.20	 iṣṭa siddhiḥ prasiddha īśe hetu asiddhiḥ agocare na anyā sāmānyatas siddhiḥ jātau= api tathā eva sā pramāṇa pratītānām cetanānām pakṣīkaraṇe siddha sādhanam tatas anyeṣām asiddhau hetoḥ āśraya asiddha tvam ātma tva mātreṇa saḥ api siddhaḥ iti ced kaḥ asya arthaḥ kim ātma tvena upalakṣitā sā eva vastu gatyā sarvajña viśva kartṛ vyaktiḥ atha tad anyā ātma mātram ātma tva mātram eva vā pakṣaḥ sarvatra pūrva doṣān ativṛtteḥ atha ayam āśayaḥ ātma tvam na sarvajña sarva kartṛ vyakti samavetam jāti tvāt go tva vat iti tat asat niṣedhya asiddheḥ niṣedhasya aśakya tvāt tathā ca aprasiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ pakṣaḥ iti āśraya asiddhiḥ iti saḥ eva doṣaḥ tvad upagata āgama loka prasiddhasya eva īśvarasya asarvajña tvam akartṛ tvam ca sādhyate iti ced na āgama ādeḥ pramāṇa tve bādhanāt aniṣedhanam ābhāsa tve tu sā eva syāt āśrayā siddhiḥ uddhatā nigada vyākhyātam etat 
NKA_3.21	 cārvākaḥ tu āha kim yogya tā viśeṣa agraheṇa yat na upalabhyate tat na asti viparītam asti na ca īśvara ādayaḥ tathā tatas na santi iti etat eva jyāyaḥ evam anumāna ādi vilopaḥ iti ced na idam aniṣṭam tathā ca loka vyavahāra ucchedaḥ iti ced na sambhāvanā mātreṇa tad siddheḥ saṃvādena ca prāmāṇya abhimānāt iti atra ucyate 
NKA_3.22	 dṛṣṭi adṛṣṭyoḥ kva sandehaḥ bhāva abhāva viniścayāt adṛṣṭi bādhite hetau pratyakṣam api durlabham sambhāvanā hi sandehaḥ eva tasmāt ca vyavahāraḥ tasmin sati syāt saḥ eva tu kutas darśana daśāyām bhāva niścayāt adarśana daśāyāma bhāva avadhāraṇāt tathā ca gṛhāt bahis gataḥ cārvākaḥ varākaḥ na nivartate pratyuta putra dāra dhana ādi a bhāva avadhāraṇāt sa uraḥ tāḍam śoka vikalaḥ vikrośet smaraṇa anubhavān na evam iti ced na pratiyogi smaraṇaḥ eva abhāva paricchedāt parāvṛttaḥ api katham punar āsādayiṣyati sattvāt iti ced anupalambha kāle api tarhi santi iti na tāvat mātreṇa abhāva avadhāraṇam tadā eva utpannāḥ iti ced na anupalambhena hetūnām bādhāt abādhe vā saḥ eva doṣaḥ 
NKA_3.23–3.24	 atas eva pratyakṣam api na syāt tad hetūnām cakṣuḥ ādīnām anupalambha bādhita tvāt upalabhyante eva golaka ādi rūpa tvāt teṣām iti ced na tad upalabdheḥ pūrvam teṣām anupalambhāt na ca yaugapadya niyamaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt iti etena na paramāṇavaḥ santi anupalabdheḥ na te nityāḥ niravayavāḥ vā pārthiva tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat na pāthasīya paramāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ nityāḥ rūpa ādi tvāt dṛśyamāna rūpa ādi vat na rūpa tva pārthiva tva ādi nitya akārya atīndriya samavāyi jāti tvāt śṛṅga tva vat na indriyāṇi santi yogyā anupalabdheḥ ayogyāni ca śaśaśṛṅga pratibandi nirasanīyāni iti evam svarga apūrva devatā nirākaraṇam nāstikānām nisanīyam mīmāṃsakaḥ ca toṣayitavyaḥ bhīṣayitavyaḥ ca iti 
NKA_3.25–3.26	 yadi evam anupalambhena adṛśya pratiṣedhaḥ na iṣyate anupalabhya upādhi pratiṣedhaḥ api naiṣṭavyaḥ tathā ca katham tathābhūta artha siddhiḥ api anumāna bīja pratibandha asiddheḥ tad abhāve śabda ādeḥ api abhāvaḥ prāmāṇya asiddheḥ sā iyam ubhayatas pāśāḥ rajjuḥ atra kaścid āha mā bhūt upādhi vidhūnanam catur pañca rūpa sampatti mātreṇa eva pratibandha nirvāhāt tasya āśya sa pakṣa āsa pakṣa darśana adarśana mātra pramāṇaka tvāt yatra tu tad bhaṅgaḥ tatra pramāṇa bhaṅgaḥ api āvaśyakaḥ na hi asti sambhavaḥ darśana adarśanayoḥ aviplave hetu rūpa viplava eti 
NKA_3.27	 aprayojakaḥ api tarhi hetuḥ syāt iti ced bhūyas darśana aviplave kaḥ ayam aprayojakaḥ nāma na tāvat sādhyam pratyakāryam akāraṇam vā sāmānyatas dṛṣṭa anumāna svīkārāt na api sāmagryām kāraṇa eka deśaḥ pūrvavat abhyupagamāt na api vyabhicārī tad anupalambhāt vyabhicāra upalambhe vā saḥ eva doṣaḥ na ca śaṅkita vyabhicāraḥ nirbīja śaṅkāyāḥ sarvatra sulabha tvāt na api vyāpya antara saha vṛttiḥ ekatra api sādhye aneka sādhana upagamāt na api alpa viṣayaḥ dhūma ādeḥ tathā abhāve api hetu tvāt nanu dhūmaḥ vahni mātre aprayojakaḥ eva tad nivṛttau= api tat anivṛtteḥ ārdra indhanava tvam vahni viśeṣam prati tu prayojakaḥ tad nivṛttau tasya eva nivṛtteḥ iti etat api ayuktam sāmānya prayojaka tāyām viśeṣa sādhaka tva ayogāt tad asiddhau tasya asiddhi niyamāt siddhau vā sāmānya viśeṣa bhāva anupapatteḥ na api kpta sāmarthye anyasmin kalpanīya sāmarthyā prayojakaḥ nāśe kāryatva sāvayava tvayoḥ api hetu bhāvāt iti 
NKA_3.28–3.29	 tat etat apeśalam katham hi viśeṣa abhāvāt kaścid vyabhicarati kaścid ca na iti śkayam avagantum tatas nirṇāyaka abhāve sati sāhitya darśanam eva śaṅkā bījam iti kva asau nirbījāḥ evam sati atiprasaktiḥ api cārvāka nandinī na upālambhāya svabhāvāt eva kaścid kiñcid vyabhicarati kaścid ca na iti svabhāvaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ iti ced kena cihnena punar asau nirṇeyaḥ iti nipuṇena bhāvanīyam bhūyas darśanasya śataśas pravṛttasya api bhaṅga darśanāt yatra bhaṅgaḥ na dṛśyate tat tathā iti ced āpātatas na dṛśyate iti sarvatra kāla krameṇa api na drakṣyate iti kaḥ niyantā iti 
NKA_3.30	 tasmāt upādhi tad virahau= eva vyabhicāra avi abhicāra nivandhanam tad avadhāraṇam ca aśakyam iti nanu yaḥ sarvaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ sarvadā asmad ādibhiḥ yadvat tayā na upalabhyate na asau tadvān yathā bakaḥ śyamikayā na upalabhyate ca vahnau dhūmaḥ upādhimattayā iti śkyam iti ced na asya api anumāna tayā tad apekṣāyām anavasthānāt sarva adṛṣṭeḥ ca sandehāt svādṛṣṭeḥ vyabhicārātaḥ sarva dā itya siddheḥ 
NKA_3.31	 tādātmya tad utpattibhyām niyamaḥ iti anye tatra tādātmyam vipakṣe bādhakāt bhavati tad utpattiḥ ca paurvāparyeṇa pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām na hi evam sati śaṅkā apiśācī avakāśam āsādayati āśaṅkyamāna kāraṇa bhāvasya api piśāca ādeḥ etat lakṣaṇa avirodhena eva tattva nirvāhāt iti na evam api ubhaya gāminaḥ avyabhicāra nibandhanasya ekasya avivecanāt pratyekam ca avyāpaka tvāt kutas ca kārya ātmānau kāraṇam ātmānam ca na vyabhicārate iti 
NKA_3.32–3.33	 atra ucyate śaṅkā ced anumā asti eva na ced śaṅkā tatas tarām vyāghāta avadhiḥ āśaṅkā tarkaḥ śaṅkā avadhiḥ mataḥ kāla antare kadācid vyabhicariṣyati iti kālam bhāvinam ākalayya śaṅkyeta tadākalanam ca na anumānam avadhīrya kasyacid mūhūrtayāmāhorātra pakṣa māsa ṛtu ayana saṃvatsara ādayaḥ hi bhāvinaḥ bhavat muhūrta ādi anumeyāḥ eva anavagateṣu smaraṇasya api anāśaṅkanīya tvāt anākalane vā kam āśritya vyabhicāraḥ śaṅkyeta tathā ca sutarām anumāna svīkāraḥ evam ca deśa antare api vaktavyam 
NKA_3.34–3.35	 svīkṛtam anumānam suhṛd bhāvena pṛcchāmaḥ katham āśaṅkā nivartanīyā iti ced na yāvat āśaṅkam tarka pravṛtteḥ tena hi vartamānena upādhi koṭau tad āyatta vyabhicāra koṭau vā aniṣṭam upanayatā icchā vicchidyate vicchanna vipakṣa icchaḥ ca pramātā bhūyas darśana upalabdha sāhacaryam liṅga gamana ākulaḥ adhitiṣṭhati adhiṣṭhitāt ca karaṇāt kriyā pariniṣpattiḥ iti kim anupapannam 
NKA_3.36	 nanu tarkaḥ api avinābhāvam apekṣya pravartate tatas anavasthayā bhavitavyam na śaṅkāyāḥ vyāghāta a= adhi tvāt tat eva hi āśaṅkyate yasmin= āśaṅkyamāne sva kriyā vyāghāta ādayaḥ doṣāḥ na avataranti iti loka maryādā na hi hetu phala bhāvaḥ na bhaviṣyati iti śaṅkitum api śakyate tathā sati śaṅkā eva na syāt sarvam mithyā bhaviṣyati ityādi vat 
NKA_3.37	 atha avyatīndriya upādhi niṣedhe kim pramāṇam iti ucyatām iti ced na vai kaścid atīndriya upādhiḥ pramāṇa siddhaḥ asti yasya abhāve pramāṇam anveṣaṇīyam kevalam sāhacarye nibandhana antara mātram śaṅkyate tatas śaṅkā eva phalatas sva rūpataḥ ca nivartanīyāḥ tatra phalam asyāḥ vipakṣasya api jijñāsā tarkāt āhanya nivartate tatas anumāna pravṛttau śaṅkā svarūpam api iti sarvam sustham 
NKA_3.38–3.39	 na ca etat anāgamam nyāya aṅga tayā tarkam vyutpādayataḥ sūtrakārasya abhimata tvāt anyathā tat vyutpādana vaiyarthyāt tat ayam saṅkṣepaḥ yatra anukūla tarkaḥ na asti saḥ aprayojakaḥ sa ca dvividhaḥ śaṅkita upādhiḥ niścata upādhiḥ ca yatra idam ucyate yāvat ca avyatireki tvam śata aṃśena api śaṅkyate vipakṣasya kutas tāvat hetoḥ gamanikā balam 
NKA_3.40–3.41	 tatra upādhiḥ tu sādhana avyāpaka tve sati sādhya vyāpakaḥ tad dharma bhūtā hi vyāptiḥ japā kusuma rakta tā iva sphaṭike sādhana abhimate cakāsti iti upādhiḥ asau= ucyate iti tat idam āhuḥ anye para prayuktānām vyāptīnām upajīvakāḥ taiḥ dṛṣṭaiḥ api na eva iṣṭā vyapaka aṃśa avadhāraṇāḥ iti tat anena vipakṣa daṇḍa bhūtena tarkeṇa sanāthe bhūyas darśane kāryam vā kāraṇam vā tatas anyat vā samavāyi vā saṃyogi vā anyathā vā bhāvaḥ vā abhāvaḥ vā sa viśeṣaṇam vā nirviśeṣaṇam vā liṅgam iti niḥśaṅkam avadhāraṇīyam anyathā tad ābhāse iti rahasyam 
NKA_3.42–3.43	 tādātmya tad utpattyoḥ api etat eva bījam yadi hi kāya ātmānau kāraṇam ātmānam ca atipatetām tadā tayoḥ tattvam vyāhanyeta atas eva sāmagrī niveśinaḥ carama kāraṇāt api kāryam anumimate saugatāḥ api tasmāt vipakṣa bādhakam eva pratibandha lakṣaṇam tathā hi śāka ādi āhāra pariṇati virahiṇi mitra atanaye na kiñcid aniṣṭam iti na asau tasya vyāpikā vyāpikā tu śyāmikāyāḥ kāraṇatva avadhāraṇāt kāraṇam ca tat tasya tat atipatya bhavati ca iti vyāhatam evam anyatra api ūhanīyam iti 
NKA_3.44	 kva punar aprayojakaḥ antarbhavati na kvacid iti eke yathā hi siddha sādhanam na bādhita viṣayam viṣaya apahāra abhāvāt na api nirṇaye sati pakṣatvā ati pātāt apakṣa dharmaḥ kāla atīta vilopa prasaṅgāt na ca anaikāntika ādiḥ vyabhicāra ādi abhāvāt tathā ayam api sūtram tu upalakṣaṇa param iti tat asat vibhāgasya nyūna adhika saṅkhyā vyavaccheda phala tvāt 
NKA_3.45	 kva tarhi dvayoḥ antar niveśaḥ asiddhe eva tathā hi vyāptasya hi pakṣa dharma tā pratītiḥ siddhiḥ tad abhāvaḥ asiddhi iyam ca vyāpti pakṣa dharmatā svarūpāṇām anyatama apratītyā bhavantī yathāsaṅkhyam anyathā siddhiḥ āśrayā siddhiḥ svarūpa asiddhiḥ iti ākhyāyate madhyamā apya āśraya svarūpa apratītyā tad viśeṣaṇa pakṣatva apratītyā vā iti dvayī tatra carama asiddha sādhanam iti vyapadiśyate vyāpti sthitau pakṣatvasya āhatya vighaṭanāt na tu evam bādhe vyāpteḥ eva prathamam vighaṭanāt iti viśeṣaḥ 
NKA_3.46	 yat tva prayojakaḥ sandigdha anaikāntikaḥ iti anaikāntike antar bhāvyate tat asat vyāpti asiddhyā hi nimittena vyabhicāraḥ śaṅkanīyaḥ anyathā vā prathame asiddhiḥ eva dūṣaṇam upajīvya tvāt na anaikāntikam upajīvaka tvāt anyathā śaṅkā tva t ūṣaṇam eva nirṇīte tad anavakāśāt iti tṛtīya stabake īśvarasya upamāna abādhya tva nirūpaṇam 
NKA_3.47	 upamānam tu bādhakamanāśaṅkanīyam eva viṣayān atirekāt iti kecid tathā hi na tāvat asya viṣayaḥ sādṛśya vyapadeśyam padārtha antaram eva sambhāvanīyam paraspara virodhe hi na prakāra antara sthitiḥ na ekatā api viruddhānāmukti mātra virodhataḥ na hi bhāva abhāvābhyām anyaḥ prakāraḥ sambhāvanīyaḥ paraspara vidhi niṣedha rūpa tvāt na bhāvaḥ iti hi niṣedha mātreṇa eva abhāva vidhiḥ tatas tam vihāya katham sva vacanena eva punar sahṛdayaḥ niṣedhet na abhāvaḥ iti evam na abhāvaḥ iti hi niṣedhaḥ eva bhāva vidhiḥ tatas tam vihāya sva vācā eva anunmattaḥ katham punar niṣedhet na bhāvaḥ iti atas evam bhūtānām eka tāpya śakya pratipattiḥ pratiṣedha vidhyoḥ ekatra asambhavāt tasmāt bhāva abhāvau= eva tattvam 
NKA_3.48	 bhāvat tve api guṇavat nirguṇam vā iti dvayam eva pūrvavat pūrvam dravyam eva uttarañca āśritam anāśritam vā iti dvayam eva pūrvavat tatra uttaram samavāyaḥ eva anavasthā bhayāt āśritam tu sāmānya vat niḥsāmānyañca iti pūrvavat dvayam eva tatra prathamam api spandaḥ aspandaḥ iti dvayam eva etat ca yathāsaṅkhyam karma guṇaḥ iti vyapadiśyate niḥsāmānyam nirguṇam āśritam tu eka āśritam aneka āśritam vā iti prāk iva dvayam eva etat api yathāsaṅkhyam viśeṣaḥ sāmānyañca iti abhidhīyate tat etat sādṛśyam etāsu ekām vidhāma āsādayat na atiricyate anāsādayan= apada arthībhūyas sthātum utsahate etena śakti saṅkhī ā ādayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ tatas abhāvena saha sapta eva padārthāḥ iti niyamaḥ atas na upamāna viṣayor atha antaram iti 
NKA_3.49–3.50	 syāt etat bhavatu sāmānyam eva sādṛśyam tat eva tasya viṣayaḥ syāt tad sadṛśaḥ ayam iti hi pratyayaḥ na indriya janyaḥ tad āpāta mātreṇa anutpatteḥ iti ced na pūrva piṇḍa anu sandhāna rūpa sahakāri vaidhuryeṇa anutpatteḥ prāc ajananāt saḥ ayam iti pratyabhijñāna vat iti nanu etat sadṛśaḥ saḥ iti na indriya janyam tena tasya asambandhāt naca idam smaraṇam tad piṇḍa anubhave api viśiṣṭasya ananubhavāt naca etat api ayam saḥ iti viparīta pratyabhijñāna vat upapādanīyam tad tedanta upasthāpana krama viparyaye api viśeṣyasya indriyeṇa sannikarṣa avirodhāt tasya sannihita vartamāna gocara tvāt prakṛte tu tad abhāvāt tasmāt tad piṇḍa smaraṇa sahāyam etat piṇḍa varti sādṛśya jñānam eva tathāvidham jñānam utpādayat upamānam pramāṇam iti 
NKA_3.51–3.52^1	 etat api na asti sādharmyam iva vaidharmyam mānam evam prasajyate arthāpattiḥ asau vyaktam iti ced prakṛtam na kim yadā hi etad visadṛśaḥ asau iti pratyeti tatra api tulyam etat na hi tat pratyakṣam asannikṛṣṭa viṣaya tvāt na smaraṇam viśiṣṭasya ananubhavāt na upamānam asādṛśya viṣaya tvāt nanu etad dharma abhāva viśiṣṭa tvam eva tasya vaidharmyam tat ca abhāva gamyam eva iṣyate na ca prakṛte api tathā astu sādṛśyasya bhāva rūpa tvāt iti ced na itas vyāvṛtta dharma viśiṣṭa tāyāḥ api vaidharmya rūpa tvāt tasya ca bhāva rūpa tvāt 
NKA_3.51–3.52^2	 syāt etat tad dharmāḥ iha na santi iti avagate arthāt āpadyate iha avidyamānāḥ tatra santi iti na hi tad vidharma tvam etasya upapadyate yadi etat vidharmā asau na bhavati iti ced evam tarhi prakṛtam api artha āpattiḥ eva na hi tad sādṛśya viśiṣṭa tvam etasya pratyakṣa siddham api tasya etat sādṛśya viśiṣṭa tvam vinā upapadyate etena dṛṣṭa āsannikṛṣṭa pratyabhijñānam vyākhyātam tatra api tad dharma śāli tvam tasya smaraṇa abhivyaktam anupapadyamānam tat idanta āspadasya ekatām vyavasthāpayati tasmāt na upamānam adhikam iti 
NKA_3.53	 evam prāpte abhidhīyate sambandhasya paricchedam sañjñāyāḥ sañjñinā saha pratyakṣa ādeḥ asādhya tvāt upamāna phalam viduḥ yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti śruta atideśa vākyasya go sadṛśam piṇḍam anubhavataḥ smarataḥ ca vākya artham ayam asau gavaya śabda vācyaḥ iti bhavati matiḥ sā iyam na tāvat vākya mātra phalam anupalabdha piṇḍasya api prasaṅgāt na api pratyakṣa phalam aśruta vākyasya api prasaṅgāt na api samāhāra phalam vākya pratyakṣayoḥ bhinna kāla tvāt vākya tad arthayoḥ smṛti dvāra upanītau= api gavaya piṇḍa sambaddhena api indriyeṇa tad gata sādṛśya anupalambhe samaya pariccheda asiddheḥ phala samāhāre tu tad antarbhāve anumāna ādeḥ api pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ tat kim tad phalasya tad pramāṇa bahis bhāvaḥ eva antarbhāve vā kiyatī sīmā  tad tad asādhāraṇa indriya ādi sāhityam asti tarhi sādṛśya ādi jñāna kāleviṣphāritasya cakṣuṣaḥ vyāpāraḥ na upalabdha gosādṛśya viśiṣṭa gavaya piṇḍasya vākya tad artha smṛtimataḥ kāla antare api anusandhāna balāt samaya pariccheda upapatteḥ 
NKA_3.54	 nanu ca vākyāt eva anena samayaḥ paricchinnaḥ go sadṛśasya gavaya śabdaḥ sañjñā iti kevalam idānīm pratyabhijānāti ayam asau= iti prayogāt va anumitaḥ yaḥ yatra asati vṛtti antare vṛddhaiḥ prayujyate sa tasya vācakaḥ yathā go śabdaḥ eva goḥ prayujyate ca ayam go sadṛśe iti kim upamānena iti na sādṛśyasya animitta tvāt nimittasya apratītitaḥ samayaḥ durgṛhaḥ pūrvam śabdena anumayā api vā na hi gavaya śabdasya sādṛśyam pravṛtti nimittam apratīta gūnām avyavahāra prasaṅgāt na ca ubhayam api nimittam svayaṃpratīta samaya saṅkrāntaye ati deśa vākya prayoga anupapatteḥ gavayat tve hi ayam vyutpannaḥ vṛddha vyavahārāt na sādṛśye katham etat nirdhāraṇīyam iti ced vastu gatiḥ tāvat iyam tad āpātataḥsandehe api na phala siddhiḥ gandhavat tvam iva pṛthivī tvasya go sādṛśyam gavaya śabda pravṛtti nimittasya upalakṣaṇam idam eva vā nimittam iti anirdhāraṇāt 
NKA_3.55^1	 syāt etat pūrvam nimitta anupalabdheḥ na phala siddhiḥ idānīntu tasmin= upalabdhe tat eva vākyam smṛti samārūḍham phaliṣyati adhyayana samaya gṛhītaḥ iva vedarāśiḥ aṅga upāṅga paryavadātasya kāla antare na ca vācyam vākyena sva arthasya prāk eva bodhita tvāt prāk eva paryavasitam iti go sādṛśyasya upalakṣaṇa nimitta tvayoḥ anyataratra tātparye sandehāt idānīntu gavayatve avagate tarka puraskārāt sādṛśyasya upalakṣaṇa tāyām vyavasthitāyām gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ itivat anvaya pratipattiḥ iti ced na śruta anvayāt anā kāṅkṣam na vākyam hi anyat icchati padārtha anvaya vaidhuryāt tat ākṣiptena saṅgatiḥ 
NKA_3.55^2	 go sadṛśaḥ gavaya śabda vācyaḥ iti sāmānādhikaraṇya mātreṇa anvaya upapattau viśeṣa sandehe api vākyasya paryavasita tvena māna antara upanīta anapekṣaṇāt taktā rakta sandehe api ghaṭaḥ bhavati iti vākya vat anyathā vākya bheda doṣāt na ca gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ iti vat padārthāḥ eva anvaya ayogyāḥ yena pramāṇa antara upanītena anvayaḥ syāt atha pratīta vākya artha bala āyātaḥ api arthaḥ yadi vākyasya eva divā bhojana niṣedha vākyasya api rātri bhojanam arthaḥ syāt tasmāt yathā gavaya śabdaḥ kasyacid vācakaḥ śiṣṭa prayogāt iti sāmānyatas niścite api viśeṣe māna antara apekṣā tathā go sadṛśasya gavaya śabdaḥ vācakaḥ iti vākyāt niścitepi sāmānye viśeṣa vācaka tve asya māna antaram anusaraṇīyam iti 
NKA_3.56	 astu anumānam tathā hi gavaya śabdaḥ gavayasya vācakaḥ asati vṛtti antare abhiyuktaiḥ tatra prayujyamāna tvat gavi go śabda vat iti ced na asiddheḥ na hi asati vṛtti antare tad viṣaya tayā prayogaḥ saṅgatim avijñāya jñātum śakyate sāmānādhikaraṇyāt iti ced na piṇḍa mātre siddha sādhanāt nimitte ca asiddheḥ sādṛśyasya animitta tvāt iti uktam 
NKA_3.57	 nanu vyāpti param idam vākyam syāt yaḥ go sadṛśaḥ sa gavaya padārthaḥ iti tathā ca vākyāt avagata pratibandhaḥ anuminuyāt ayam asau gavayaḥ go sadṛśa tvāditi deśa vākya avagata piṇḍa vat iti na viparyayāt na hi go sadṛśam buddhau= āropya anena pṛṣṭaḥ sa kim śabda vācyaḥ iti kintu sāmānyatas gavaya padārtham avagamya sa kīdṛś iti tathā ca yad yoga prāthamyābhyām tasya eva vyāpya tvam tatas kim tena prakṛta anupayogāt 
NKA_3.58	 atha kiṃlakṣaṇakaḥ asau= iti praśna arthaḥ tadā vyatireki param syāt lakṣaṇasya tathā abhavāt tathā ca go sadṛśaḥ gavayaḥ iti asya arthaḥ yaḥ gavayaḥ iti na vyavahriyate na asau go sadṛśaḥ iti evañca prayoktavyam ayam asau gavayaḥ iti vyavahartavyaḥ go sadṛśa tvāt yaḥ tu na tathā go sadṛśaḥ yathā hastī na ca hasti ādīnām vipakṣa tve pramāṇam asti sarva aprayogasya duravadhāra tvāt katipaya avi avahārasya ca anaikāntika tvāt 
NKA_3.59–3.60^1	 nanu liṅga mātre praśnaḥ bhaviṣyati kīdṛś kim liṅgam iti na na hi anena liṅgam avijñāya gavaya śabdasya vācaka tvam kasyacid vācya tvam vā avagatam yena tad artham praśnaḥ syāt pravṛtti nimitta viśeṣa liṅge praśnaḥ yena nimittena gavaya śabdaḥ pravartate tasya kim liṅgam iti ced na na hi tat avaśyam anumeyam eva iti anena niścitam yatas idam syāt jñāna upāya mātra praśne tad viśeṣeṇa uttaram iti ced na aviśeṣāt indriya sannikarṣam api uttarayet paryāya antaram vā yathā gavayam aham katham jānīyām iti praśne vanam gataḥ drakṣyasi iti yathā vā kaḥ pikaḥ iti atra kokile iti 
NKA_3.59–3.60^2	 tasmāt nimitta bheda praśnaḥ eva ayam gavayaḥ gavaya pada vācyaḥ kīdṛś kena nimittena iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ tasya ca nimitta viśeṣasya sākṣāt upadarśayitum aśkya tvāt pṛṣṭaḥ tad u lakṣaṇam kiñcid ācaṣṭe tat ca upamāna sāmagrī samutthāpanam eva tasya ca pramāṇasya sataḥ tarkaḥ sahāya tām āpadyate sādṛśyasya eva nimitta tāyām kalpanā gauravam nimitta antara kalpane ca kpta kalpyavirodhaḥ iti tat eva nimittam avagacchati iti lakṣaṇantu asya anavagata saṅgati sañjñāsam abhivyāhṛta vākya arthasya sañjñinī anusandhānam upamānam vākya arthaḥ ca kvacid sādharmyam kvacid vaidharmyam atas na avyāpakam tasmāt niyata viṣaya tvāt eva na tena bādhaḥ na tu anatirekāt iti sthitiḥ 
NKA_3.61	 śabdaḥ api na bādhakam anumāna an atirekāt iti vaiśeṣika ādayaḥ tathā hi yadi api ete padārthāḥ mithas saṃsargavantaḥ vākya tvāt iti vyadhikaraṇam padārtha tvāt iti ca anaikāntikam padaiḥ smārita tvāt iti api tathā yadi api ca etāni padāni smārita artha saṃsargavanti tad smāraka tvāt ityādau sādhya abhāvaḥ na hi atra matvarthaḥ saṃyogaḥ samavāyaḥ tādātmyam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ vā sambhavati jñāpyajñāpaka bhāvaḥ tu svātantryeṇa anumāna antarbhāva vādibhiḥ na iṣyate na ca liṅga tayā jñāpaka tvam yat liṅgasya viṣayaḥ tat eva tasya paraspara āśraya prasaṅgāt tad upalambhe hi vyāpti siddhiḥ tad siddhau ca tad anumānam iti tathā api ākāṅkṣa ādimadbhiḥ padaiḥ smārita tvāt gām abhyāja iti padārthavat iti syāt na ca viśeṣa asiddhiḥ deṣaḥ saṃsargasya saṃsṛjyamāna viśeṣāt eva viśiṣṭa tvāt yat vā etāni padāni smārita artha saṃsarga jñāna pūrvakāṇi ākāṅkṣa ādimattve sati tad smāraka tvāt gām abhyāja iti pada vat na ca evam artha asiddhiḥ jñāna avacchedaka tayā eva tad siddheḥ tasya ca saṃsṛjyamāna upahitasya eva avacchedaka tvāt na viśeṣa apratilambhaḥ iti 
NKA_3.62–3.63^1	 atra ucyate anekāntaḥ paricchede sambhave ca na niścayaḥ ākāṅkṣā sat tayā hetuḥ yogyā sattira bandhanā ete padārtha āmithaḥsarṅgavantaḥ iti saṃsṛṣṭāḥ eva iti niyamaḥ vā sādhyaḥ sambhāvita saṃsargāḥ iti vā na prathamaḥ anāpta ukta pada kadamba smāritaiḥ aneka antāt āpta uktyā viśeṣaṇīyam iti ced na vākya artha pratīteḥ prāk tad asiddheḥ na hi avipralambhaka tva mātram iha āpta śabdena vivakṣitam tad ukteḥ api padārtha saṃsarga vyabhicārāt api tu tad anubhava prāmāṇyam api na ca etat śakyam asarva jñe sarvadā sarva viṣaye satya jñānavān ayam iti niścetum bhrānteḥ puruṣa dharma tvāt 
NKA_3.62–3.63^2	 yatra kvacid āpta tvam anāptasya api asti iti na tena upayogaḥ tatas asmin= arthe ayam abhra antaḥ iti kenacid upāyena grāhyam naca etat saṃsarga viśeṣam apratītya śakyam buddheḥ arthaṃbhedam antareṇa nirūpayitum aśakyatvāt padārtha mātre ca abhrānta tva siddhau na kiñcid anāpta sādha araṇyāt eteṣām saṃsarge ayam abhrāntaḥ iti śakyam iti ced na eteṣām saṃsarge iti asyāḥ eva buddheḥ asiddheḥ ananubhūta care smaraṇa ayogāt tad anubhavasya liṅga adhīna tayā tasya ca viśeṣaṇa asiddha tvena anupapatteḥ iti 
NKA_3.64–3.65^1	 na api dvitīyaḥ yogya tā mātra siddhau= api saṃsarga aniścayāt vākyasya ca tad eka phala tvāt yogya tā mātrasya prāk eva siddheḥ anyathā tad asiddhau= āsannasa ākāṅkṣa pada smārita tvāt iti eva hetuḥ syāt tathā ca agninā siñcet ityādinā smāritaiḥ anaikāntaḥ tathāvidhānām sarvathā saṃsarga ayogya tvāt iti evam dvitīye api prayoge hetuḥ ākāṅkṣa ādimattve sati iti tatra kā iyam ākāṅkṣā nāma na tāvat viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ tasya saṃsargaḥ svabhāva tayā sādhya tvāt na api tad yogya tā yogya tayā eva gata artha tvāt na api avinābhāvaḥ nīlam sarojam ityādau tad abhāve api vākya artha pratyayāt tatra api viśeṣa ākṣipta sāmānyayoḥ avinā abhāvaḥ asti iti ced na aho vimalam jalam nadyāḥ kacche mahiṣaḥ carati ityādau vākya bheda anupapatti prasaṅgāt na api pratipattuḥ jijñāsā paṭaḥ bhavati ityādau śukla ādi jijñāsāyām raktaḥ paṭaḥ bhavati iti asya eka deśa vat sarvadā vākya aparyavasāna prasaṅgāt guṇa kriyā ādi aśeṣa viśeṣa jijñāsāyām api padasmārita viśeṣa jijñāsā ākāṅkṣā 
NKA_3.65^2	 paṭaḥ iti ukte kiṃrūpaḥ kutra kim karoti iti ādi rūpa jijñāsā tatra bhavati iti ukte kim karoti iti eṣā eva padasmārita viṣayā na tu kim rūpaḥ ityādiḥ api yadā tu raktaḥ iti ucyate tadā kiṃrūpaḥ iti eṣā api smārita viṣayā syāt iti na kiñcid anupapannaḥ am iti ced evam tarhi cakṣuṣī nimīlya paribhāvayatu bhavān kim asyām jātāyām anvaya pratyayaḥ atha jñātāyām iti tatra prathame na anayā vyabhicāra vyāvartanāya hetuḥ viśeṣaṇīyaḥ manaḥ saṃyoga ādi vat sattā mātreṇa upayogāt āsatti yogya tā mātreṇa viśiṣṭaḥ tu niścitaḥ api na gamakaḥ ayam eti putraḥ rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ apasāryatām ityādau vyabhivacārāt 
NKA_3.66	 dvitīyaḥ tu syāt api yadi anumāna antara vat tat sadbhāve api tad jñāna vaidhuḥ yāt anvaya pratyayaḥ na jāyate na tu etat asti āsatti yogya tā mātra pratisandhānāt eva sa ākāṅkṣasya sarvatra vākya artha pratyayāt nivṛtta ākāṅkṣasya ca tad abhāvāt katham eṣa niścayaḥ sa ākāṅkṣaḥ eva pratyeti na tu jñāta ākāṅkṣaḥ iti ced tāvat mātreṇa upapattau= anupalabhyamāna jñāna kalpanā anupapatteḥ anyatra tathā darśanāt ca yathā hi dūrāt dṛṣṭa sāmānyaḥ jijñāsate kaḥ ayam iti pratyāsīdan= ca sthāṇuḥ ayam iti pratyeti tadā asya jñātum aham icchāmi iti anuvyavasāya abhāve api sthāṇuḥ ayam iti artha pratyayaḥ bhavati tathā iha api aviśeṣāt viśeṣa upasthāna kāle saṃsarga avagatiḥ eva jāyate na tu jijñāsā avagatiḥ iti na ca viśeṣa upasthānāt prāk eva jijñāsā avagatiḥ prakṛta upayoginī tāvat mātra sya anākāṅkṣā tvāt 
NKA_3.67	 na ca evambhūtaḥ api ayam aikāntikaḥ hetuḥ yadā hi ayam eti putraḥ rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ apasāryatām iti vaktā uccārayati śrotā ca vyāsaṅga ādinā nimittena ayam eti putraḥ iti aśru tvā eva rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ apasāryatām iti śṛṇoti tadā asti ākāṅkṣa ādimattve sati pada kadambaka tvam na ca smārita artha saṃsarga jñāna pūrvaka tvam iti 
NKA_3.68	 syāt etat yāvat samabhivyāhṛta tvena viśeṣite hetau na ayam doṣaḥ tathāvidhasya vyabhicāra udāharaṇa asaṃsparśāt kutastyastarhi katipaya pada śrāviṇaḥ saṃsarga pratyayaḥ aliṅgaḥ eva liṅga tva adhyāropāt etāvān eva ayam samabhivyāhāraḥ iti tatra śrotuḥ abhimānaḥ na tad sandehe api śruta anurūpa saṃsarga avagamāt bhavati hi tatra pratyayaḥ na jāne kim aparamanena uktam etāvat eva śrutam yat rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ apasāryatām iti bhrāntiḥ asau= iti ced na tāvat asau duṣṭa indriya jāḥ parokṣa ākāra tvāt na liṅga ābhāsa jāḥ liṅga abhimāna abhāve api jāyamāna tvāt etāvat pada kadamba pratisandhānam eva tām janayati iti ced yadi evam tat eva aduṣṭam sat abhrāntim janayat kena vāraṇīyam vyāpti pratisandhānam vinā api tasya saṃsarga pratyāyane sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt cakṣuḥ ādi vat 
NKA_3.69	 na asti eva tatra saṃsarga pratyayaḥ asaṃsarga āgraha mātreṇa tu tathā vyavahāraḥ iti ced tarhi yāvat samabhivyāhāreṇa api viśeṣaṇena apratīkāraḥ tathābhūtasya anāpta vākyasya saṃsarga jñāna pūrvaka tva abhāvāt asaṃsarga āgraha pūrvakatva mātre sādhye na vyabhicāraḥ iti ced evam tarhi saṃsargaḥ na siddhyet āpta vākyeṣu setsyati iti ced na sarva viṣayā aptatvasya asiddheḥ yatra kvacid āpta tvasya anaikāntika tvāt prakṛta viṣaye ca āptatva siddhau saṃsarga viśeṣasya prāk eva siddhi abhyupagamāt iti uktam 
NKA_3.70	 na ca sarvatra jijñāsā nibandhanam ajijñāsoḥ api vākya artha pratyayāt ākāṅkṣā padārthaḥ tarhi kaḥ jijñāsām prati yogyatā sā ca smārita tad ākṣiptayoḥ avinā abhāve sati śrotari tad utpādya saṃsarga avagama prāgabhāvaḥ na ca eṣaḥ api jñānam apekṣate pratiyogi nirūpaṇa adhīna nirūpaṇa tvāt tad abhāvasya tasya ca viṣaya nirūpya tvāt iti 
NKA_3.71	 prābhākaraḥ tu loka veda sādhāraṇa vyutpatti balena anvita abhidhānam prasādhya vedasya apauruṣeya tayā vaktṛ jñāna anumāna an avakāśāt saṃsarge śabdasya eva svātantryeṇa prāmāṇyam āsthiṣata loke tu anumānataḥ eva vaktṛ jñāna upasarjana tayā saṃsargasya siddheḥ anvita abhidhāna bala āyātepi pratipādaka tve anuvādakatā mātram vākyasya iti nirṇītantaḥ tad atisthavīyaḥ nirṇīta śakteḥ vākyasyāt hi prāk eva arthasya nirṇaye vyāpti smṛti vilambena liṅgasya eva anuvāditā yāvatī hi vede sāmagrī tāvatī eva loke api bhavantī katham iva na artham gamayet na hi apekṣaṇīya antaram asti liṅge tu paripūrṇe api avagate vyāpti smṛtiḥ apekṣaṇīyā asti iti vilambena kim nirṇeyam anvayasya prāk eva pratīteḥ 
NKA_3.72	 loke vaktuḥ āpta tva niścayaḥ apekṣaṇīyaḥ iti ced na tat rahitasya api sva artha pratyāyane śabdasya śakteḥ avadhāraṇāt anyathā vede api artha pratyayaḥ na syāt tad abhāvāt na ca loke anyāni eva padāni yena śakti vaicitryam syāt anāpta uktau vyabhicāra darśanāt tulyā api sāmagrī sandehena śithilāyate iti ced na cakṣuḥ ādau vyabhicāra darśanena śaṅkāyām api satyām jñāna sāmagrītaḥ tad utpatti darśanāt jñāyamānasya ayam vidhiḥ yat sandehe sati na niścāyakam yathā liṅgam cakṣuḥ ādi tu sat tayā iti ced na vākyasya niścata tvāt āpta ukta tvasya ca artha pratyayam pratyanaṅga tvāt loke api ca āptatva aniścaye api vākya artha pratīteḥ bhavati hi veda anukāreṇa paṭhyamāneṣu apauruṣeya tva abhimāninaḥ gauḍa mīmāṃsakasya artha niścayaḥ na ca asau bhrāntiḥ pauruṣeya tva niścaya daśāyām api tathā niścayāt iti 
NKA_3.73	 syāt etat na āpta ukta tvam artha pratīteḥ aṅgam iti brūmaḥ kintu ana āpta ukta tva śaṅkā nirāsaḥ sa ca kvacid apauruṣeya tva niścayāt kvacid āpta ukta tva avadhāraṇāt iti ced tat kim apauruṣeya tvasya apratītau sandehe vā veda vākyāt vidita padārtha saṅgateḥ artha pratyayaḥ eva na bhavet bhavan= api vā na śraddheyaḥ prathame satya ādayaḥ eva pramāṇam naca asaṃsarga agrahe tadānīm saṃsarga vyavahāraḥ bādhakasya atyantam abhāvāt tathā api tad kalpanāyām anvaya uccheda prasaṅgāt dvitīye tu aśraddhā pratyakṣa vat nimitta antarāt nivartsyati iti vede yadi loke api tathā syāt aviśeṣāt 
NKA_3.74	 anyathā vedasya api anuvāka tā prasaṅgaḥ tat ucyate vyasta pumdūṣaṇa āśaṅkaiḥ smārita tvāt padaiḥ amī anvitā iti nirṇīte vedasya api na tat kutas yadā hi apauruṣeya tva niścayāt prāk vedaḥ na kiñcid abhidhatte iti pakṣaḥ tadā āpta ukta tva niścaya uttara kālam loka vat vede api apauruṣeya tva niścayāt paścāt anumāna avatāraḥ iyān= tu viśeṣaḥ yat atra padārthān eva pakṣīkṛtya nirasta pumdoṣā śaṅkaiḥ ākāṅkṣa ādimadbhiḥ padaiḥ smārita tvāt āpta ukta pada kadambaka smārita padārtha vat saṃsargaḥ eva āhatya sādhyaḥ buddhi vyavahitaḥ tu itaratra iti phalataḥ na kaścid vivaśeṣaḥ iti tathā ca anvita abhidhāne api jaghanya tvāt vedasya anuvādaka tva prasaṅgaḥ na ca evam sati tatra pramāṇam asti viśiṣṭa pratipati anyathā anupapatyā hi śabdasya tatra śaktiḥ parikalpanīyā sā ca anumānena eva upapannā iti vṛthā prayāsaḥ tasmāt loke śabdasya anuvādaka tā iti viparīta kalpanā iyam āyuṣmatām 
NKA_3.75	 kim ca idam anvita abhidhānam nāma na tāvat anvita pratipādana mātram avivādāt na api sva artha abhidhāyāḥ tatra tātparyam avivādāt eva na api saṅgati balena tad pratipādanam vākya arthasya apūrva tvāt na api sva artha saṅgatibalena tasya sva arthaḥ eva upakṣayāt na api sā eva saṅga tiḥ ubhaya pratipādikā pratīti krama anupapatteḥ yaugapadya abhyupagame tu yogya tva ādi pratisandhāna śūnyasya api padārtha pratyaya vat vākya artha pratyaya prasaṅgāt na api sā eva saṅgatiḥ sva arthe nirapekṣā vākya arthe tu padārtha pratipādana avāntara vyāpāra iti yuktam tasyāḥ svayam akaraṇa tvāt saṅgatāni padānihi karaṇam na tu saṅgatiḥ tathā api tad pratipādana anuguṇa saṅgati śālīni padāni iti ced na tāvat vākya artha pratipādana anuguṇa tā saṅgareḥ tad āśraya tvena sāmānya mātra gocara tvāt tadvat mātra gocara tvāt vā na api tad anuguṇa vyāpārava tvena akaraṇa tvāt iti uktam tad anuguṇa karaṇa vyāpāra utthāpaka tvāt tad anuguṇa tve na naḥ vivādaḥ anvitaḥ eva śaktiḥ iti ced uktam atra vākya arthasya apūrva tvāt pratīti krama anupapatteḥ ca iti 
NKA_3.76	 smṛta kriyā anvite kārake smṛta kāraka anvitā yāñca kriyāyām saṅgatiḥ atas na ukta doṣa avakāśaḥ na api paryāyata āpattiḥ prādhānyena niyamāt na api paunaruktyam viśeṣa anvaye tātparyāt na api itaretara āśraya tvam sva artha smṛtau= anapekṣaṇāt na api vākya bheda āpattiḥ paraspara padārtha smṛti sannidhau tad itara anapekṣaṇāt iti ced na anvite saṅgatigrahaḥ iti kor athaḥ yadi yatra saṅgatiḥ tad vastu gatyā padārtha anvitam na kiñcid prakṛta upayogi na hi yatra cakṣuṣaḥ sāmarthyam avagatam tat vastu gatyā sparśa vat iti tadvat tā api tasya viṣayaḥ atha anvitatayā eva tatra vyutpattiḥ iti arthaḥ tat asat pramāṇa abhāvāt 
NKA_3.77–3.78	 anvitā artha pratipatti anyathā anupapattiḥ iti ced na ananvita abhidhānena api upapatteḥ ākāṅkṣā anupapattiḥ astu na hi sāmānyatas anvita anavagame anvaya viśeṣe jijñāsā syāt na dṛṣṭe phala viśeṣe rasa viśeṣa jijñāsā vat ākṣepataḥ api upapatteḥ śabda mahimānam antareṇa yatas kutaścid api smṛteṣu padārtheṣu anvaya pratītiḥ syāt na ca evam tatas śabda śaktiḥ avaśyam kalpanīyā iti ced kutas tarhi kavi kāvyāni vilasanti na hi saṃsarga viśeṣam apratītya vākyaracanā nāma na ca sva utprekṣāyām pratyakṣam anumānam śabdaḥ tad ābhāsāḥ vā sambhavanti anyatra cantā vaśena padārtha smaraṇebhyaḥ asaṃsarga āgrahaḥ asau= iti ced mama tāvat saṃsarga grahaḥ eva asau tava api sā eva pada āvalī kvacid anvaye paryavasyati kvacid ananvaya agrahe iti kutas viśeṣāt 
NKA_3.79	 āptān āpta vaktṛkatayā iti ced kim tathāvidhena vaktrā tatra kaścid viśeṣaḥ āhitaḥ āho vaktā eva ācchedaka tayā viśeṣaḥ prathame abhihita anvaya vādinām iva tava api śakti kalpanā gauravam dvitīye tu vaktuḥ iva padānām api avacchedaka tayā eva viśeṣaka tvam astu evam tarhi padānām api anvaya pratītau= asti upayogaḥ kaḥsandehaḥ param padārtha abhidhānena na tu anyathā yathā tava eva āptasya saṃsarga para tayā pada samabhivyāhāra mātreṇa na tu anyathā anyathā guru mata vidām eva ślokaḥ āpta pada prakṣepeṇa paṭhanīyaḥ prāthamyāt abhidhātṛ tvāt tātparya upagamāt api āptānām eva sā śaktiḥ varam abhyupagamyatām iti 
NKA_3.80–3.81	 tasmāt prakāra antareṇa saṃsarga pratyayaḥ bhavatu mā vā padārthānām ākāṅkṣa ādimattve sati abhihitānām avaśyam anvayaḥ iti kutas ati prasaṅgaḥ na ca evam sati padārthāḥ eva karaṇam teṣām anāgata ādi rūpa tayā kāraka tva anupapattau tad viśeṣasya karaṇa tvasya ayogāt tad saṃsarge pramāṇa antara asaṅkīrṇa udāharaṇa abhāvāt ca padānām tu pūrva bhāva niyamena padārtha smaraṇa avāntara vyāpāravat tayā tad upapatteḥ vyāpārasya avyavadhāyaka tvāt iti kṛtam prasakta anuprasaktyā 
NKA_3.82	 astu tarhi śabdaḥ eva bādhakam sarvajñe kartari tathā hi prakṛteḥ kriyamāṇāni guṇaiḥ karmāṇi sarvaśas ahaṅkāra vimūḍha ātmā kartāham iti manyate ityādi paṭhanti asya ayam arthaḥ na pāramārthikam cetanasya kartṛ tvam asti ābhimānikam tu tat na ca sarvajñasya abhimānaḥ na ca asarvajñasya jagat kartṛ tvam asti ucyate na pramāṇam anāpta uktiḥ na adṛṣṭe kvacid āpta tā adṛśya dṛṣṭau sarvajñaḥ na ca nitya āgamaḥ kṣamaḥ yadi hi sarvajña kartṛ abhāvā avedakaḥ śabdaḥ na āpta uktaḥ na tarhi pramāṇam atha āptaḥ asya vaktā katham na tad artha darśī atīndriya artha darśī iti ced katham asarva jñaḥ katham vā na kartā āgamasya eva praṇayanāt na ca nitya āgama sambhavaḥ vicchedāt itya āveditam 
NKA_3.83	 api ca na ca asau kvacid ekāntar sattvasya api pravedanāt nirañjana avabodha arthaḥ na ca san= api tad paraḥ na hi asattva pakṣaḥ eva āgamaḥ niyataḥ īśvara sadbhāvasya eva bhūyaḥsu pradeśeṣu pratipādanāt tathā ca agre darśayiṣyāmaḥ tathā ca sati kvacid asattva pratipādanam anekāntam na bādhakam sattva pratipādanam api tarhi na sādhanam iti ced āpātatas tāvat evam etat yadā tu niḥśeṣa viśeṣa guṇa śūnya ātma svarūpa pratipādana artha tvam akartṛka tva āgamānām avadhārayiṣyate tadā na tad niṣedhe tātparyam am īṣām iti sattva pratipādakānām eva āgamānām prāmāṇyam bhaviṣyati iti na ca teṣām api anyatra tātparyam iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
NKA_3.84	 astu artha āpattiḥ tarhi bādhikāḥ tathā hi yadi abhaviṣyat na upādekṣyat na hi asau= anupadiśya pravartayitum na jānāti atas upadeśaḥ eva anyathā anupapadyamānaḥ tathāvidhasya abhāvam audāsīnyam vā avedayati na anyathā eva upapatteḥ hetu abhāve phala abhāvāt pramāṇe asati na pramā tad abhāvāt pravṛttiḥ no karma vāde api ayam vidhiḥ buddhi pūrvām hi pravṛttiḥ na buddhim anutpādya śakya sampādanāḥ na ca prakṛte buddhiḥ api upadeśam antareṇa śakya siddhiḥ tasya eva tad kāraṇa tvāt bhūta āveśa nyāyena pravartayet iti ced pravartayet eva yadi tathā phala siddhiḥ syāt na tu evam kutas etat avasitam upadeśānyatha anupapattyā eva yasya api mate adṛṣṭa vaśāt eva bhūtānām pravṛttiḥ tasya api tulyam etat yadi asti pravṛtti nimittam adṛṣṭam kim upadeśena tatas eva pravṛtti siddheḥ na ced tathā api kim upadeśena tad abhāve tasmin sati api apravṛtteḥ nityaḥ svatantraḥ upadeśaḥ na paryanuyojyaḥ iti ced yūyam paryanuyojyāḥ ye tam avadhānataḥ dhārayanti vicārayanti ca iti 
NKA_3.85	 na ca arthāpattiḥ anumānataḥ bhidyate loke tad asaṅkīrṇa udāharaṇa abhāvāt prakāra antara abhāvāt ca tathā hi aniyamyasya na ayuktiḥ na aniyantā upapādakaḥ na mānayoḥ virodhaḥ asti prasiddhe vā api asau samaḥ jīvan= caitraḥ gṛhe na asti iti anupapadyamānam asati bahis sadbhāve tam āpadayati iti udaharanti tatra cintyate kim anupapannam jīvataḥ gṛha abhāvasya iti na hi aniyamayasya aniyāmakam vinā kiñcid anupapannam atiprasaṅgāt nanu svarūpam eva tat na tāvat bahis sattvena kartavyam tad akārya tvāt tasya sthitiḥ eva asya tena vinā na syāt iti asya svabhāvaḥ iti ced evam tarhi tad niyata svabhāvaḥ eva asau vyāpteḥ eva vyatireka mukha nirūpyāyāḥ tathā avyapadeśāt 
NKA_3.86–3.87	 katham vā bahis sattvam asya upapādakam na hi aniyāmakaḥ bhavan= api aniyamyam upapādayati atiprasaṅgāt eva svabhāvaḥ asya yat anena bahis sattvena geha asa tvam kroḍīkṛtya sthātavyam iti ced sā iyam vyāptiḥ eva anvaya mukha nirūpyā tathā vyapadiśyate iti na vayam avinā abhāvam artha āpattau= apajānīmahe kintu tat jñānam na ca asau sattā mātreṇa tad anumāna tvam āpādayati iti ced na anupapatti pratisandhānasya avaśya abhyupagantavya tvāt anyathā ātu ati prasaṅgāt arthāpatti ābhāsān avakāśāt ca yadā hi anyathā eva upapannam anyathā anupapannam iti manyate tadā asya viparyayaḥ na tu anyathā iti 
NKA_3.88–3.89	 tathā api katham atra vyāptiḥ gṛhyeta iti ced yadā aham iha tadā na anyatra yadā anyatra tadā na iha iti sarva pratyakṣā siddham etat kā tatra api kathantā sarva deśa apratyakṣa tve tatra abhāvaḥ duravadhāraṇaḥ iti api na asti teṣām eva saṃsargasya ātmani pratiṣedhāt ayogyānām pratiṣedhe kā vārtā iti ced tad avayavānām tad saṃsarga pratiṣedhāt eva anumānāt anyeṣām na kācid na hi akāraṇībhūtena paramāṇunā na idam saṃsṛṣṭam iti niścetum śakyam iti na ca avinābhāva niścayena api gamayan= apakṣa dharmor athāpattiḥ iti yuktam pakṣa dharma tāyāḥ animitta tva prasaṅgāt aviśeṣāt vyadhikaraṇena avinābhāva niścaya ayogāt ca yat yatra yadā iti prakāra anupapatteḥ 
NKA_3.90	 pramāṇayoḥ virodhe arthāpattiḥ avirodha upapādikā na tu evam anumānam iti api na asti virodhe hi rajju sarpa ādi vat ekasya bādhaḥ eva syāt na tu ubhayoḥ pramāṇyam prāmāṇye vā na virodhaḥ sthūlam idam ekam itivat saha sambhavāt caitraḥ ayam ayam tu maitraḥ iti vat vā viṣaya bhedāt prakṛte kvāpi asti iti sāmānyatas gehasya api praveśāt eka viṣaya tā api asti iti ced yadi evam kvacid asti kvacid na asti iti vat na virodhaḥ atra api virodhaḥ eva iti ced ekam tarhi bhajyeta 
NKA_3.91	 na bhajyeta arthāpattyā ubhayoḥ api upapādanāt iti ced kim anupapadyamānam virodhaḥ eva anyathā anupapadyamānaḥ vibhinna viṣaya tayā vyavasthāpayati iti ced atha abhinna viṣaya tayā eva kim na vyavasthāpayet vyavasthāpanam avirodha āpādanam eka viṣaya tayā eva ca anayoḥ virodhaḥ sa katham tayā eva śamayitavyaḥ na hi yaḥ yat viṣa mūrcchitaḥ sa tena eva utthāpyate iti ced eka viṣaya tayā anayoḥ virodhaḥ iti etat eva kutas vibhinna deśa svabhāva tayā eva sarvatra upalambhāt iti ced nanu iyam vyāptiḥ eva tathā ca ghaṭṭakuṭyām prabhātam iti 
NKA_3.92	 dhūmopi vā anupapadyamāna tayā eva vahnim gamayet na hi tena vinā asau= upapadyate virodhaḥ api dhūmāt vahninā bhavitavyam anupalabdheḥ ca na bhavitavyam iti tathā ca anu palabdheḥ arvāc bhāga vyavasthāpanam dhūmasya ca vyavadhānena anupalabhya vahni viṣaya tva sthitiḥ arthāpattiḥ iti kutas anumānam vahnim ān ayam iti am anumānam vyāpteḥ anyathā anumāna abhāve virodha asiddheḥ arvāc bhāga anupalabdhi virodhena para bhāge asya vahniḥ iti asya artha āpattiḥ eva iti ced na vyāpti grāhakeṇa pramāṇena virodhasya ukta tvāt na api uttarā arthāpattiḥ anyathā pāṇḍara tvasya apālāla tva virodhena pālāla tva sthitiḥ api artha āpattiḥ eva syāt tad viśiṣṭasya tena eva vyāpteḥ na evam iti ced yadi evam arvāc bhāga anupalabhyamāna vanhi tvena viśiṣṭasya dhūmasya tena eva vyāpteḥ katham evam bhaviṣyati iti tulyam 
NKA_3.93–3.94	 kevala vyatirekya anumānam para abhimatam arthāpattiḥ anvaya abhāvāt iti ced evam etāvatā viśeṣeṇa anumāner athāpatti vyavahāram na vārayāmaḥ tatra anumāna vyavahāraḥ kutas iti ced avinābhūta liṅga samutpanna tvāt sādhya dharmeṇa vinā hi abhavanam anvayinaḥ iva vyatirekiṇaḥ api aviśiṣṭam tad niścayaḥ ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām anyatareṇa vā iti tasmāt arthāpattiḥ iti anumānasya paryāyaḥ ayam tad viśeṣa vacanam vā pūrvavat ādi vat iti yuktam anupalabdhiḥ tu na bādhikā iti cintitam na ca pratyakṣa ādeḥ atiricyate tat ucyate pratipatteḥ apārokṣyāt indriyasya anupakṣayāt ajñāta karaṇa tvāt ca bhāva āveśāt ca cetasaḥ 
NKA_3.95	 yā hi sākṣātkāriṇī pratītiḥ sā indriya karaṇikā yathā rūpa ādi pratītiḥ tathā iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti api sākṣātkāri tvam asyāḥ asiddham iti ced na eka jātīya tve jñāta ajñāta karaṇa tva anupapatteḥ na hi tasmin= eva kārye tat eva karaṇam ekadā jñātam ajñātañca ekadā upayujyate liṅga indriyayoḥ api vyatyaya prasaṅgāt jñānasya akāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt ca na hi tat atipatyā api bhavataḥ tad kāraṇa tvam vyāghātāt tasmāt jñāta anupalabdhi janyasya sākṣātkāri tvāt tad viparīta kāraṇakam idam tad viparīta jātīyam iti nyāyyām nanu kva nāma jñāta anupalabdhiḥ asākṣāt kāriṇīm abhāva pratītim janayati tat yathā nipuṇataram anusṛtaḥ mayā mandire caitraḥ na ca upalabdhaḥ iti śrutyā śrotā anum inoti nūnam na āsīt eva iti etena prāk nāstitā api vyākhyātāḥ nanu tathā api avāntara jāti bhedaḥ astu ajñāta anupalabdhi janye sākṣātkāraḥ tu kutas iti ced kāraṇa virodhāt kārya virodhena bhavitavyam iti uktam eva 
NKA_3.96	 ananyatra upakṣīṇa indriya vyāpāra anantara bhāvi tvāt ca adhikaraṇa grahaṇe tad upakṣīṇam iti ced na andhasya api tvac indriya upanīte ghaṭa ādau rūpa viśeṣa abhāva pratīti prasaṅgāt asti hi tasya adhikaraṇa grahaṇam asti ca pratiyogi smaraṇam asti ca śyāmerakta tvasya yogyasya abhāvaḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca adhikaraṇa grāhaka indriya grāhya abhāva vādinaḥ api samānam etat iti ced na pratiyogi grāhaka indriya grāhyaḥ abhāvaḥ iti abhyupagamāt mama api pratiyogi grāhaka indriya gṛhīte adhikaraṇe anupalabdhiḥ pramāṇam iti abhyupagamaḥ iti ced na vāyau tvac indriya upanīte rūpa abhāva prati iti anudaya prasaṅgāt tathā api tat tatra sannikṛṣṭam iti ced hanta evam ananyatra carita artham indriyam avaśyam apekṣaṇīyam rūpa abhāva anubhavena 
NKA_3.97	 syāt etat tathā api vastu antara grahaḥ eva tasya upayogaḥ iti ced na tasya tam pratyakāraṇa tvāt kāraṇa tve vā mahā andhakāre kara parāmarśena sparśa vat dravya abhāvam na pratīyāt pratīyāt ca puras visphārita akṣaḥ pṛṣṭha lagnasya āśyāma tvam ārjava avasthānam api adhikaraṇasya upayujyate iti ced tarhi nayana sannikarṣaḥ api upayokṣyate tad eka sahakāri prabhā sannikarṣa apekṣaṇāt vātāyana vivara visāri kara parāmṛṣṭe api adhikaraṇe tad upalambha prasaṅgāt ca 
NKA_3.98	 tathā api yogya tā āpādana upakṣīṇañcakṣuḥ tad itara sāmagrī sākalye hi anupalabhyamānasya abhāvaḥ niścīyate tat ca cakṣuṣi adhiḥ akaraṇa sannikṛṣṭe sati syāt iti ced nanu paripūrṇāni kāraṇāni eva sākalyam tathā ca kim kutra upakṣīṇam atha anyonya melanam mithas pratyāsatti ādi śabda vācyam tad upakṣaya viṣayaḥ na tarhi kvacid cakṣuḥ kāraṇam syāt iti na hi rūpa ādi upalabdhim api asannikṛṣṭam etat upajanayati 
NKA_3.99	 atha adhikaraṇa samaveta kiñcid upalambhaḥ api tad viṣaya abhāva grahe anupalabdheḥ apekṣaṇīyaḥ tatas tatra idam caritārtham vāyu ādiṣu tu rūpa ādi abhāva pratītirānu mānikī tathā anupalabdhyā hi anumīyate ayam nīrūpaḥ vāyuḥ iti na asiddheḥ na hi upalambha abhāvaḥ bhavatām abhāva upalambhaḥ upalambhasya atīndriya tva abhyupagamāt prākaṭya abhāvena anumeyaḥ iti ced na vāyau rūpa vattā prākaṭya abhāvasya api asiddheḥ rūpa abhāvena samāna tvāt vyavahāra abhāvena anumeyaḥ iti ced na kāya vāc vyāpāra abhāve api upekṣā jñāna bhāva abhyupagamāt mūka svapna upapatteḥ ca na ca vyavahāra abhāva mātreṇa anumātum api śakyate anaikāntika tvāt asiddheḥ ca tad viṣayaḥ tu vyavahāraḥ tad viṣaya jñāna janyaḥ vā tad viṣaya jñāna janakaḥ vā tad āśraya dharma janakaḥ vā tad abhāvaḥ ca tad jñāna tad āśraya dharma abhāva antarbhūtaḥ eva iti aśakya niścayaḥ eva ātma āśraya ita retara āśraya cakraka pravṛtti prasaṅgāt 
NKA_3.100–3.101	 na ca ajñātasya upalambha ādi abhāvasya liṅgatā na ca prākaṭya abhāvaḥ sattā mātreṇa upalambha abhāvam āvedayati iti yuktam liṅga abhāvasya tathātve ati prasaṅgāt avinā abhāva balena tu niyame tad pratisandhānāpatteḥ na hi avinābhāvaḥ sattā mātreṇa jñāna hetum niyamayati dhūma ādau= api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt iti jñāna pratyakṣa tvena tvad diśā bhaviṣyati iti ced na śabda dhvaṃsā ādinā ukta uttara tvāt 
NKA_3.102–3.103^1	 api ca pratiyogi grāhaka indriyeṇa adhikaraṇa dharma pratītiḥ anupalabdheḥ aṅgam iti tad rahitāyāḥ tasyāḥ kārya vyabhicārāt vyavasthāpyeta vyāpti balāt vā na tāvat ukta rūpa anupalabdhiḥ tām vinā abhāva pratyayam ajanayantī dṛśyate na api vyāpteḥ tathā sati vayau rūpa abhāva pratyayaḥ tām ākṣipet evam bhūta tvāt anākṣepe vā na tad kāraṇakaḥ bhavet na vā bhavet tatas na bhavati eva liṅgāt tad utpattiḥ iti ced nanu liṅgam api sā eva na tattva antaram yathā yoni sambandhaḥ aliṅga daśāyām indriya sannikarṣam apekṣate liṅgadaśāyām tu tad anapekṣaḥ eva brāhmaṇya jñāne tathā etat syāt iti ced na kārya jāti bhedāt tad upapatteḥ prakṛte ca tad anabhyupagamāt 
NKA_3.102–3.103^2	 pārokṣya apārokṣye vihāyāni athā api asau bhaviṣyati iti ced na anupalambhāt sambhāvyate tāvat iti ced sambhāvyatām na tu etāvatā api tam āśritya karaṇa niyama niścayaḥ ajñāta karaṇa tvāt ca yat ajñāyamāna karaṇa jam jñānam tad sākṣāt indriya jam yathā rūpa pratyakṣam tathā āca iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti jñānam iti yathā vā smaraṇam ajñāyamāna karaṇa jam sākṣāt manaḥ janma kutas tarhi na sākṣāt kārī anubhava rūpam saṃskāra atirikta sannikarṣa abhāvāt iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
NKA_3.104	 tathā api bhāva viṣaye iyam vyavasthā abhāva jñānam tu ajñāta karaṇa tve api na sākṣāt indriya jam bhaviṣyati iti ced na utsargasya bādhaka abhāvena saṅkoca anupapatteḥ anyathā sarva vyāptīnām bhāva mātra viṣaya tva prasaṅgaḥ aviśeṣāt tathā api vipakṣe kim bādhakam iti ced nanu idam eva tāvat anyat api ucyamānam ākarṇaya tat yathā akāraṇaka kārya prasaṅgaḥ rūpa ādi upalabdhīnām api vān indriya karaṇa tva prasaṅgaḥ na hi anumiti ādibhiḥ upalabhyamāna karaṇikābhiḥ cakṣuḥ ādi vyavasthāpanam apitu anupalabhyamāna karaṇikābhiḥ rūpa ādi upalabdhibhiḥ eva yadi api sākṣātkāritā api tatra eva paryavasyati tathā api prathamatas anupalabhyamāna karaṇa tvam eva prayojakam cakṣuḥ ādi kalpane na hi upalabhyamāne karaṇa antare sākṣāt kāriṇīṣu api tāsu cakṣuḥ ādi anupalabhyamānam kaścid akalpayiṣyat atas eva asākṣātkāri tve api smṛteḥ manaḥ eva karaṇam upāgaman dhīrāḥ saṃskāraḥ tu artha viśeṣa pratti āsattau= upayujyate indriyāṇām prāpya kāri tva vyavasthāpanāt 
NKA_3.105	 bhāva āveśāt ca cetasaḥ sarvatra hi bāhya artha anubhave janayitavye bhāva bhūta pramāṇa āviṣṭam eva cetaḥ upayujyate na atas anyathā iti vyāptiḥ tathā eva śakteḥ avadhāraṇāt na hi anupalabdhi mātra sahāyam tat abhāve api anubhavam ādhātum utsahate śabda liṅga ādeḥ apekṣā darśanāt na ca yatra yat apekṣam yasya janaka tvam upalabdham tat eva tasya eva tad anapekṣam janakam iti nyāya saham ārda indhana sambandham antareṇa api dahanāt dhūma sambhāvana āpatteḥ tathā ca gatam kārya kāraṇa bhāva parigraha vyasanena 
NKA_3.106	 api ca pratiyogini sāmarthyāt vyāpāra avi avadhānataḥ akṣa āśraya tvāt doṣāṇām indriyāṇi vikalpanāt yat hi pramāṇam yat bhāva avagāhi tat tad abhāva gāhi yathā liṅgam śabdaḥ vā ghaṭa ādi avagāhi ca indriyam iti anyathā hi śabda ādikam api na abhāvam āvedayet bhāvaḥ eva sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt na ca evam eva nyāyyam devadattaḥ gehe na asti iti śabdāt mayā tatra jijñāsamānena api na dṛṣṭaḥ maitraḥ iti avagata anupalabdhyā anumānāt api avagateḥ 
NKA_3.107	 grāhayatu vā aśrayam indriyam tathā api na tena idam vyavadhīyate vyāpāra tvāt anyathā sarva savikalpakānām pratyakṣa tvāya dattaḥ jala añcaliḥ syāt nanu evam sati dhūma upalambhaḥ api asya vyāpāraḥ syāt tathā ca gatam anumānena api iti ced na yayā kriyayā vinā yasya yat kāraṇa tvam na nirvahati tam prati tasyāḥ eva vyāpāra tvāt na ca dhūma ādi upalabdhim antareṇa cakṣuṣaḥ vanhi jñāna kāraṇa tvam na nirvahati saṃyoga vat iti 
NKA_3.108	 asti ca bhāva abhāva viparyayaḥ saḥ ayam yasya doṣam anuvidhatte tat eva atra karaṇam iti nyāyyam na ca anupalabdhiḥ svabhāvataḥ duṣṭāḥ na api adhikaraṇa grahaṇam pratiyogi smaraṇam vā svabhāvataḥ duṣṭam anupad patti daśāyām anutpatteḥ utpatti daśā yāñca sva artha prakāśana svabhāva tāyāḥ aparāvṛtteḥ asaṃsṛṣṭayoḥ adhikaram apratiyoginoḥ saṃsṛṣṭa tayā pratimānam duṣṭam saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ ca asaṃsṛṣṭa tayā iti ced nanu ayam eva viparyayaḥ tathā ācā atma āśrayaḥ doṣaḥ tasmāt duṣṭa indriyasya tad viparyaya sāmarthye aduṣṭasya tad samīcīna jñāna sāmarthyam api tathā ca prayogaḥ indriyam abhāva pramākaraṇam tad viparyaya karaṇa tvāt yat yat viparyaya karaṇam tat tad pramākaraṇam yathā rūpa pramākaraṇam cakṣuḥ iti 
NKA_3.109^1	 vikalpanāt khalu api aghaṭam bhū talam iti hi viśiṣṭa dhīravaśyam indriya karaṇikā svīkartavyā pramāṇa antaram vā saptamam āstheyam yathā hi viśeṣya mātra upakṣīṇam indriyam akaraṇam atra tathā viśeṣaṇa mātra upakṣīṇa anupalabdhiḥ api na karaṇam syāt sva sva viṣaya mātra pravṛttayoḥ pramāṇayoḥ samāhāraḥ kāraṇam iti ced na viṣaya bhede phala vaijātye ca tad anupapatteḥ na hi mṛtsu tantuṣu ca vyāpriyamāṇayoḥ kulāla kuvindayoḥ samāhāraḥ syāt na api ghaṭa paṭa ādi kāriṇām cakravema ādīnām samāhāraḥ kvacid upayujyate 
NKA_3.109^2	 tatra karbura kārya abhāvāt na tathā prakṛte tu viśiṣṭa pratyayasya parokṣa aparokṣa rūpasya darśanāt tathā iti ced na viruddha jāti samāveśa abhāvāt bhāve vā karambitaḥ eva kārye dvayoḥ api śaktiḥ abhyupagantavyā darśana balāt na hi niyata viṣayeṇa sāmarthyena karbura kārya siddhiḥ anyatra api tathā prasaṅgāt nanu ubhayoḥ api ubhayatra sāmarthye kor atho mithas sannidhānena iti ced na tad sahitasya eva tasya tatra sāmarthyāt iti etena surabhi candanam ityādayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ tathā ca abhāva viṣaye api indriya sāmarthyasya durapahnava tvāt alam asat graheṇa iti 
NKA_3.110	 syāt etat na agṛhīte viśeṣaṇe viśaṣṭa buddhiḥ udeti tad kārya tvāt na ca viśiṣṭa sāmarthye kevala viśeṣaṇe api sāmarthyam kevala saurabhe api cakṣuṣaḥ vṛtti prasaṅgāt atas abhāva viśeṣaṇa grahaṇāya māna antara sambhavaḥ api ca katham anālocitor atha indriyeṇa vikalpyeta na ca māna antarasya api eṣā rītiḥ anumāna ādibhiḥ anāla ucitasya api arthasya vikalpanāt aprāpteḥ ca na hi abhāvena indriyasya saṃyoga ādiḥ sambhavati na ca viśeṣaṇa tvam sambandha antara pūrvaka tvāt tasya avaśya abhyupagantavya tvāt ca anupalabdheḥ na hi tad upalabdhau tasya abhāva upalambhaḥ iti ced 
NKA_3.111–3.113	 ucyate avaccheda graha dhrauvyāt adhrauvye siddha sādhanāt prāpti antare anavasthānā atra ced anyaḥ api durghaṭaḥ sa hi artha viśeṣaṇī bhaviṣyan kevalaḥ api visphuret yasya avacchedaka jñānam na vyañjakam sa ca vikalpayitavyaḥ ālocyate yaḥ viśeṣaṇa jñāna nirapekṣeṇa indriyeṇa vijñāpyate yaḥ tu tad puraḥsaraḥ eva prakāśate tatra tasya vikalpa sāmagrī samavadhānavataḥ eva sāmarthyāt na ayam vidhiḥ svabhāva prāptau satyām api adhikā prāptiḥ pratipatti balena rūpa ādau= abhyupagatā iha tu anavasthāt ustha tayā na tad abhyupagamaḥ na tu svabhāva pratyāsattiḥ etāvatā eva viphalāyate 
NKA_3.114	 na ced evam pramāṇa antare api sarvam etat durghaṭam syāt tathā hi sarvam eva mānam sākṣāt paramparayā vā nirvikalpaka viśrāntam na hi anumāna ādikam api anālocana pūrvakam tatas anālocitaḥ abhāvaḥ katham anupalabdhyā api vikalpyeta na ca tayā tad ālocanam eva janyate pratiyogi anavacchinnasya tasya nirūpayitum aśakyatvāt śakya tve vā kim aparāddham indriyeṇa tathā sambandha antara garbha tva niyamena viśeṣaṇa tvasya māna antare api kaḥ pratīkāraḥ tad abhāvasya tadānīm apisamāna tvāt parasya tādātmyam asti iti ced nanu yadi asau= asti asti eva na ced na eva na hi abhyupagamena arthāḥ kriyante anabhyupagamena vā nivartante iti 
NKA_3.115–3.116	 avaśya abhyupagantavya tve kāraṇa tvam siddhayet na tu māna antara tvam anyathā bhāva upalambhe api abhāva anupalabdhiḥ eva pramāṇam syāt na indriyam abhāva upalambhe bhāva anupalambha vat bhāva upalambhe abhāvānupalambhasya api vajra lepāya māna tvāt iti pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ ebhiḥ evam adharaḥ dūre virodha udayaḥ prāyas yad mukha vīkṣaṇa eka vidhuraiḥ ātmā api na āsādyate tam sarva anuvidheyam ekam asama svacchanda līla utsavam devānām api devam udbhavat ati śraddhāḥ prapadyāmahe 
NKA_4.1–4.2	 nanu sat api īśvara jñānam na pramāṇam tad lakṣaṇā yogāt anadhigata artha gantuḥ tathā abhāvāt anyathā smṛteḥ api prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt na ca nityasya sarva viṣa sya cān adhigata artha tā vyāghātāt atra ucyate avyāpteḥ adhika vyāpteḥ alakṣaṇam apūrva dṛś yathārtha anubhavaḥ mānam anapekṣatayā iṣyate na hi adhigater athe adhigatiḥ eva na utpadyate kāraṇānām apratibandhāt na ca utpadyamānā api pramātuḥ anapekṣitā iti na pramā prāmāṇyasya ātad adhīna tvāt na api pūrva aviśiṣṭa tā mātreṇa aprāmāṇyam uttara aviśiṣṭa tayā pūrvasya api aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt tad anapekṣa tvena tu tasya pramāṇye tad uttarasya api tathā eva syāt aviśeṣāt chinne kuṭhāra ādīnām iva paricchinne nayana ādīnām sādhakatama tvam eva na asti iti api na asti phala utpāda anutpādābhyām viśeṣāt 
NKA_4.3	 tat phalam pramā eva na bhavati gṛhīta mātra gocara tvāt smṛti vat iti ced na yathārtha anubhava tu a niṣedhe sādhye bādhita tvāt anadhigata artha tva niṣedhe siddha sādhanāt sādhya sama tvāt ca vyavahāra niṣedhe tad nimitta viraha upādhika tvāt bādhita tvāt ca nacān adhigata artha tvam eva tad nimittam viparyaya ipi pramāvī avahāra prasaṅgāt na api yathārtha tva viśiṣṭam etat eva dhārāvahana buddhi avyāpteḥ 
NKA_4.4	 na ca tad tad kāla kalā viśiṣṭa tayā tatra api anadhigata artha ṛtvam upapādanīyam kṣaṇa upādhīnām anākalanāt naca ajñāteṣu api viśeṣaṇeṣu tad janita viśiṣṭa tā prakāśataḥ iti kalpanīyam sva rūpeṇa tad janane anāgata ādi viśiṣṭa tā anubhava virodhāt tad jñānena tu tad janane sūrya gati ādīnām ajñāne tad viśiṣṭa tā anutpādāt na ca etasyām pramāṇam asti nanu anupakārya anupakārakayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāve katham atiprasaṅgaḥ vāraṇīyaḥ vyavacchitti pratyāyanena vyavacchittau svabhāvena anyathā tatra avyanavasthānāt iti 
NKA_4.5–4.6	 jñāta tā eva upādhiḥ iti ced na nirākariṣyamāṇa tvāt tad sadbhāvepi vā smṛteḥ api tathā eva prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt janaka agocara tvepi uttarottara smṛtau pūrva pūrva smaraṇa janita jñāta tāvabhāsanāt astu vā pratyakṣe yathā tathā gṛhīta vismṛta artha śrutau kā vārtā apramā eva asau= iti ced gatam idānīm veda prāmāṇya pratyāśayā na hi anādau saṃsāre svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti vākya arthaḥ kenacid na avagataḥ sandehe api prāmāṇya sandehāt na ca tatra api kāla kalā viśeṣāḥ parisphuranti na ca eka janma avaccheda paribhāṣaya idam lakṣaṇam tatra api anubhūta vismṛta veda artham pratyaprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt 
NKA_4.7	 katham tarhi smṛteḥ vyavacchedaḥ ananubhava tvena eva yathārtha ūhi anubhavaḥ pramā iti prāmāṇikāḥ paśyanti tatu a jñānāt iti sūtraṇāt avyabhicāri jñānam iti ca nanu smṛtiḥ pramā eva kim na syāt yathā artha jñāna tvāt pratyakṣa ādi anubhūti vat iti ced na siddhe vyavahāre nimitta anusaraṇāt na ca sva icchā kalpitena nimittena loka vyavahāra niyamanam avyavasthayā loka vyavahāra viplava prasaṅgāt na ca smṛti hetau pramāṇa abhiyuktānām mahā ṛṣīṇām pramāṇa vyavahāraḥ asti pṛthak anupadeśāt ukteṣu anantarbhāvāt anupadeśaḥ iti ced na pratyakṣasya asākṣāt kāri phala tva anupapatteḥ liṅga śabda ādeḥ ca sattā mātreṇa pratītya sādhana tvāt iti 
NKA_4.8	 evam vyavasthite tarkyate api yat iyam anubhava eka viṣayā satī tad mukha nirīkṣaṇena tat yathārtha tva ayatha artha tve anuvidhīyamānā tad prāmāṇyam avyavasthāpya na yathārtha tayā vyavahartum śakyate iti vyavahāre api pūrva anubhavaḥ eva pramitiḥ anapekṣa tvāt na tu smṛtiḥ nityam tad apekṣaṇāt asamī cīne hi anubhave smṛtiḥ api tathā eva nanu evam anumānam api apramāṇam āpadyeta mūla pratyakṣa anuvidhānāt na viṣaya bhedāt āgamaḥ tarhi na pramāṇam tad viṣaya māna antara anuvidhānāt na pramātṛ bhedāt dhārāvāhika buddhayaḥ tarhi na pramāṇam ādya pramāṇa anuvidhānāt na kāraṇa viśuddhi mātra apekṣayā prathama vat uttarāsām api pūrva mukha nirīkṣaṇa abhāvāt kāraṇa bala āyātam kākatālīyam paurvāparyam iti 
NKA_4.9	 yadi hi smṛtiḥ na pramitiḥ pūrva anubhave kim pramāṇam smṛti anyathā anupapattiḥ iti ced na tayā kāraṇa mātra siddheḥ na tu tena anubhavena eva bhavitavyam iti niyāmakam asti ananubhūtepi tarhi smaraṇam syāt iti ced kim na syāt na hi atra pramāṇam asti pūrva anaubhava ākāra ullekhaḥ smṛteḥ dṛśyate saḥ anyathā na syāt iti ced tat kim bauddha vat viṣaya ākārāni atha anupapattyā viṣaya siddhiḥ tvayā api iṣyate tathābhūtam jñānam eva vā tad siddhiḥ ādye tadvat eva anaikāntika tvam na hi yat ākāram jñānam tad pūrvaka tvam tasya iti niyamaḥ anāgata jñāne vibhrame ca vyabhicārāt dvitīye ca smṛti prāmāṇyam avarjanīyam mā bhūt pūrva anubhava siddhiḥ kim naḥ chinnam iti ced na tarhi smṛti anubhavayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ iti na tad aprāmāṇye api pūrva apara avasthāvat ātma pratyabhijñāna prāmāṇyāt eva tad upapatteḥ yaḥ aham anvabhavam amum artham saḥ aham smarāmi iti mānasa pratyakṣam asti iti 
NKA_4.10–4.11	 na ca gṛhīta grāhi tvam īśvara jñānasya tadīya jñāna antara agocara tvāt viśvasya na ca tat eva jñānam kāla bhedena apramāṇam anapekṣa tvasya aparāvṛtteḥ tathā api vā prāmāṇye atiprasaṅgāt iti syāt etat anupakārakam viṣayasya tadīyam etadīyam vā na bhavitum arhati aviśeṣāt na ca tasya iti aniyatam tatra pramāṇam atiprasaṅgāt na ca tad abhijñānam antareṇa tad upakārasya utpattiḥ tathā anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā kāryatvasya anaikāntika tvāt atra ucyate 
NKA_4.12	 svabhāva niyama abhāvāt upakāraḥ api durghaṭaḥ su ghaṭa tve api satyarthe asati kā gatiḥ anyathā viśeṣa abhāvāt tatra eva phalam na anyatra iti asya api niyamasya anupapatteḥ svabhāva niyamena ca upapattau tathā eva viṣaya vyavasthā upapatteḥ avaśyañca etat anumantavyam atīta ādi viṣaya tva anurodhāt na hi tatra jñānena kiñcid kriyate iti śakyam avagantum asatvāt na ca tad dharma sāmānya ādhāram kiñcid kriyate iti yuktam tena tasya eva viṣaya tva prāpteḥ tādātmyāt viśeṣasya api sā eva jñāta tā iti ced tat kim cakṣuṣā ghaṭe jñāyamāne rasaḥ api jñāyate tādātmyāt ghaṭa ākāreṇa jñāyate eva asau iti ced atha rasa ākāreṇa kim na jñāyate tena rūpeṇa jñāta tānādhāra tvāt iti ced na tarhi vartamāna sāmānya jñāne api atīta anāgata ādi jñānam tena ākāreṇa prākaṭya ana ādhāra tvāt iti 
NKA_4.13	 nanu kriyayā karmaṇi kiñcid karttavyam iti vyāpteraḥ tu anumānam na  anekāntāt asiddheḥ vā na ca liṅgam iha kriyā tad vaiśiṣṭya prakāśa tvāt na adhyakṣa anubhavaḥ adhike dhātu artha mātra abhiprāyeṇa prayoge saṃyoga ādibhiḥ anekāntāt na hi śara saṃyogena gagane kiñcid kriyate antya śabda abhivyaktyā vā spanda abhiprāyeṇa asiddheḥ vyāpāra abhiprāyeṇa śabda liṅga indriya vyāpāraiḥ vyabhicārāt na hi taiḥ prameye kiñcid kriyate api tu pramātari eva phala abhiprāyeṇa api tathā antatas tena eva anekāntāt anavasthānāt ca āśu vināśi dharma abhiprāyeṇa dvi tva ādibhiḥ aniyamāt āśukāraka abhiprāyeṇa karmaṇi asiddheḥ karmaṇi āśu kārakam jñānam iti eva hi sādhyam kartari āśu kāraka tvasya karma upakāraka tvena avyāpteḥ śabda ādi vyāpāraiḥ eva anekāntāt 
NKA_4.14	 syāt etat anubhava siddham eva prākaṭyam tathā hi jñātaḥ ayam arthaḥ iti sāmānyatas sākṣātkṛtaḥ ayam arthaḥ iti viśeṣataḥ viṣaya viśeṣaṇam eva kiñcid parisphurati iti ced tat asat yathā hi arthena eva viśeṣaḥ hi nirākāra tayā ādhiyām tathā kriyayā eva viśeṣaḥ hi vyavahāreṣu karmaṇām kim na paśyasi ghaṭa kriyā paṭa kriyā iti vat kṛtaḥ ghaṭaḥ kariṣyate ghaṭaḥ ityādi tathā eva gṛhāṇa ghaṭa jñānam paṭa jñānam iti vat jñātaḥ ghaṭaḥ jñāsyate jñāyate iti katham asambaddhayoḥ dharma dharmi bhāvaḥ iti ced dhvastaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti yathā etat api katham iti ced nūnam dhvaṃsena api ghaṭe kiñcid kriyate iti vaktu madhya vasitaḥ asi tad nirūpaṇa adhīna nirūpaṇaḥ dhvaṃsaḥ svabhāvāt eva tadīyaḥ iti kim atra sambandha antareṇa iti ced prakṛte api evam eva 
NKA_4.15–4.17	 etena phala anādhāra tvāt arthaḥ katham karma iti nirastam vināśya vat karaṇa vyāpāra viṣaya tvena tad upapatteḥ svābhāvika phala nirūpaka tvañca tulyam nanu jñānam atīndriya tvāt asādhāraṇa kārya anumeyam tad abhāve katham anumīyeta apratītañca katham vyavahāra patham avataret iti jñāna vyavahārāni atha anupapattyā jñāta tā kalpanam tat api asat paraspara āśraya prasaṅgāt jñāta tayā hi jñānam anumīyeta jñāte ca tad vyavahārāni atha anupapattiḥ tām jñāpayet kutas ca jñānam atīndriyam indriyeṇa anupalabhyamāna tvāt iti ced na anumāna upanyāse sādhya aviśiṣṭa tvāt anupalabdhi mātra upanyāse tu yogyatā viśeṣitā asau katham aindriyikā upalambha abhāvam gamayet tad viśeṣaṇe tu katham atīndriyam jñānam iti 
NKA_4.18^1	 tathāvidha jñāta tāna āśraya tvāt iti ced na āśraya asiddheḥ vyavahārānyatha anupapattyā eva siddhaḥ āśrayaḥ iti ced na jñāna hetunā eva tad upapatteḥ tasya ātma manaḥ saṃyoga ādi rūpasya sattve api suṣupti daśāyām artha vyavahāra abhāvāt na evam iti ced na tāvat mātrasya vyavahāra ahetu tvāt anyathā jñāna svīkāre api tulya tvāt smaraṇāni atha anupapatya iti ced na tasya api asiddheḥ asti tāvat vyavahāra nimittam kiñcid iti ced kim atas  na hi etāvatā jñānam tat iti siddhyati tasya eva asiddheḥ tathā api niyatasya kartuḥ pravṛtteḥ kartṛ dharmeṇa eva kenacid pravṛtti hetunā bhavitavyam iti ced astu icchā pratyakṣa siddhāḥ na tu jñānam 
NKA_4.18^2	 sā eva katham niyata adhikaraṇe utpadyatām iti ced na jñāna abhyupagame api tulya tvāt sva hetoḥ kutaścid iti ced tatas eva icchāḥ tu kim jñāna kalpanayā iti syāt etat prakāśamāne khalu arthe tad upāditsādiḥ upajāyate na tu suṣupti avasthāyāma prakāśamāne api arthe iti anubhava siddham tatas icchāyāḥ kāraṇam vilakṣaṇam eva kiñcid parikalpanīyam yasmin sati susvāpa lakṣaṇam audasīnyam artha viṣayam ātmanaḥ nivartate iti ced hanta evam susvāpa nivṛttim anubhava niddhām pratijānānena jñānam eva aparokṣyam iṣyante acetayan= eva hi suṣuptaḥ iti ucyate acaitanya nivṛttiḥ eva hi caitanyam jñānam iti tathā ca kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ hetuḥ 
NKA_4.19^1	 etena kṣaṇika tvāt iti nistam api ca kim idam kṣaṇika tvam nāma yadi āśutara vināśi tvam tadā anaikāntikam atha ekakṣaṇa avasthāyi tvam tat asiddham pramāṇa abhāvāt nanu sthāyi vijñānam yādṛśam artha kṣaṇam gṛhṇat utpadyate dvitīye api kṣaṇe kim tādṛśam eva gṛṇhāti anyādṛśam vā na vā kam api iti na prathamaḥ tasya kṣaṇasya atīta tvāt pratyakṣa jñānasya ca vartamānā abhava tvāt na ca atītam eva vartamāna tayā ullikhati bhrānta tva prasaṅgāt na dvitīyaḥ viramya vyāpāra ayogāt prathamatas api tathā abhyupagame anāgata avekṣaṇa prasaṅgāt 
NKA_4.19^2	 na tṛtīyaḥ jñāna tva hāneḥ iti mahāvratīyāḥ tat asat jñānam gṛṇhāti iti asya eva ār athasya anabhyupagamāt api tu tat eva grahaṇam iti abhyupagamaḥ tathā ca jñānam prathame yam artham ālambya jātam dvitīye api kṣaṇe tad ālambanam eva tat nava iti praśna arthaḥ tatra tad ālambanam eva tat iti parama arthaḥ na ca evam bhrānta tvam viparīta anavagāhanāt tathā api jñeya nivṛttau katham jñāna anuvṛttiḥ tad anuvṛttau vā katham jñeya nivṛttiḥ iti ced kim asmin= anupapannam na hi jñānam arthaḥ ca iti ekam tattvam eka āyuṣkam vā iti 
NKA_4.20^1	 sati api vā kṣaṇika tve katham apratyakṣam ittham yathā ucyate na sva prakāśam vastu tva āditara vastu vat na ca jñāna antara grāhyam jñāna yaugapadya niṣedhena samāna kālasya tasya abhāvāt grāhaka kāle grāhyasya atīta tvena vartamāna abha tva anupapatteḥ grāhya kāle ca grāhakasya anāgata tvāt iti ced nanu evam jñāta tā api na pratyakṣā syāt kṣaṇika tvāt katham ittham na sva prakāśāḥ vastu tvāt na janaka grāhyā anāgata tvāt viramya vyāpāra ayogāt ca na sama samaya jñāna grāhyā jñāna janaka indriya sambandhān anubhavāt 
NKA_4.20^2	 na ca tad uttara jñāna grāhyā tadānīm atīta tvāt iti kṣaṇika tvam eva tasyāḥ kutas iti ced tvad ukta yukteḥ eva tathā hi yam kṣaṇam āśritya jātā tatas param api tam eva āśrayante anyam vā na vā kam api iti tatra na prathamaḥ tasya tadānīm asattvāt na dvitīyaḥ apratisaṅkramāt eka kṣaṇa avagāhini ca jñāne tad anyakṣaṇa āśraya jñāta tā phala tvena bhrānta tva prasaṅgāt rajata avagāhini purovarti vṛtti jñāta tā phalaḥ iva na ca anyam api kṣaṇam jñānam avagāhate tadānīm tasya asattvāt na tṛtīyaḥ niḥsvabhāvatā prasaṅgāt na hi asau tadānīm tadīyāni adīyā vā iti 
NKA_4.21–4.22	 atītena api tena eva kṣaṇena upalakṣita anuvartate iti ced evam tarhi vartamāna artha tā prakāśasya na syāt anyathā jñānasya api tathā anuvṛtteḥ kaḥ doṣaḥ na hi vartamāna artha prakāśa sambandham antareṇa jñānasya anyā vartamāna avabhāsa tā nāma artha nirapekṣa prakāśana anuvṛtti mātreṇa tathātve bhūta bhāvi viṣayasya api jñānasya tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt atha mā bhūt ayam doṣaḥ iti sthūlaḥ eva vartamānaḥ prakāśena āśrīyate iti abhyupagamaḥ tadā tat jñānasya api saḥ eva viṣayaḥ iti tasya api na kṣaṇika tvam iti 
NKA_4.23	 nanu jñānam aindriyakam ced viṣaya sañcāraḥ na syāt sañjāta sambandha tvāt na ca jijñāsā niyamān niyamaḥ tasyāḥ saṃśaya pūrvaka tvāt tasya ca dharmi jñāna pūrvaka tvāt dharmiṇaḥ ca sannidhi mātreṇa jñāne jijñāsā apekṣaṇe vā ubhayathā api anavasthānāt iti tat na jñāta tā pakṣe api tulya tvāt tasyāḥ api hi jñeya tve tad paramparā jñāna āpātāt jijñāsā niyamasya ca tadvat anupapatteḥ naca indriya sambandha vicchedāt virāmaḥ iti yuktam ātma prākaṭyā vyāpanāt svabhāvataḥ eva kācid asau= ajijñāsitā api jñāyate na tu sarva iti ced tulyam prāk utpanna jñāta tā smaraṇa janita jijñāsaḥ samunmīlita nayanaḥ sañjāta jñāna samutpādita prākaṭyam jijñāsuḥ eva pratipadyate iti atas na anavasthā iti ced tulyam etat 
NKA_4.24	 nanu jñānam na sa vikalpaka grāhyam tasya nirvikalpaka pūrvaka tvāt nirvikalpaka gṛgītasya tāvat kāla anavasthānāt tasya tena eva vināśāt na api kevala nirvikalpaka vedyam tasya sa vikalpa ka unneya tvena tad abhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt na ca samavāya abhāva vat nirvikalpaka nirapekṣa sa vikalpaka gocara tvam jñānasya iti sāmpratam tayoḥ viśeṣaṇa aṃśasya prāk grahaṇāt anumāna ādi vat tad upapatteḥ prakṛte tu jñāna tva ādeḥ anupalabdheḥ agṛhīta viśeṣaṇāyāḥ ca buddheḥ viśeṣya anupasaṅkramāt katham evam syāt na utpanna mātrasya eva bāhya viṣaya jñānasya ālocanāt tatas tat puraḥsaram prathamatas eva tad jātīyasya jñāna antarasya vikalpanāt indriya sannikarṣasya tadā eva viśeṣaṇa grahaṇa lakṣaṇa sahakāri sampatteḥ vyakti antara samavetam api hi sāmānyam gṛhītam tat eva iti upayujyate anyathā anumāna ādi vikalpānām anutpāda prasaṅgaḥ tad gatasya viśeṣaṇasya agrahaṇāt anya gatasya ca anupayogāt kim liṅga grahaṇa sahakāri syāt iti etena śabda ādi pratyakṣam vyākhyātam iti 
NKA_4.25^1	 syāt etat viṣaya nirūpyam hi jñānam iṣyate na ca atīndriyasya paramāṇu ādeḥ manasā vedanam asti na ca agṛhītasya viśeṣaṇa tvam na ca nitya parokṣasya aparokṣa viśiṣṭa buddhi viṣaya tvam vyāghātāt iti na bāhya indriya grāhyasya agrāhyasya vā pūrva jñāna upanītasya eva manasā vedanāt anyathā atīndriya smaraṇasya api anutpatti prasaṅgāt iyān= tu viśeṣaḥ tasmin sati tad balāt eva asati tu tad janita vāsanā balāt na ca evam sati smaraṇam etat agṛhīta jñāna gocara tvāt na ca viṣaya aṃśe tat tathā syāt iti yuktam avacchedaka tayā prāc avasthāvat avabhāsanāt na ca pratyabhijñānam api grahaṇa smaraṇa ākāram virodhāt 
NKA_4.25^2–4.26	 atha grahaṇa smaraṇayoḥ kiyatī sāmagrī adhikor atha sannikarṣaḥ grahaṇasya saṃskāra mātram sannikarṣaḥ smaraṇasya atha grahaṇa tve api kutas etat aparokṣa ākāram kāraṇa antara nirapekṣeṇa saṃskāra adhika sannikarṣavata indriyeṇa janita tvāt atha kaḥsannikarṣaḥ jñānena saṃyukta samavāyaḥ tad arthena saṃyukta samaveta viśeṣaṇa tvam iti manasaḥ nirapekṣasya bahis vyāpāre andha badhira ādi abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced jñāna avacchedakam prati na ayam doṣaḥ na ca jñāna apekṣayā bahis iti asti na api tad viṣaya apekṣayā nirapekṣa tvam tasya eva jñānasya apekṣaṇāt atha api jñānam pratyakṣam iti atra kim pramāṇam pratyakṣam eva yat asūtrayat jñāna vikalpānām bhāva abhāva saṃvedanāt adhyātmam iti 
NKA_4.27	 nanu na īśvara jñānam pramā nitya tvena aphala tvāt na api pramāṇam akāraka tvāt atas eva ca na tad aśrayaḥ pramātā iti ucyate mitiḥ samyak paricchittiḥ tadvat tā ca pramātṛ tā tad ayoga vyavacchedaḥ pramāṇyam gautame mate samīcīnaḥ hi anubhavaḥ pramā iti vyavastathitam tathā ca anitya tvena viśeṣaṇam anarthakam nitya anubhava siddhau tad vyavacchedabhyā aniṣṭa tvāt asiddhau ca vyavacchedya abhāvāt na ca idam anumānam āśraya asiddhi bādhayoḥ anyatara ākrānta tvāt na tat pramākaraṇam iti tviṣyate eva pramayā sambandha abhāvāt tad āśrayasya tu pramātṛ tvam etat eva yat tad samavāyaḥ kāraka tve sati iti tu viśeṣaṇam pūrvavat nirarthakam anusandheyam yadi evam āpta prāmāṇyāt iti sūtra virodhaḥ tena hi īśvarasya prāmāṇyam pratipādyate na tu pramātṛ tvam iti ced na nimitta samāveśena vyavahāra samāveśa avirodhāt pramāsam avāyaḥ hi pramātṛ vyavahāra nimittam pramayā tvayā ayoga vyavacchedena sambandhaḥ pramāṇa vyavahāra nimittam tat ubhayañceśvare atra api kāryayā iti viśeṣaṇam pūrvavat anarthakam ūhanīyam
