NKA_4.28	 syāt etat pramīyate anena iti pramāṇam pramiṇoti iti pramātā iti kāraka śabda tvam anayoḥ tathā ca katham akārakam arthaḥ iti ced na etasya vyutpatti mātra nimitta tvāt pravṛtti nimittam tu yathā upadarśitam eva vyavasthāpanāt anyathā asmad ādiṣu na pramātṛ vyavahāraḥ syāt sarvatra svātantrya abhāvāt karaṇa vyavahāraḥ tu anyatra yadi api anya nimittakaḥ api tathā api iha ukta nimitta vivakṣayā eva iti evantarhi pañcama pramāṇa abhyupagame apasiddhāntaḥ na hi tat pratyakṣam anumānam āgamaḥ vā anindriya liṅga śabda karaṇa tvāt na sākṣātkāri pramāvat tayā pratyakṣa antarbhāvāt indriya artha sannikarṣa utpanna tvasya ca laukika mātra viṣaya tvāt 
NKA_4.29–4.30	 syāt etat tathā api īśvara jñānam na pramā viparyaya tvāt yadā khalu etat asmad ādi vibhramānālambate tadā etasya viṣayam aspṛśataḥ na jñāna avagāhana sambhavaḥ iti tad arthaḥ api ālambanam abhyupeyam tathā ca tat api viparyayaḥ viparīta artha ālambana tvāt tad anavagāhane vā asmad ādeḥ vibhramān aviduṣaḥ tad upaśamāya upadeśānām asarvajña pūrvakatvam iti na vibhramasya aprāmāṇye api tad viṣayasya tattvam ullikhataḥ abhra anta tvāt anyathā bhrānti samuccheda prasaṅgaḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā api āropita artha vacchinna jñāna ālambana tvena katham na bhrānta tvam iti ced na yat yatra na asti tatra tasya avagatiḥ iti bhrānti artha tvāt etad ālambanaḥ ta ca evam ullakhataḥ sarvatra yathārtha tvāt na hi na tat rajatam na api tatra asat na api tat na avagatam iti sākṣāt kāriṇi nitya yogini para dvāra anapekṣa sthitau bhūta artha anubhave niviṣṭa nikhila prastāri vastukramaḥ leśa adṛṣṭi nimitta duṣṭi vigama prabhraṣṭa śaṅkā tuṣaḥ śaṅkā unmeṣa kalaṅkibhiḥ kim aparaiḥ tat me pramāṇam śivaḥ 
NKA_5.1–5.2	 nanu īśvare pramāṇa upapattau satyām sarvam etat evam syāt tat eva tu na paśyāmaḥ iti ced na hi eṣa sthāṇoḥ aparādhaḥ yat enam andhaḥ na paśyati tathā hi kāryā ayojana dhṛtya ādeḥ padāt pratyayataḥ śruteḥ vākyāt saṅkhyā viśeṣāt ca sādhyaḥ viśva vid avyayaḥ kṣiti ādi kartṛ pūrvakam kārya tvāt iti na bādhaḥ asya upajīvya tvāt pratibandhaḥ na durbalaiḥ siddhi asiddhyoḥ virodhaḥ naḥ na asiddhiḥ anibandhanā 
NKA_5.3	 tathā hi atra ye śarīra prasaṅgam udghāṭayanti kaḥ teṣām āśayaḥ kim īśvaram pakṣayitvā kartṛ tvāt śarīri tvam tatas śarīra vyāvṛtteḥ akartṛ tvam atha kṣiti ādikam eva pakṣayitvā kāryatvāt śarīri kartṛka tvam yat vā śarīra ajanya tvāt akārya tvam tatas eva vākartṛka tvam para vyāpti stambhana artham viparīta vyāpti upadarśana mātram vā iti tatra prathama dvitīyayoḥ āśraya asiddhi bādhāpa siddhānta pratijñā virodhāḥ tṛtīye tu vyāptau satyām na idam aniṣṭam asatya antu na prasaṅgaḥ caturthe bādhān ekāntau pañcametu asamartha viśeṣaṇa tvam ṣaṣṭhe apinā gṛhyamāṇa viśeṣayā vyāptyā bādhaḥ na ca agṛhyamāṇā viśeṣayā vyāptyā gṛhyamāṇa viśeṣāyāḥ sat pratipakṣa tvam asti ca kāryatva vyāpteḥ pakṣa dharma tā parigrahaḥ viśeṣaḥ kartā aśarīrī viparītaḥ na kartā iti ca anayoḥ tad virahaḥ 
NKA_5.4	 nanu yat buddhimat hetukam tat śarī hetukam iti niyame yat śarīra hetukam na bhavati tat buddhimat hetukam api na bhavati iti viryaya niyamopi syāt tathā ca pakṣa dharma tā api labhyate iti ced na gagana ādeḥ sa pakṣa bhāgasya api sambhavāt kevala vyatirekitva anupapatteḥ anvaye tu viśeṣaṇā sāmarthyāt hetu vyāvṛtti mātram eva hi tatra kartṛ vyāvṛtti vyāptam na tu śarīra rūpa hetu vyāvṛttiḥ iti uktam vyāptaḥ ca pakṣa dharmaḥ upayujyate na tu anyaḥ ati prasaṅgāt etena tad vyāpaka rahita tvāt iti sāmānya upasaṃhārasya asiddha tvam uktam veditavyam na hi yat vyāvṛttiḥ yat abhāve anvaya vyatirekābhyām upasaṃhartum aśakyā tat tasya vyāpakam nāma iti 
NKA_5.5–5.6	 viśeṣa virodhaḥ tu viśeṣa siddhau saha upalambhena tad asiddhau mithas dharmi parihāra anupalambhena nirastaḥ na āśaṅkām api adhirohati iti syāt etat asti tāvat kāryasya avāntara viśeṣaḥ yatas śarīri kartṛka tvam anumīyate tathā ca tad prayuktām eva vyāptam upajīvet kāryatva sāmānyam iti syāt na syāt na hi viśeṣa usti iti sāmānyam aprayojakam tathā asati saurabha kaṭu tva nīlim ādi viśeṣe sati na dhūma sāmānyam agniṅga mayet kim nāma sādhaka sāmānye sādhya sāmānyam āśritya pravartamāne tad viśeṣaḥ sādhya viśeṣa vyāptim āśrayet na tu viśeṣe sati sāmānyam akiñcitkaram tasya api viśeṣa antara apekṣa yā kiñcitkara tva prasaṅgāt 
NKA_5.7	 saurabha ādi viśeṣam vihāya api dhūme vanhiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na tu viśeṣam vihāya kārye kartā iticed na kārya viśeṣaḥ kāraṇa viśeṣe vyavatiṣṭhate na tu kārya kāraṇa sāmānyayoḥ pratibandham anyathākuryāt iti kim na dṛṣṭam kāryam kāraṇa mātre aṅkuraḥ bīje tad viśeṣaḥ dhānye tad viśeṣaḥ śālau tad viśeṣaḥ kalame ityādi bahulam loke kva vā dṛṣṭa maṇu dravya ārabhyam dravyam nitya rūpa ādi ārabdham rūpa ādi tathā api sāmānya vyāpteḥ avirodhāt siddhi ati eva avaśyañca etat evam aṅgīkartavyam anyathā kāryatvasya akasmika tva prasaṅgāt 
NKA_5.8	 syāt etat anvayayvatireki tāvat idam kāryatvam iti parama arthaḥ tatra ākāśa ādeḥ vipakṣāt kim kartṛ vyāvṛtteḥ kāryatva vyāvṛttiḥ āhosvit kāraṇa mātra vyāvṛtteḥ iti sandihyate tat asat kartuḥ api kāraṇa tvāt kāraṇeṣu ca anyatama vyatirekasya api kārya anutpattim prati prayojaka tvāt anyathā kāraṇa tva vyāghātāt karaṇa ādi viśeṣa vyatireka sandeha prasaṅgāt ca katham hi niścīyate kim ākāśāt kāraṇa vyāvṛttyā kāryatva vyāvṛttiḥ uta karaṇa vyāvṛttyā evam kim upādāna vyāvṛttyā kim asamavāyi vyāvṛttyā kim nimitta vyāvṛttyā iti kāryatvāt karaṇam upādānam asamavāyi nimittam vā buddhi ādiṣu na siddhyet kartuḥ kāraṇa tve siddhe sarvam etat ucitam tat eva tu asiddham iti ced kim paṭa ādau kuvinda ādiḥ akāraṇam eva kartā prastute vā udāsīnaḥ eva sādhayitum upakrāntaḥ tasmāt yat kiñcid etat api iti 
NKA_5.9^1	 nanu kartā kāraṇānām adhiṣṭātā sākṣāt vā śarīta vat sādhya paramparayā vā daṇḍa ādi vat tatra na pūrvaḥ paramāṇu ādīnām śarīra tva prasaṅgāt na dvatīyaḥ dvāra abhāvāt na hi kasyacid sākṣāt adhiṣṭeyasya abhāve paramparayā ādhiṣṭānam sambhavati tat ayam pramāṇa arthaḥ paramāṇu ādayaḥna sākṣāt cetana adhiṣṭheyāḥ śarīra itara tvāt yat punar sākṣāt adhiṣṭheyam na tat evam yathā asmad śarīram iti na api paramparayā adhiṣṭheyāḥ sva vyāpāre śarīra anapekṣa tvāt sva ceṣṭāyām asmad śarīra vat vyatirekeṇa vā daṇḍa ādi udāharaṇam evañca kṣiti ādi na cetanā adhiṣṭhita hetukam śarīra itara hetuka tvāt iti atipīḍayā sat pratipakṣa tvam api ca paṭa ādau kuvinda ādeḥ kim kāraka adhiṣṭhāna artham apekṣā teṣām acetanānām svatas apravṛtteḥ 
NKA_5.9^2	 āho kāraka tvena na pūrvaḥ teṣām parameśvareṇa eva adhiṣṭhānāt na hi asya jñānam icchā prayatnaḥ vā vema ādīn na vyāpnoti iti sambhavati na ca adhiṣṭhitānām adhiṣṭhātṛ antara apekṣā tad artham eva tathā asatyanavasthānāt eva aviśeṣāt na dvitīyaḥ adhiṣṭhātṛ tvasya anaṅga tva prasaṅge dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya vikala tva āpatteḥ na ca hetu tvena eva tasya apekṣāḥ tu iti vācyam evam tarhi yat kāryam tat sa hetukam iti vyāptiḥ na tu sa kartṛkam iti tathā ca tayā eva prayoge siddha sādhanāt kiñca anitya prayatna pūrvakatva prayuktām vyāptim upajīvat kārya tvam na buddhimat pūrvaka tvena svabhāva pratibaddham na hi anitya prayatnaḥ api buddhyā śarīra vat kāraṇa tvena apekṣyate yena tad nivṛttau= api akāryā buddhiḥ na nivartate iti 
NKA_5.10^1	 tat etat prāk eva nirasta prāyam na uttarāntaram apekṣate tathā hi sākṣāt adhiṣṭhātari sādhye paramāṇu ādīnām śarīra tva prasaṅgaḥ iti kim idam śarīra tvam yat prasajyate yadi sākṣāt prayatna vat adhiṣṭheya tvam tat iṣyate eva na ca tatas anyat prasañjakam api atha indriya āśraya tvam tat na tad avacchinna jñāna janana dvāreṇa indriyāṇām upayogāt anavacchinne prayatne na ayam vidhiḥ nitya tvāt atas eva na artha āśraya tvam na hi nitya jñānam bhoga rūpam abhoga rūpam vā yatnam apekṣate tasya kāraṇa viśeṣa tvāt na ca nitya sarvajñasya bhoga sambhāvanā api viśeṣa adarśana abhāve mithyājñānānavakāśe doṣa an utpattau dharma adharmayoḥ asattvāt tasmāt sākṣāt prayatnān adhiṣṭheya tvāt sva vyāpāre tad anapekṣa tvāt ca iti dvayam sādhya aviśiṣṭam 
NKA_5.10^2	 anindriya āśraya tvāt abhoga āyatana tvāt sva vyāpāre tad anapekṣa tvāt ca iti trayam api anyathā siddham abhoga āyatana tvāt anindriya āśrayaḥ api bhoktṛ karma anupagrahāt abhoga āyatanam api sparśavat vegavat dravya antaranudya tvāt tad anapekṣam api syāt acetana tvāt cetanā adhiṣṭhatam api syāt iti kaḥ virodhaḥ tathā ca sākṣāt prayatna adhiṣṭhita itara janya tvāt iti sādhya samaḥ indriya āśrayeta rajanyatvāt bhoga āyatana itara janya tvāt iti dvayam api anyathā siddham kārya jñāna ādi avapekṣa tvāt śarīretara janyam api syāt acetana hetuka tvāt cetanā adhiṣṭhitukam apī iti kaḥ virodhaḥ aprasiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ capakṣaḥ na hi cetanā anadhiṣṭhata hetuka tvam kvacid pramāṇa siddham na ca cetanā adhiṣṭhita hetukatva niṣedhaḥ sādhyaḥ hetoḥ asādha araṇya prasaṅgāt gagana ādeḥ api sa pakṣāt vyāvṛtteḥ 
NKA_5.11^1	 yat punaruktam kuvinda ādeḥ paṭa ādau katham apekṣā iti tatra kārakatayā iti kaḥsandehaḥ kintu kāraka tvam eva tasya jñāna cikīrṣā prayatnavataḥ na svarūpavataḥ tat eva ca adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam yat tu adhiṣṭhite kim adhiṣṭhānena iti tat kim kuvindaḥ udvāryate īśvaraḥ vā anavasthā vā apādyate na prathamaḥ anvaya vyatireka siddha tvāt na dvatīyaḥ paramāṇu adṛṣṭa adhiṣṭhātṛ tva siddhau jñāna ādīnām sarva viṣaya tve vema ādi adhiṣṭhānasya api nyāya prāpta tvāt na tu tad adhiṣṭhāna artham eva īśvara siddhiḥ na tṛtīyaḥ tasmin pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā api eka adhiṣṭhitam aparaḥ kimartham adhitiṣṭhati iti praśne kim uttaram iti ced hetu praśnaḥ ayam prayojana praśnaḥ vā 
NKA_5.11^2	 na ādyaḥ īśvara adhiṣṭhānasya nitya tvāt kuvinda ādi adhiṣṭhānasya sva hetu adhīna tvāt na dvitīyaḥ kārya niṣpādanena bhoga siddheḥ spaṣṭa tvāt eka adhiṣṭhānena eva kāryam syāt iti ced syāt eva tathā api na sambhede anyatara vaiyarthyam parimāṇam prati saṅkhyā parimāṇa pracaya vat pratyekam sāmarthya upalabdhau sambhūyakāri tva upapatteḥ asti tatra vaijātyam iti ced iha api kiñcid bhaviṣyati iti na ca akurvataḥ kulāla ādeḥ kāya saṅkṣobha ādi sādhyaḥ bhogaḥ siddhyet iti tad artham asya kartṛ tvam īśvaraḥ anumanyate tad artha mātra tvāt aiśvaryasya iti 
NKA_5.12	 yatu anitya prayatnā ityādi bhavet api evam yadi anitya prayatna nivṛttau= eva buddhiḥ api nivarteta na tu etat asti udāsīnasya prayatna abhāve api buddhi sadbhāvāt hetu bhūtā buddhiḥ nivat tate ithi ced na udāsīna buddheḥ api saṃskāram prati hetu tvāt kāraka viṣayā buddhiḥ nivartate iti ced na udāsīnasya api kāraka boddhṛ tvāt na hi ghaṭa ādikam akurvantaḥ cakra ādikam na īkṣāmahe hetu bhūtā kāraka buddhiḥ nivartate iti ced na ayatamānasya api duḥkha hetu bhūtāyāḥ api tad hetu kaṇṭaka sparśa buddheḥ bhāvāt cikīrṣā hetu bhūtaḥ anubhavaḥ nivartate iti ced na kenacid nimittena akurvataḥ api cikīrṣā tad hetu buddhi sambhavā tat anapekṣa kṛti hetu cikīrṣā kāraṇam buddhiḥ nivartate iti ced na tarhi buddhi mātram tathā ca anitya prayatna hetuka tva prayuktam viśiṣṭa prayatna cikīrṣā hetu buddhimat pūrvaka tvam iti tad nivṛttau tat eva nivartatām na tu buddhimat pūrvakatva mātram tatra tasya aprayojaka tvāt iti buddhimat pūrvaka tva sādhya pakṣe parīhāraḥ sa kartṛkam iti prayatna pradhāna pakṣe śaṅkā eva na asti tasya eva tatra anupādhi tvāt 
NKA_5.13	 etena śarīra sambandhe buddhi gata kāryatva vat buddhi sambandhe prayatna gata kārya tvam upādhiḥ iti nirastam yaḥ hi buddhyā śarīra vat śarīra nivṛttyā buddhi nivṛtti vat vā prayatnena buddhim buddhi nivṛttyā prayatna nivṛttim sādhayet saḥ evam kadācid upālabhyaḥ vayantu avagata hetu bhāvam kalita śakti sakala kāraka prayoktāram kāryāt eva anumimānāḥ na evam āskandanīyāḥ tatra tasya anupādhi tvāt 
NKA_5.14–5.15	 na ca prayatnaḥ ātma lābha artham eva matim apekṣate viṣaya lābha artham api apekṣaṇāt tatas prayatnāt buddhiḥ tad nivṛtteḥ ca prayatna nivṛttiḥ siddhyā iti vistṛtam anyatra kārya buddhi nivṛttyā tu kāryaḥ eva prayatnaḥ nivartate na nityaḥ nitye ca prayatne nityā eva buddhiḥ pravartate na anityāḥ na hi tayā tasya viṣaya lābha sambhavaḥ śarīra ādeḥ prāk tad asambhave deha an utpattau sarvadā anutpatteḥ śarīra ajanya tva vat ca anitya prayatna ajanya tvam iti saṅkṣepaḥ tarka ābhāsatayā anyeṣām tarka aśuddhiḥ adūṣaṇam anukūlaḥ tu tarkaḥ atra kārya lopaḥ vibhūṣaṇam kāraka vyāpāra vigame hi kārya anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ cetana acetana vyāpārayoḥ hetu phala bhāva avadhāraṇāt kāraṇa antara abhāvaḥ iva kartṛ abhāve kārya anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ kartuḥ apikāraṇa tvāt 
NKA_5.16^1	 yaḥ tu āha pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām tad utpatti niścayaḥ dṛśyayoḥ eva na tu adṛśyayoḥ pratyakṣasya anupalambhasya ca tāvat mātra vidhi niṣedha samartha tvāt dhūma agni vat kampa māruta vat ca na hi dhūmaḥ kāryaḥ analasya iti udaryasya api na hi śākhā kampaḥ mātariśvanaḥ iti stimitasya api syāt kintu bhauma spṛśyayoḥ eva tathā iha api śarīravataḥ eva kāraṇa tvam avagantum ucitam na anyasya iti tat asat pratyakṣa anupalambhau hi dṛśya viṣayau= upāyaḥ tad utpatti niścaye na tu dṛśyatā eva tatra upeyā kinnāma dṛśya āśritam sāmānya dvayam 
NKA_5.16^2	 tad ālīḍhasya hi tad utpatti niścaye dṛśyam adṛśyam vā sarvam eva tat jātīyam tad utpattimat tayā niścitam bhavati yathā sparśa rūpa rasa gandhānām uttarottara nimitta tāyām tava asmākañcā atīndriya samavāya ādi siddhau naced evam udāhṛtayoḥ eva dahana pavanayoḥ āloka rūpavatoḥ tad utpatti niścaye kathana āloka nirasta rūpayoḥ siddhiḥ yat udarya stimita sādhāraṇī siddhiḥsyāt iti tat bhavet api evam yadi śarīra ādikam vinā kāryam iva bhaumam sparśavat vegavan tañca vinā agni mātrāt pavana mātrāt vā dhūma kampau syātām na tu evam na ca evam cetana vyabhicāraḥ api śakya abhidhānaḥ iti alam bāla pralāpānām samādhānaiḥ 
NKA_5.17	 tad utpatteḥ asiddhau= api tad tad upādhi vidhūnanena svābhāvika tva sthitau yadi kartāram atipatya kāryam syāt svabhāvam eva atipatet iti kārya vilopa prasaṅgaḥ iti etat ca sarvam ātma tattva viveke nipuṇataram upapāditam iti na iha pratanyate evañca siddhe pratibandhe na pratibandya ādeḥ pratibandya ādeḥ kṣudra upadravasya avakāśaḥ pratibandha siddha āviṣṭa āpādanāt tad asiddhau tatas eva tad siddheḥ aprasaṅgāt iti nanu tasya sarvadā sarvatra aviśeṣe kāryasya sarva dā utpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti nirapekṣa īśvara pakṣe doṣaḥ sa apekṣe upekṣaṇīyaḥ eva astu iti bālasya pradīpa kalikā krīḍayā eva nagara dāhaḥ tat na sthema bhājaḥ jagataḥ eva akāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt om iti bruvataḥ saugatasya dattam uttaram prāk 
NKA_5.18	 ārṣam dharma upadeśañca veda śāstra avirodhinā yaḥ tarkeṇa anusandhatte sa dharmam veda na itaraḥ tam imam artham āgamaḥ saṃvadati visaṃvadati tu pareṣām vicāram viśvatas cakṣuḥ uta viśvatomukhaḥ viśvatobāhuḥ uta viśvataspād sam bāhubhyām dhamati sam patatraiḥ dyāvābhūmī janayan devaḥ ekaḥ atra prathamena sarvajña tvam cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭeḥ upalakṣaṇāt dvitīyena sarva vaktṛ tvam mukhena vāc upalakṣaṇāt tṛtīyena sarva sahakāri tvam bāhunā sahakāri tva upalakṣaṇāt caturthena vyāpaka tvam padā vyāpteḥ upalakṣaṇāt pañcamena dharma adharma lakṣaṇa pradhāna kāraṇa tvam tau hi lokayātrā vahanāt bāhū ṣaṣṭhena paramāṇu rūpa pradhāna adhiṣṭheya tvam te hi gati śīla tvāt patatra vyapadeśāḥ patanti iti sandhamati san janayan= iti ca vyavahita upasarga sambandhaḥ tena saṃyojayati samutpādayan= iti arthaḥ dyāvāḥ iti ūrdhva sapta loka upalakṣaṇam bhūmi iti adhastāt ekaḥ iti anāditā iti smṛtiḥ api aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ mattaḥ sarvam pravartate ityādiḥ etena brahma ādi pratipādakāḥ āgamāḥ boddhavyāḥ 
NKA_5.19–5.20^1	 āyojanāt khalu api svātantrye jaḍa tā ha aniḥ na adṛṣṭam dṛṣṭa ghātakam hetu abhāve phala abhāvaḥ viśeṣaḥ tu viśeṣavān paramāṇu ādayaḥ hi cetanā ayojitāḥ pravartante acetana tvāt vā asya ādi vat anyathā kāraṇam vinā kārya anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ acetana kriyāyāḥ cetana adhiṣṭhāna kārya tva avadhāraṇāt kriyā viśeṣa viśrāntaḥ ayam arthaḥ na tu tanmātra gocaraḥ ceṣṭā hi cetanā adhiṣṭhānam apekṣate iti ced atha kā iyam ceṣṭā nāma yadi prayatna vat ātma saṃyoga asamavāyi kāraṇikā kriyā prayatna mātra kāraṇikā iti vā vivakṣitam tat na tasya eva tatra anupādhi tvāt 
NKA_5.19–5.20^2	 atha hita ahita prāpti parihāra phala tvam tattvam tat na viṣa bhakṣaṇa udbandhana ādya vyāpanāt iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra phala tvam iti ced kartāram prati anyam vā ubhayathā api paramāṇu ādi kriyā sādha araṇyāt aviśeṣaḥ bhrānta samīhāyāḥ atathābhūtāyāḥ api cetana vyāpāra apekṣaṇāt ca śarīra samavāyi kriyā tvam tat iti ced na mṛta śarīra kriyāyāḥ api cetana pūrvakatva prasakteḥ jīvate iti ced na netra spanda ādeḥ cetana adhiṣṭhāna abhyupagama prasaṅgāt sparśavat dravya antara aprayoge sati iti ced na jvalana pavana ādau tathā abhāva abhyupagama āpatteḥ śarīrasya sparśavat dravya antarā prayuktasya iti ced na ceṣṭayā eva śarīrasya lakṣyamāṇa tvāt 
NKA_5.21	 sāmānya viśeṣaḥ ceṣṭā tvam yatas unnīyate prayatna pūrvikā iyam kriyā iti ced na kriyā mātreṇa eva tad unnayanāt bhoktṛ buddhimat pūrvaka tvam yatas iti ced tarhi tad viśrānta tvam eva tasya na ca etāvatā eva kriyā mātram prayatna cetana mātrasya cetanā adhiṣṭhānena vyāptiḥ apasāryate viśeṣasya viśeṣam prati prayojaka tayā sāmānya vyāptim pratyavirodhaka tvāt anyathā sarva sāmānya vyāpteḥ ucchedāt iti uktam etena aśarīra tva ādinā sat pratipakṣa tvam apāstam 
NKA_5.22	 atra api āgama saṃvādaḥ yadā sa devaḥ jāgarti tadā idam ceṣṭate jagat yadā svapiti śānta ātmā tadā sarvam nimīlati ajñaḥ jantuḥ anīśaḥ ayam ātmanaḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ īśvara preritaḥ gacchet svargam vā śvabhram eva vā mayā adhyakṣeṇa prakṛtiḥ sūyate sacarācaram tapāmi aham aham varṣam nigṛṇhāmi utsṛjāmi ca ityādi atra jāgara svāpau sahakāri lābha alābhau īśvara preraṇāya āma jña tvam aprayata māna tvañca hetū darśitau paramāṇu ādi sādhāraṇau svarga śvabhre ca iṣṭa aniṣṭa upa lakṣaṇe etat eva sarva adhiṣṭhānam uttaratra vibhāvyate mayā ityādinā na kevalam preraṇāyām aham adhiṣṭhātā apitu pratirodhe api yaḥ hi yatra prabhavati sa tasya preraṇā vat dhāraṇe api samarthaḥ yathār avācīraḥ śarīra prāṇa preraṇa dhāraṇayoḥ iti darśitam tapāmi ityādinā 
NKA_5.23	 dhṛteḥ khalu api kṣiti ādi brahmāṇḍa paryantam hi jagat sākṣāt paramparayā vā vidhāraka prayatna adhiṣṭhitam guru tve satya patana dharmaka tvāt viyati vihaṅgama śarīra vat tad saṃyukta dravya vat ca etena indra agni yama ādi lokapāla pratipādakāḥ api āgamāḥ vyākhyātāḥ sarva āveśa nibandhanaḥ ca sarva tādātmya vyavahāraḥ ātmā eva idam sarvam iti yathā ekaḥ eva māyāvī aśvaḥ varāhaḥ vyāghraḥ vānaraḥ kinnaraḥ bhikṣuḥ tāpasaḥ vipraḥ ityādiḥ adṛṣṭāt eva tat upapatteḥ anyathāsidhdham idam iti ced tad bhāvepi prayatna anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānena tasya api sthitim prati kāraṇa tvāt kāraṇa eka deśasya ca kāraṇa antaram pratyanupādhi tvāt upādhi tve vā sarveṣām akāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt śarīra sthitiḥ evam na tu anya sthitiḥ iti ced na prāṇa indriyayoḥ sthiteḥ avyāpanāt prāc nyāyena apa asta tvāt ca 
NKA_5.24	 atra api āgamaḥ etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi dyāvāpṛthivyau vidhṛte tiṣṭhataḥ iti praśāsanam daṇḍa bhūtaḥ prayatnaḥ uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ tu anyaḥ paramātmā iti udāhṛtaḥ yaḥ lokatrayam āviśya vibharti avyayaḥ īśvaraḥ iti smṛtiḥ atra uttama tvam asaṃsāri tvam sarvajña tva ādi ca parama tvam sarva upāsyatā lokatrayam iti sarva upalakṣaṇam āveśaḥ jñāna cikīrṣā prayatnavataḥ saṃyogaḥ bharaṇam dhāraṇam avyaya tvam āgantuka viśeṣa guṇa śūnya tvam aiśvaryam saṅkalpa apratighātaḥ iti etena kūrma ādi viṣayāḥ api āgamāḥ vyākhyātāḥ 
NKA_5.25	 saṃharaṇāt khalu api brahmāṇḍa ādi dvi aṇuka paryantam jagat prayatna vat vināśyam vināśya tvāt pāṭyamāna paṭa vat atra api āgamaḥ eṣa sarvāṇi bhūtāni sva abhivyāpya mūrtibhiḥ janma vṛddhi kṣayaiḥ nityam sambhrāmayati cakra vat sarva bhūtāni kaunteya prakṛtim yānti māmikām kalpa kṣaye punar tāni kalpa ādau visṛjāmi aham ityādiḥ etena raudram aṃśam pratipādayanta upya āgamāḥ vyākhyātāḥ 
NKA_5.26	 padāt khalu api kāryatvāt nirūpa adhi tvam evam dhṛti vināśayoḥ vicchedena padasya api pratyaya ādeḥ ca pūrvavat pada śabdena atra padyate gamyate vyavahāra aṅgam arthaḥ anena iti vṛddha vyavahāraḥ eva ucyate atas api īśvara siddhiḥ tathā hi yat etat paṭa ādi nirmāṇa naipuṇyam kuvinda ādīnām vāc vyavahāraḥ ca vyakta vācām lipitat krama vyavahāraḥ ca bālānām sa sarvaḥ svatantra puruṣa viśrāntaḥ vyavahāra tvāt nipuṇatara śilpi nirmitā pūrva ghaṭa ghaṭanā naipuṇya vat caitra maitra ādi pada vat patra akṣara vat pāṇinīya varṇa nirdeśa kramavat ca iti 
NKA_5.27	 ādimān vyavahāraḥ evam ayantu anīdiranyathā api bhaviṣyati iticed na tat asiddheḥ ādimattām eva sādhayitum ayam ārambhaḥ na ca evam saṃsārasya anādi tva bhaṅga prasaṅgaḥ tathā api tasya avirodhāt na hi caitra ādi vyavahāraḥ ayam ādimān iti bhavasya api anāditā na asti tad anādi tve vā na caitra ādi pada vyavahāra upya ādimān iti astu arvāgdarśī kaścid eva atra mūlam iti ced na tena aśakya tvāt kalpa ādau= ādarśa ābhāsasya api asiddheḥ sādhitau ca sarga pralayau nanu vyavahārayitṛ vṛddhaḥ śarīrī samadhigataḥ naceśvaraḥ tathā tat katham evam syāt na śarīra anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyini kārye tasya apita dvat tvāt gṛṇhāti hi īśvaropi kārya vaśāt śarīram antarā antarā darśayati ca vibhūtim iti atra api āgamaḥ pitā aham asya jagataḥ mātā dhātā pitāmahaḥ tathā yadi hi ayam na varteyam jātu karmaṇi atandritaḥ mama vartma anuvartante manuṣyāḥ pārtha sarvaśas utsīdeyuḥ ime lokāḥ na kuryām karma ced aham iti etena namaḥ kulālebhyaḥ karmārebhyaḥ ityādi yajūṃṣi boddhavyāni 
NKA_5.28	 pratyayaḥ api pratyaya śabdena atra samāśvāsa viṣaya prāmāṇyam ucyate tathā ca prayogaḥ āgama sampradāyaḥ ayam kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakaḥ pramāṇa tvāt pratyakṣa ādi vat nahi prāmāṇya pratyayam vinā kvacid samāśvāsaḥ naca asiddhasya prāmāṇyasya pratītiḥ na ca svatas pramāṇyam iti āveditam na ca na idam pramāṇam mahā jana parigrahāt iti uktam na ca asarvajñaḥ dharma adharmayoḥ svātantryeṇa prabhavati nacā sarva jñasya guṇavat tā iti niḥśaṅkam etat 
NKA_5.29	 śruteḥ khalu api tathā hi sarvajña praṇītāḥ vedāḥ veda tvāt yat punar na sarvajña praṇītam na asau vedaḥ yathā itara vākyam nanu kim idam veda tvam nāma vākya tvasya adṛṣṭa viṣaya vākya tvasya ca viruddha tvāt adṛṣṭa viṣaya pramāṇa vākya tvasya ca asiddheḥ manu ādi vākye gata tvena virodhāt ceti ced na anupalabhyamāna mūla antara tve sati mahā jana parigṛhīta vākya tvasya tattvāt na hi aramat ādīnām pratyakṣa ādi mūlam na api bhrama vipralipse mahā jana parigrahāt iti uktam na api paramparā eva mūlam mahāpralaye vicchedāt iti uktam 
NKA_5.30	 anvayataḥ vā veda vākyāni pauruṣeyāṇi vākya tvāt asmad ādi vākya vat asmaryamāṇa kartṛka tvāt na evam iti ced na asiddheḥ anantarañca vaktrebhyaḥ vedāḥ tasya viniḥsṛtāḥ pratimanvantarañcā eṣā śrutiḥ anyā vidhīyate vedānta kṛt veda vid eva ca aham iti smṛteḥ tasmāt yajñāt sarva hutaḥ ṛcaḥ sāmāni jajñire ityādi śruti pāṭhaka smṛteḥ ca arthavāda mātram idamiti ced na karta smaraṇasya sarvatrāvidhi artha tvāt tathā ca asmaraṇe kālidāsa ādeḥ asmaraṇāt evañca kumāra sambhava ādeḥ akartṛka tva prasaṅgaḥ anaikāntika tvam vā hetoḥ 
NKA_5.31–5.32	 pramāṇa antara agocara artha tva asat sat pratipakṣa tvam iti ced na praṇetāram pratyasiddheḥ anyam pratyanaikāntika tvāt ākasmika smita bīja sukha anusmṛteḥ kāraṇa viśeṣasya anyam prati pramāṇa antara agocarasya api tena eva vaktrā pratipādyamāna tvāt vaktā eva prakṛte na sambhavati hetu abhāve phala abhāvāt cakṣuḥ ādīnām tatra asāmarthyāt asmad ādi indriya vat manasaḥ bahis asvātantryāt na cetanasya jñānasya indriyasya manasaḥ vā pakṣīkaraṇe āśraya asiddheḥ prāk eva prapañcanāt nitya nirākaraṇe ca asāmarthyāt paramāṇu ādayaḥ na kasyacid pratyakṣāḥ tad sāmagrī rahita tvāt iti ced na draṣṭāram pratyasiddheḥ anyam prati siddha sādhanāt 
NKA_5.33	 tathā api vākya tvam na pramāṇam aprayojaka tvāt pramāṇa antara gocara artha tva prayuktam tatra pauruṣeya tvam na tu vākya tva prayuktam na sugata ādi āgamānām apauruṣeya tva prasaṅgāt pramāṇa vākyasya sataḥ iti ced na praṇetṛ pramāṇa antara gocara artha tvasya sādhya anupravośāt svatantra puruṣa praṇīta tvam hi pauruṣeya tvam artha pratīti eka viṣayau hi vivakṣā prayatnau svātantryam manu ādi vākyasya apauruṣeya tva prasaṅgāt ca tad arthasya śabda itara pramāṇa agocara tvāt prayujyamāna vākya itara gocara artha tva mātram iti ced na tasya vede api satvāt ekasya api arthasya śākhā bhedena bahubhiḥ vākyaiḥ pratipādanāt astu evam na tu teṣāḥ mithas mūla mūli bhāvaḥ iti ced na ukta uttara tvāt 
NKA_5.34^1	 saṅkhyā viśeṣāt khalu api dvi aṇuka tri aṇuke tāvat paramāṇavatī dravya tvāt tat ca parimāṇam kāryam kārya guṇa tvāt na ca tasya paramāṇu parimāṇam dvi aṇuka parimāṇam vā kāraṇam nitya parimāṇa tvāt aṇu parimāṇa tvāt ca anyathā anāśraya kārya utpatti prasaṅgāt dvi aṇukasya mahat tva prasaṅgāt ca tri aṇukavat aṇu a ārabhyatva aviśeṣāt tatra kāraṇa bahu tvena mahat tve aṇu parimāṇasya anārambhaka tva sthiteḥ aṇu tvam eva mahat ārambhe viśeṣaḥ iti api na yuktam mahataḥ mahat anārambha prasaṅgāt aṇu tva mahat tvayoḥ viruddha tayā eka jātīya kārya anārambhaka tva prasaṅgāt 
NKA_5.34^2	 bahubhiḥ api paramāṇubhiḥ dvābhyām api dvi aṇukābhyām ārambha prasaṅgāt ca evam sati kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced paramāṇu kāryasya mahat tva prasaṅgaḥ kāraṇa bahu tvasya tad hetu tvāt anyathā dvābhyām tribhiḥ caturbhiḥ iti aniyamena api aṇvārambhe tad vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt aṇunaḥ eva tāratamya abhyupagamaḥ tu saṅkhyām avadhīrya na syāt astu mahat ārambhaḥ eva tribhiḥ iti ced na mahataḥ kāryasya kārya dravya ārambha tva niyamāt tathā api vā tāratamye saṅkhyā eva prayojikā iti na ca pracayaḥ apekṣaṇīyaḥ avayava saṃyogasya abhāvāt tasmāt parimāṇa pracayau mahataḥ eva ārambhakau= iti sthitiḥ 
NKA_5.35	 atas aneka saṅkhyā pariśiṣyate sā apekṣā buddhi janyāḥ aneka saṅkhyā tvāt na ca asmad ādīnām apekṣā buddhiḥ paramāṇuṣu sambhavati tat yasya asau sa sarvajñaḥ anyathā apekṣā buddheḥ abhāvāt saṅkhyā anutpattau tad gata parimāṇa anutpāde a parimitasya dravyasya anārambhaka tvāt tri aṇuka an utpattau viśva anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ asmāt ādīnām evā anumānikī apekṣā buddhiḥ astu iti ced na itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt jāte hi sthūla kārye tena paramāṇu ādi anumānam tasmin sati dvi aṇuka ādi krameṇa sthūla utpattiḥ astu adṛṣṭāt eva parimāṇam kṛtam apekṣā buddhyā iti ced na astu tatas eva sarvam kim dṛṣṭa kāraṇena iti ādeḥ asamādheya tva prasaṅgāt iti 
NKA_5.36	 athavā kāryā iti ādikam anyathā vyakhyāyate uddeśaḥ eva tātparyam vyākhyā viśva dṛśaḥ satī īśvara ādi padam sārtham loka vṛtta anusārataḥ āmnāyasya hi bhāvya arthasya kārye puruṣa pravṛtti nivṛttī bhūta arthasya tu yadi api na āhatya pravartaka tvam nivartaka tvam vā tathā api tātparyataḥ tatra eva prāmāṇyam tathā hi vidhi śaktiḥ eva avasīdantī stuti ādibhiḥ uttabhyate praśaste hi sarvaḥ pravartate ninditāt ca nivartate iti sthitiḥ 
NKA_5.37	 tatra pada śaktiḥ tāvat abhidhā tat bala āyātaḥ padārthaḥ ākāṅkṣa ādimattve sati ca anvaya śaktiḥ padānām padārthānām vā vākyam tad bala āyātaḥ vākya arthaḥ tātparya arthaḥ tu cintyate tat eva param sādhyam pratipādyam prayojanam uddeśyam vā yasya tat idam tat param tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam tat yat viṣayam sa tātparya arthaḥ iti syāt 
NKA_5.38	 tatra na prathamaḥ pramāṇena arthasya karmaṇaḥ asādhya tvāt phalasya ca tat pratipattitaḥ anyasya abhāvāt praśasta nindita sva artha pratipādana dvāreṇa pravṛtti nivṛtti rūpam sādhyam param ucyate iti ced na gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ iti atra tīrasya apravṛtti nivṛtti rūpasya asādhyasya api paratvāt tīra viṣaye pravṛtti nivṛttī sādhye iti tīrasya api paratvam iti ced na svarūpa ākhyāna mātreṇa api paryavasānāt 
NKA_5.39	 na dvitīyaḥ pada vākyayoḥ padārtha tad saṃsargau vihāya pratipādya antara abhāvāt pada śakti saṃsarga śaktī vinā sva artha avina abhāvena pratipādyam param ucyate iti api na sāma pratam na hi yat yat śabda arthau= inābhūtam tatra tatra tātparyam śabdasya ati prasaṅgāt tadā hi gaṅgāyām jalam ityādi api tīra param syāt avinā abhāvasya tādavasthyāt mukhye bādhake sati tat tathā syāt iti ced na tasmin= asati api bhāvāt tat yathā gaccha gacchasi ced kānta panthānaḥ santu te śivāḥ mama api janma tatra eva bhūyāt yatra gataḥ bhavān iti mukhya artha ābādhane api vāraṇe tātparyam na ca param vyāpakam eva avyāpake api tātparya darśanāt tat yathā mañcāḥ krośanti iti puruṣe tātparyam na ca mañca puruṣa yoḥ avinābhāvaḥ na api puruṣa krośanayoḥ 
NKA_5.40	 na api tṛtīyaḥ tat hi pratipādya apekṣitam pratipādaka apekṣitam vā syāt na ādyaḥ śabda prāmāṇyasya ātad adhīna tvāt tathā tve vā atiprasaṅgāt yasya yat apekṣitam tam prati tasya paratva prasaṅgāt tad artha sādhya tvena apekṣā niyamaḥ iti ced na kārya jñā api abhedena sādhyasya bahuvidha tve bhinna tātparyatayā vākya bheda prasaṅgāt dhūmasya hi pradeśa śyāmala tāmaśaka nivṛtti ādi anekam kāryam ārda indhana dahana ādi anekam jñāpyam tathā āca iha pradeśe dhūma udgamaḥ iti abhihite tātparyataḥ kaḥ vākya arthaḥ bhavet cetanā apekṣāya aniyantum aśakya tvāt na api pratipādaka upekṣitam vede tad abhāvāt 
NKA_5.41	 caturthaḥ tu syāt yat uddeśena yaḥ śabdaḥ pravṛttaḥ sa tad paraḥ tathā eva loka vyutpatteḥ tathā hi praśaṃsā vākyam upādānam uddiśya loke prayujyate tad upādāna param nindā vākyam hānam uddiśya prayujyate tat hāna param evam anyatra api svayam ūhanīyam tasmāt loka anusāreṇa vede api evam svīkāraṇīyam anyathā artha vādānām sarvathā eva anarthakya prasaṅgāt sa ca uddeśaḥ vyavasāyaḥ adhikāraḥ abhiprāyaḥ bhāvaḥ āśayaḥ iti anarthāntaram iti tad ādhāra praṇetṛ puruṣa dhaureya siddhiḥ tathā ca prayogaḥ vaidikāni praśaṃsā vākyāni upādāna abhiprāya pūrvakāṇi praśaṃsā vākya tvāt pariṇati surasamāmra phalam iti ādi loka vākya vat iti evam nindā vākyāni hāna abhiprāya pūrvakāṇi nindā vākya tvāt pariṇati virasam panasa phalam ityādi vākya vat anyathā nirarthaka tva prasaṅgaḥ ca vipakṣe bādhakam uktam 
NKA_5.42	 apica no ced evam śruta arthāpattiḥ api hīyeta siddhaḥ hi arthaḥ pramāṇa viṣayaḥ na tu tena eva kartavyaḥ na ca pīnaḥ devadattaḥ divā na bhuṅkte iti atra rātrau bhuṅkte iti vākya śeṣaḥ asti anupalambha bādhita tvāt utpatti abhivyakti sāmagrī tālu ādi vyāpāra virahāt ayogyasya āśaṅkitum api aśakya tvāt tasmāt abhiprāya sthaḥ eva pariśiṣyate gati antara abhāvāt sa ced vede na asti na asti śruta arthāpattiḥ iti tad vyutpādana ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt kāryāt tātparyāt api unnīyate asti praṇetā iti 
NKA_5.43^1	 ayojanāt khalu api na hi vedāt avyakhyātāt kaścid artham adhigacchati na ca eka deśa darśinaḥ vyākhyānam ādaraṇīyam paurvāparya aparāmṛṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ anyām kurute matim iti nyāyena anāśvāsāt tricatura padakāt api vākyāt eka deśa śrāviṇaḥ anyathā artha pratyayaḥ syāt kim uta atīndriyāt antara antarā vākya sambheda duradhi gamāt tatas sakala veda veda artha darśī kaścid eva abhyupeyaḥ anyathā andha paramparā prasaṅgāt sa ca śruta adhīta avadhṛta smṛta sāṅga upāṅga veda arthaḥ tad viparītaḥ vā na sarvajñāt anyaḥ sambhavati kohya pratyakṣīkṛta viśva tad anuṣṭhānaḥ etāvān eva ayam āmnāyaḥ iti niścinuyāt 
NKA_5.43^2	 kaḥ ca arvāk dṛś niḥśeṣāḥ śratīḥ granthator athatova adhīyīta adhyāpayet vā atra api prayogaḥ vedāḥ kadācid sarva veda artha vid vyākhyātāḥ anuṣṭhātṛ mati calane api niścala artha anuṣṭhāna tvāt yat evam tat sarvam tad artha vid vyākhyātam yathā manu ādi saṃhitā iti anyathā tvan āśvāsena avyavasthānāt ananuṣṭhānam avyavasthā vā bhavet anādeśika tvāt anuṣṭhātāraḥ eva ādeṣṭāraḥ iti ced na teṣām aniyata bodha tvāt vedavat veda artha anuṣṭhānam api anādi iti ced na tat hi svatantram vā veda artha bodhatantram vā ādye nirmūla tva prasaṅgaḥ dvitīye tu aniyama āpattiḥ na hi asarvajñā viśeṣe pūrveṣām tad avabodhaḥ pramāṇam na tu idānīntanānām iti niyāmakam asti 
NKA_5.44^1	 padāt khalu upi śrūyate hi praṇava īśvara īśāna ādi padam tat ca sārthakam avigānena śruti smṛti itihāseṣu prayujyamāna tvāt ghaṭa ādi pada vat iti sānāsyataḥ siddheḥ kaḥ asya arthaḥ iti vyutpatsoḥ vimarśe sati nirṇayaḥ svarga ādi pada vat uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ tu anyaḥ paramātmā iti udāhṛtaḥ yaḥ lokatrayam āviśya bibhartti avyayaḥ īśvaraḥ iti artha vādāt yava varāha ādi vat vākya śeṣāt vā tat yathā īśvara praṇidhānam upakramya śrūyate sarvajña tā tṛptiḥ anādi bodhaḥ svatantra tā nityam alupta śaktiḥ ananta śaktiḥ ca vibhoḥ vidhi jñāḥ ṣaṣ āhuḥ aṅgāni maheśvarasya iti evambhūtor athaḥ pramāṇa bādhitaḥ iti ced na prāk eva pratiṣedhāt tathā api na tatra pramāṇam asti iti ced svarge asti iti kā śraddhā 
NKA_5.44^2	 na hi ukta viśeṣaṇe sukhe kiñcid pramāṇam asti asmad ādīnām yājñika pravṛtti anyathā anupapatyā tathā eva tat iti avadhāryate iti ced na itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt avadhṛte hi svarga rūpe tatra pravṛttiḥ pravṛtti anyathā anupapattyā ca tad avadhāraṇam iti pūrva vṛddha pravṛttyā tad avadhāraṇe ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced na andha paramparā prasaṅgāt viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭa vaśāt kadācid kasyacid evam vidham api sukham syāt iti na asti virodhaḥ tad niṣedhe pramāṇa abhāvāt iti ced tulyam itaratra api atra api prayogaḥ yaḥ śabdaḥ yatra vṛddhaiḥ asati vṛtti antare pyujyate sa tasya vācakaḥ yathā svarga śabdaḥ sukha viśeṣe prayujyamānaḥ tasya vācakaḥ prayujyate ca ayam jagatkartarī iti anyathā nirarthaka tva prasaṅge sārthaka pada kadamba samabhivyāhāra anupapattiḥ iti 
NKA_5.44^3	 etena rudra upendra mahā indra ādi devatā viśeṣa vācakāḥ vyākhyātāḥ api ca asmat padam loka vat vede api prayujyate tasya ca loke na acetaneṣu anyatamat arthaḥ tatra sarvathā eva aprayogāt na api ātma mātram arthaḥ para ātmani api prayoga prasaṅgāt api tu yaḥ tam svātantryeṇa uccārayati tam eva āha tathā eva anvaya vyatirekābhyām avasāyāt tatas loka vyutpattim anatikramya vede api anena sva prayoktā eva vaktavyaḥ anyathā prayoga prasaṅgāt na ca yaḥ yadā uccārayati vaidikam aham śabdam saḥ eva tadā tasya arthaḥ iti yuktam tathā asati mām upāsīta iti ādau saḥ eva upāsyaḥ syāt aham sarvasyaprabhavaḥ mattaḥ sarvam pravartate iti upādhyāya śiṣya paramparā eva ātmani aiśvaryam samadhigacchet 
NKA_5.44^4	 tathā ca upāsanām pratyunmatta keliḥ syāt loka vyavahāraḥ ca ucchidyeta tasmanna anuvaktā asya vācyaḥ api tu vaktā eva iti sthite prayujyate vede asmad śabdaḥ sva prayoktṛ vacanaḥ asmad śabda tvāt loka vat iti evam anye api yaḥ kaḥ saḥ ityādi śabdāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ teṣām buddhi upakrama praśna parāmarśa ādi upahita maryāda tvāt tasya ca vaktṛ dharma tvāt buddhi apakramaḥ hi prakṛta tvam jijñāsā aviṣkaraṇañca praśnaḥ pratisandhānañca parāmarśaḥ iti evañca saṃśaya ādi vācaka api unneyāḥ na ca jijñāsā saṃśaya ādayaḥ sarvajñe pratiṣiddhāḥ iti yuktam śiṣya pratibodhanāya āhārya tvena avirodhāt kaḥ dharmaḥ katham lakṣaṇakaḥ ityādi bhāṣya vat iti etena dhik ahaḥ bata hanta ityādayaḥ nipātāḥ vyākhyātāḥ 
NKA_5.45–5.46	 pratyayāt api liṅga ādi pratyayāḥ hi puruṣa dhaureya niyoga arthāḥ bhavantaḥ tam prati pādayanti tathā hi pravṛttiḥ kṛtiḥ eva atra sā ca icchataḥ yatas ca sā tat jñānam viṣayaḥ tasya vidhiḥ tad jñāpakaḥ athavā pravṛttiḥ khalu vidhi kāryā satī na tāvat kāya parispanda mātram ātmā jñātavyaḥ iti ādya vyāpanāt na api icchā mātram tatas eva phala siddhau karma anārambha prasaṅgāt tatas prayatnaḥ pariśiṣyate ātma jñāna bhūta dayā ādau= api tasyāḥ bhāvāt tat uktam pravṛttiḥ āramabhaḥ iti 
NKA_5.47–5.48	 sā iyam pravṛttiḥ yatas sattā mātra avasthitāt na asau vidhiḥ tatra śāstra vaiyarthyāt apratītāt eva kutaścid pravṛtti siddhau tad pratyāyana artham tad abhyarthana abhāvāt na ca pravṛtti hetu janana artham tad upayogaḥ pravṛtti hetoḥ icchāyāḥ jñāna yoni tvāt jñānam anutpādya tad utpādanasya aśakya tvāt tasya ca nirālambanasya anutpatteḥ apravartaka tvāt ca niyāmaka abhāvāt tasmāt yasya jñānam prayatna jananīm icchām prasūte sortha viśeṣaḥ tad jñāpakaḥ vār atha viśeṣaḥ vidhiḥ preraṇā pravartanā niyuktiḥ niyogaḥ upadeśaḥ iti anarthāntaram iti sthite vicāryate sa hi kartṛ dharmaḥ vā syāt karma dharmaḥ vā karaṇa dharmaḥ vā niyoktṛ dharmaḥ vā iti na prathamaḥ iṣṭa hāneḥ aniṣṭa āpteḥ apravṛtteḥ virodhataḥ asattvāt pratyaya tyāgāt kartṛ dharmaḥ na saṅkarāt sa hi na spandaḥ eva ātmānam anupaśyet iti ādi avyāpteḥ grāmam gacchati iti ādau= ati vyāpteḥ ca na api tad kāraṇam prayatnaḥ tasya sarva ākhyāta sādhāraṇa tvāt 
NKA_5.49	 nanu na sarvatra prayatnaḥ eva pratyaya arthaḥ karoti ityādau prakṛti artha atirekiṇaḥ tasya abhāvāt saṅkhyā mātra abhidhānena pratyayasya caritārtha tvāt tatas liṅga ādi vāt ca eva prayatnaḥ iti na kuryāt iti atra api tulya tvāt prayatna mātrasya prakṛti artha tve api tasya para aṅgatā āpannasya pratyaya artha tvāt na tulya tvam iti ced na tathā api tulya tvāt na ca ekasya tad vācaka tve anyasya tad viparyayaḥ āpadyeta ekaḥ dvau bahavaḥ eṣiṣati ityādau vyabhicārāt tatra dvitīya sṅkhya icchā ādi kalpane karoti prayatate iti ādau= api tathā syāt pratyekam anyatra sāmarthya avadhṛtau sambhede tathā kalpanāyāḥ tulya tvāt rathaḥ gacchati ityādau tad asambhave kā gatiḥ iti ced tantavaḥ paṭam kurvanti iti atra yā loka upacāraḥ ayam aparyanuyojyaḥ iti ced tulyam liṅaḥ kāryatve vṛddha vyavahārāt vyutpattau sarvam samañjasam ākhyāta mātrasya tu na tathā iti ced na vivaraṇa ādeḥ api vyutpatteḥ asti ca tat iha kim karoti pacati pākam karoti iti arthaḥ ityādi darśanāt 
NKA_5.50	 tathā api phala anukūla tā āpanna dhātu artha mātra abhidhāne tad atirikta prayatna abhidhāna kalpanāyām kalpanā gauravam syāt atas vivaraṇam api tāvat mātra param iti ced bhavet api evam yadi pākena iti vivṛṇuyāt na tu etat asti dhātu arthasya eva pākam iti sādhya tvena nirdeśāt tatas tam pratyeva kiñcid anukūla tā āpannam pratyayena abhidhānīyam iti yuktam 
NKA_5.51	 tathā api tena prayatnena eva bhavitavyam na tu anyena iti kutas iti ced niyamena tathā vivaraṇāt bādhakam vinā tasya anyathā kartum aśakyatvāt anyathā ati prasaṅgāt syāt etat yasya kasyacid phalam pratyanukūla tā āpatti mātram eva karoti arthaḥ na tu prayatnaḥ eva saḥ api hi anena eva upādhinā pratyayena vaktavyaḥ na tu yatna tva mātreṇa prayatna padena aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt tad varam tāvat mātram eva astu lāghavāya anyathā tu anukūla tva prayatna tve dvau= upādhī kalpanīyau acetaneṣu sarvatra gauṇa arthāḥ tiṅaḥ asati bādhake kalpanīyāḥ iti ced atra ucyate 
NKA_5.52^1	 kṛta akṛta vibhāgena kartṛ rūpa vyavasthayā yatnaḥ eva kṛtiḥ pūrvā parasmin sā eva bhavanā yatna pūrvaka tvam hi pratisandhāya ghaṭa ādau kṛtaḥ iti vyavahārāt hetu sattva pratisandhāne api yatna pūrvakatva pratisandhāna vidhurāṇām aṅkura ādau tat avyavahārāt karoti arthaḥ yatnaḥ eva tāvat avasīyate anyathā hi yat kiñcit anukūla pūrvakatva aviśeṣāt ghaṭa ādayaḥ kṛtāḥ na kṛtāḥ tu aṅkura ādayaḥ iti kutas vyavahāra niyamaḥ tena ca sarvam ākhyāta padam vivriyate iti sarvatra saḥ eva arthaḥ iti nirṇayaḥ tathā ca samudite pravṛttam padam tat eka deśe api prayujyate viśuddhi mātram puraskṛtya brāhmaṇe śrotriya pada vat 
NKA_5.52^2	 anyathā api madhyama uttama puruṣa gāminaḥ pratyayāḥ prathame puruṣe jānāti icchati prayatate adhyavasyati śete saṃśete ityādayaḥ ca gauṇa arthāḥ eva acetaneṣu na ca vṛtti antareṇa api prayoga sambhave śakti kalpanā yuktāḥ anyāyaḥ ca aneka artha tvam iti sthiteḥ atas eva anubhavaḥ api yāvat uktam bhavati pāka anukūla vartamāna prayatnavān tāvat uktam bhavati pacati iti evam tathābhūta ativṛtta prayatnaḥ apākṣīt iti evam tathā bhūta bhāvi prayatnaḥ pakṣyati iti na tu pacati iti pāka ānukūlayat kiñcidvān iti anyathā atithau= api para śrama śayāne pacati iti pratyaya prasaṅgāt 
NKA_5.53	 api ca kartṛ vyāpāraḥ eva kṛñarthaḥ cetanaḥ ca kartā anyathā tad vyavasthā anupapatteḥ na hi abhidhīyamāna vyāpāravat tvam kartṛ tvam anabhidhāna daśāyām kurvataḥ api akartṛ tva prasaṅgāt na api ākhyāta pratyaya abhidhāna yogya vyāpāra śāli tvam kartṛ tvam yogyatāyāḥ eva anirūpaṇāt phala anuguṇa mātrasya sarva kāra kavya apāra sādhāraṇa tvāt na api vivakṣātaḥ niyamaḥ avivakṣā daśa āyāma niyama prasaṅgāt sva vyāpāre na idam aniṣṭam iti ced evam tarhi sva vyāpāre ca kartṛ tvam sarvatra eva asti kārake iti nyāyena karaṇa ādi vilopa prasaṅgaḥ na sva vyāpāra apekṣayā karaṇa ādi vyavahāraḥ kintu pradhāna kriyā apekṣayā asti hi kāñcid kriyām uddiśya pravartamānānām kārakāṇām avāntara vyāpāra yogaḥ na tu avāntara vyāpāra artham eva teṣām pravṛttiḥ iti ced tarhi tad apekṣayā eva kartṛ karma ādi vyavahāra viśeṣa niyame kim kāraṇam iti cintyatām svātantryāt iti ced nanu tat eva kim anyat prayatna ādi samavāyāt iti vivicya abhidhīyatām iti tasmāt sarvatra samāna vyāpāraḥ eva ākhyāta arthaḥ 
NKA_5.54^1	 tathā api phala anuguṇa tā eva astu pratyayasya pravṛtti nimittam prayatnaḥ tu ākṣepataḥ lapsyate iti ced na bhāvanā eva hi yatna ātmā sarvatra ākhyāta gocaraḥ tayā vivaraṇa dhrauvyāt ākṣepa anupapattitaḥ kena hi tadā ākṣipyeta natāvat anukūla tva mātreṇa tasya prayatna tvena avyāpanāt na hi yatna tva eka artha sama vāyi eva anukūla tvam atas eva na saṅkhyayā tasyāḥ saṅkhyeya mātra paryavasāyi tvāt kartrā iti ced na dravya mātrasya akartṛ tvāt vyāpāravataḥ ca abhidhāne vyāpāra abhidhānasya avaśya abhyupagamanīya tvāt na api dhātu arthena tat ākṣepaḥ vidyate ityādau tad asambhavāt na hi atri dhātu arthaḥ bhāvanā apekṣī sat tayā nitya tvāt tatra na bhaviṣyati iti ced na pūrva aparībhūta bhāvanā anubhavasya aviśeṣāt 
NKA_5.54^2	 bhāvanā uparāgeṇa hi atathābhūtaḥ api arthaḥ tathā bhāsate iti na ca pada antara labdhayā bhāvanayā anukūla tāyāḥ pratyaya arthasya anvayaḥ tad asambhavāt na khalu prakṛtyā eva sā abhidhīyate dhātūnām kriyā phala mātra abhidhāyi tvāt anyathā pākaḥ iti ādau= api bhāvanā anubhava prasaṅgāt na api caitraḥ ityādinā pada antareṇa prakṛti pratyayayoḥ ubhayoḥ api akāraka artha tvāt odanam ityādeḥ kāraka pada tvāt tasya ca kriyā upahita tvāt tena abhidhānam ākṣepaḥ vā katham anyathā odanam iti ukte kim bhuṅkte pacati vā iti viśeṣa ākāṅkṣā iti ced na pacati iti ukte kim odanam temanam vā iti viśeṣa ākāṅkṣā darśanāt sā ca ākṣepa abhidhānayoḥ anyataram antareṇa na syāt tasyām daśāyām na ced ākṣepaḥ nūnam abhidhānam eva iti 
NKA_5.55	 syāt etat abhidhīyatām tarhi kartā api tad anabhidhāne hi saṅkhyeya mātram ākṣipya saṅkhyā katham kartāram anviyāt na tu karma ādikam api śāka sūpau pacati śāka sūpa odanān pacati ityādau virodha nirastā saṅkhyā caitraḥ iti kartāram aviruddham anugacchati iti ced caitraḥ odanam pacati iti atrakā gatiḥ ekatra nirṇītaḥ śāstra arthaḥ aparatra api tathā yava varāha ādi vat iti ced na pacyate iti ādau= api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt caitrābhyām caitraiḥ iti virodha nirastā sūpaḥ iti aviruddham karma samanukrāmati iti ced caitra maitrābhyām pāka sūpau pacyete iti atra kā gatiḥ anyatra nirṇītena arthena vyavahāraḥ iti ced na pacati ityādau= api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt tatra pūrvakaḥ eva nirṇayaḥ pacyate iti atra tva paraḥ iti ced na viśeṣa abhāvāt ātmanepada parasmaipadābhyām viśeṣaḥ iti ced na pacyate pacate pakṣyate ityādau viplava prasaṅgāt iti 
NKA_5.56	 dṛśyate ca samāna pratyaya abhihitena anvayaḥ saṅkhyāyāḥ tat yathā bhūyate supyate ityādau na hi tatra kartrā karmaṇā vā anyena eva vā kenacid anvayaḥ kintu bhāvena eva ananvaye tad abhidhāyinaḥ anarthaka tva prasaṅgāt ākṣiptena ca anvaye tatra api kartṛ eva anvaya āpatteḥ kaḥ hisupyate svapiti iti anayoḥ kartṛ ākṣepam prati viśeṣaḥ syāt etat bhāva karmaṇoḥ iti ādi anuśāsana balāt tāvat bhāva karmaṇī pratyaya vācye tatas tad abhihitā saṅkhyā tābhyām anvīyate yaḥ tu pratyayaḥ na tatra utpannaḥ tad abhihitā saṅkhyā mukhyam vā pūrva codanān loka vat iti nyāyena kartāram eva āśrayate iti niyamaḥ na viparyyaya prasaṅgāt śeṣāt kartari para smaipadam kartari śap iti anuśāsana balāt bhāva kartārau pratyaya vācyau tatas tad abhihitā saṅkhyā api tābhyām anvīyate yaḥ tu pratyayaḥ na tatra utpannaḥ tad abhihitā saṅkhyā tena eva nyāyena karma eva samāśrayet iti niyama upapatteḥ tasmāt mati kardamam apahāya yathā anuśāsanam eva gṛhyate iti prāptam evam prāpte abhidhīyate 
NKA_5.57^1	 ākṣepa labhye saṅkhyeye na abhidhānasya kalpanā saṅkhyeya mātra lābhe api sākāṅkṣeṇa vyavasthitiḥ saṅkhyā api tāvat iyam bhāvanā anugāminī yam yam bhāvanā anveti tam tam saṅkhyā api iti sthiteḥ eka pratyaya vācya tva niyamāt bhāvanāca śuddham prātipadikā artha mātram ākāṅkṣati na hi vyāpāravantam vyāpāraḥ āśrayate ātma āśrayāt samavāyam prati tad anupayogāt vijātīya vyāpāravataḥ akartṛ tvāt ca na ca dvitīya ādyāḥ prātipadika vibhaktayaḥ tatas prathama anirdiṣṭena eva bhāvanā anvīyate iti tasya anvaya yogya tā niyamāt saṅkhyā api tad anugāminī tena eva anvīyate iti na ati prasaṅgaḥ nañartha vat yathā hi caitraḥ na brāhmaṇaḥ na gauraḥ na spandate na kuṇḍalī ityādau viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya samabhivyāhāra viśeṣe api nañā tad anabhidhāna aviśeṣe api nañarthasya viśeṣaṇa aṃśaiḥ eva anvayaḥ na viśeṣya aṃśena nanu bādhāt tatra tathā na hi viśeṣyeṇa tad anvaye viśeṣaṇa upādānam arthavat bhavet tad niṣedhena eva viśeṣaṇa niṣedha upalabdheḥ 
NKA_5.57^2	 ubha niṣedhe ca āvṛttau vākya bhedāt anāvṛttau nirākāṅkṣa tvāt iti ced tulya tvāt samāna pratyaya upātta bhāvanā ākṣipta anvaya upapattau bādhakam vinā sannihita tyāgena vyavahita parigrahasya guru tvāt bhāvanāyāḥ ca sāmānyākṣepe api sā kāṅkṣa parityāge nirākāṅkṣa anvaya anupapatteḥ na hi anyatara ākāṅkṣāḥ anvaya hetuḥ apitu ubhayā kāṅkṣā prātipadikā arthaḥ hi phalena anvayam alabhamānaḥ kriyā sambandham apekṣate bhāvanā api vyāpāra bhūtā satī vyāpāriṇam iti ubhaya ākāṅkṣāḥ anvaya hetuḥ kaṭam kaṭena ityādi tu kāraka tayā eva phala samanvitam na vyāpāra antaram apekṣate iti nirākāṅkṣam iti atas eva asyate supyate ityādau na ākṣiptena anvayaḥ na hi caitreṇa iti tṛtīyānta śabdasya bhāvanāyām ākāṅkṣā asti bhāvya ākāṅkṣā asti iti ced na phalena śayana ādi dhātu arthena anvayāt phala sambandhinaḥ ca atra kartṛ anatiḥ ekāt na hi śayana ādayaḥ dhātu arthāḥ kartṛ atiḥ eki sambaddhāḥ na ca phala tad sambandhi vyatirekeṇa anyaḥ bhāvyaḥ nāma yam apekṣeta 
NKA_5.58^1	 syāt etat kim iti na prayujyate kaṭaḥ karoti caitram ityādi abhihita anabhihita vyavasthā abhāvāt iti ced na cetram iti prathama antasya asādhu tvāt dvitīya antasya tu karma vacana tvena tad sambandhāt bhāvya anapekṣiṇī bhāvanā bhāvaka mātram apekṣeta na ca kaṭasya caitram pratibhāvaka tvam viryayāt anāptena tu vivakṣāyām prayujyate eva prayujyatām tarhi kaṭaḥ karoti caitraḥ ityādi na nitya sandigdha tvena vākya artha asamarpaka tvāt tatas tad upapattaye viśeṣasya vyañjanīya tvāt 
NKA_5.58^2–5.59	 vyajyatām tarhi tṛtīyayā caitreṇa iti evam devadattaḥ kriyate kaṭam iti vyajyatām dvitīyayā iti ced na aprayogāt na hi anāptena api evam prāyāṇi prayujyante lakṣaṇa avirodhena kutas etat eva iti ced lokasya aparyanuyojya tvāt na hi gārgikayā iti padam sādhu iti ślāghā abhidhāyi pada sannidhim anapekṣya prayujyate tasya tad upādhinā eva vihita tvāt iti ced etat eva kutas loke tathā eva prayoga darśanāt iti ced tulyam karoti ityādi karma vibhakti samabhivyāhāreṇa eva prayujyate kriyate iti kartṛ vibhakti sama bhavya āhāreṇa eva iti kim atra kriyatām imam eva viśeṣa murarīkṛtya anabhihita adhikāra anuśāsanena hi etāvān parāmarśaḥ sarveṣām hṛdi padam ādadhāti iti abhidhāna anabhidhāna vibhāgaḥ eva vyutpādana daśāyām peśalaḥ iti 
NKA_5.60	 syāt etat bhavatu sarva ākhyāta sādhāraṇī bhāvanā kāla viśeṣa sambandhinī sā laḍa ādi arthaḥ kāla traya aparāmṛṣṭā liṅā arthaḥ iti ced na yatna padena samāna artha tva prasaṅgāt viṣaya uparāgān uparāgābhyām viśeṣaḥ iti ced na yāga yatnaḥ iti anena paryāyata āpatteḥ kartṛ saṅkhyā abhidhānān abhidhānābhyām viśeṣaḥ iti ced na yāga yatnavān iti anena sāmya āpatteḥ iṣṭaḥ eva ayam arthaḥ iti ced na itas vatsara śatena api apravṛtteḥ phala sama bhivyāhāra abhāvāt na pravarttate iti ced na svarga kāmaḥ yāga yatnavān iti atas api apravṛtteḥ tat kasya hetoḥ na hi yatnaḥ yatnasya hetuḥ yatna pratītiḥ vā yatnasya kāraṇam api tu icchā 
NKA_5.61	 na ca sā api pratītā yatna jananī yena sā eva vidhi arthaḥ iti anugamyatām api tu sat tayā na ca liṅaḥ śruti kāle sā satī na ca liṅā iva tām janayati artha viśeṣam apratyāyayantyāḥ tasyāḥ tad janaka tve vyutpatti grahaṇa vaiyarthyāt anupalabdha liṅāñca icchā anutpatti prasaṅgāt iti etena vṛddha vyavahārāt vyutpattiḥ bhavantī bālasya ātmani pravṛtti hetuḥ yaḥ avagataḥ tam eva āśrayet svayañca kuryām iti saṅkalpāt eva ayam pravṛttaḥ tatas saḥ eva liṅā arthaḥ iti nirastam kuryām iti prayatnaḥ vā syāt icchā vā na ādyaḥ sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt na dvitīyaḥ sā hi sat tayā eva prayatna utpādinī na ca liṅaḥ śruti kāle sā sati iti uktam phala icchā tu nisarga vāhi tayā sati api na prayatnam prati hetuḥ anya viṣaya tvāt tad arthañca śāstra vaiyarthyāt tasyāḥ kāraṇa antarataḥ eva siddheḥ tat prati iti artham api śāstra anapekṣaṇāt tasyāḥ manaḥ vedya tvāt aprāpte ca śāstram arthavat prāpte ca śāstra anavakāśāt tad abhidhāne ca svarga kāmaḥ iti kartṛ viśeṣaṇa paunaruktyāt tadā hi yajeta iti asya eva yāga kartā svarga kāmaḥ iti arthaḥ syāt 
NKA_5.62^1	 yadica phala viṣayā eva sādhana viṣayam prayatnam janayet anyatra api prasuvīta niyāmaka abhāvāt hetu phala bhāvaḥ eva niyāmakaḥ iti ced na ajñātasya tasya niyāmaka tve liṅam vinā api svarga icchātaḥ yāge pravṛtti prasaṅgāt jñātasya tu tad sādhana tvasya niyāmaka tve tad icchā eva tatra pravartayatuḥ yaḥ yat kāmayate sa tad sādhanam api kāmayataḥ eva iti niyamāt na ca sā tadānīm satī na ca tat jñānam eva prayatna janakam tat ca liṅā kriyate iti yuktam svarga kāmaḥ yāga cikīrṣāva an iti atas api pravṛtti prasaṅgāt liṅaḥ vā icchām pratītya anicchan= api sarvaḥ pravarteta sva sambandhi tayā tad avagamaḥ tathā na tu sāmānyatas iti ced na prathama puruṣeṇa tad anabhidhāne tasya avidhi artha tva prasaṅgāt 
NKA_5.62^2	 odana kāmaḥ tvam pāka cikīrṣā avāniti atas api pravṛtti āpatteḥ ca apica saṅkalpa jñānāt yadi prayatnaḥ jāyeta tathā api saṅkalpasya kutas janma kimarthañca saṅkalpa jñānāt eva prayatna arthañcā iti ced nanu icchā viśeṣaḥ saṅkalpaḥ sa tāvat sukhe svabhāvataḥ tad sādhane ca aupa adhikaḥ saṅkalpa viṣayaḥ tu katham tad sādhana tvāt eva iti ced tarhi tad sādhana tva ajñānāt na tu saṅkalpa svarūpa jñānāt bhavitum arhati iti anyathā iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam api anarthakam āpadyeta tasmāt saṅkalpaḥ pravartakaḥ iti abhyupeyate kintu sattā mātreṇa na tu jñātaḥ iti na asau vidhiḥ jñānañca viṣaya upahāreṇa eva vyavahārayati iti tad viṣayaḥ eva avaśiṣyate iti kartṛ dharma vyudāsaḥ 
NKA_5.63	 astu tarhi karma dharmaḥ na iti ucyate atiprasaṅgāt na phalam na apūrvam tatvahānitaḥ tad alābhāt na kāryañca na kriyā api apravṛttitaḥ karma hi phalam vā syāt tad kāraṇam apūrvam vā tad kāraṇam kriyā vā na prathamaḥ phala icchāyāḥ pravṛttim pratyahetutvāt atiprasaṅgāt iti ukta tvāt na dvitīyaḥ avyutpatteḥ liṅaḥ hi pravṛtti nimittam apūrva tvam vā syāt kāryatvam vā syāt ubhayam vā na prathamaḥ śabda pravṛtti nimittasya apūrva tvasya pramāṇa antarāt avagatau= apūrva tva vyāghātāt anavagatau= avyutpatteḥ sambandhanaḥ anavagame sambandhasya pratyetum aśakyatvāt tatas eva avagatau= itaretara āśraya doṣāt na ca gandhava tvena upanītāyām pṛthivyām pṛthivī śabda vat adūra viprakarṣeṇa kāryatvena upanītena apūrva tvena nimittena apūrve pravartate liṅiti yuktam tatra ubhayoḥ api pratīyamāna tvena sandehe kalpanā gaurava puraskāreṇa pṛthivī tvaḥ eva saṅgati viśrānteḥ upapatteḥ na tu atra apūrva tva pratītiḥ 
NKA_5.64	 syāt etat kāryatvam upalakṣaṇīkṛtya tāvat eṣā liṅ pravṛttā tad upalakṣitaḥ ca yāgaḥ vā yatnaḥ vā anyaḥ vā śabda itara pramāṇa gocaraḥ na adhikāri viśeṣaṇa svarga sādhana samarthaḥ na ca akāmya phale kāmī niyoktum śakyate tatas anyat evālaukikam kiñcid anena upalakṣyate yaḥ liṅā ādi pravṛtti gocaraḥ iti kim anupapannim iti ced na upalakṣaṇam hi smaraṇam anumānam vā ubhayam api anavagata sambandhena aśakyam na hi saṃskāra vat manaḥ vat a dṛṣṭa vat vā kāryatvam apūrva tvam upalakṣayati jñāna apekṣaṇāt tatas hastī iva hastipakam dhūmaḥ iva dhūma dhvajam tad sambandha jñānāt upalakṣayet na tu anyathā tathā ca nyāya sampādana api araṇyeḥ uditam na hi yukti sahasraiḥ api avidite saṅgatigrahaḥ avidita saṅgatiḥ vā śabdaḥ pravartate iti etena bheda agrahāt kriyā kārye vyutpattiḥ iti nirastam na hi ajñāte bheda agrahaḥ vyavahāra aṅgam atiprasaṅgāt kiñca apūrva tve pravṛtti nimitte kalpyamāne laukikī liṅanarthikā prasajyeta tatra upalakṣaṇīya abhāvāt tatra kāryatvam eva pravṛtti nimittam iti yadi prakṛte api tathā eva astu kpta tvāta sambhavāt ca iti 
NKA_5.65^1	 astu tarhi tat eva pravṛtti nimittam tarka sampādanayātu a pūrva vyakti lābhaḥ iti ced na nitya niṣedha āpūrvayoḥ alābha prasaṅgāt naca asmin pakṣe ekatra nirṇītena śāstra arthena anyatra tathā eva vyavahāraḥ iti sambhavati kāryatvasya eva pravṛtti nimitta tvena nirṇīta tvāt na tu apūrva tvasya nyāya sampādanāyāḥ ca tatra asambhavāt phala anuguṇyena hi vyakti viśeṣaḥ labhyate na ca tat tatra śrūyate na ca aśrutam api kalpayitum śakyate bīja abhāvāt tat hi vidhi anyathā anupapatyā kalpyeta kāryya tva pratyayāni atha anupapatyā vā loka vat na prathamaḥ bhavatām darśane tasya upeya rūpa tvāt yatas śruta svarga phala tve api sādhya vivṛddhiḥ ucyate na dvitīyaḥ śabda balena tad pratyaye tad anapekṣaṇāt loke hi tad pratyayaḥ iṣṭa abhyupāyata adhīnaḥ na tu vede iti abhyupagamāt 
NKA_5.65^2	 anyathā iṣṭa abhyupāya ta eva prathamam vedāt avagantavyā pramāṇa antara abhāvāt tatas kāryyata iti ānumānikaḥ vidhiḥ syāt na śābdaḥ ānumānikam phalam astu yat kartavyam tat iṣṭa abhyupāyaḥ iti vyāpteḥ iti api na yuktam sukhena vyabhicārāt anya tve sati iti ced na duḥkha abhāvena vyabhicārāt phalam vihāya iti ced tat eva kim uktam syāt iṣṭam svabhāvataḥ iti ced tarhi tatas anyat aniṣṭam syāt tat ca kartavyam iti vyāghātaḥ tad sādhanam iti ced tad sādhana tve sati iti sādhya aviśiṣṭam viśeṣaṇam svabhāvataḥ na idam iṣṭam kartavyañca tatas nūnam iṣṭa sādhanam iti sādhana arthaḥ iti ced na svabhāvataḥ na idam iṣṭam iti asiddheḥ ananya uddeśa pravṛtta kṛti vyāpta tvāt anyathā tad asiddheḥ tatas vyāghātāt anyatara apāyaḥ iti 
NKA_5.66	 astu nitya niṣedha apūrvayoḥ alābhaḥ kim naḥ chinnam iti ced kim naḥ chinnam yadā kāma adhikāre api tad alābhaḥ nahi liṅā kāryam svarga sādhanam uktam na api svarga kāma pada samabhivyāhārāni atha anupapatyā tat labdham brāhmaṇa tva āt ivat adhi kārya vat cheda mātreṇa eva upapatteḥ naca idam anumānam yasya yat icchātaḥ yat kartavyam tat tasya iṣṭa sādhanam iti anya icchayā svābhāvika kartavya tva asiddheḥ tat icchayā eva tad kartavya tāyāḥ sukhena anaikāntika tvāt aupādhika kartavyatāyāḥ ca iṣṭa sādhana tvam apratītya pratyetum aśakya tvāt kim anayā viśeṣa cintayā pratīyate tāvat śabdāt anyat icchataḥ anyat kāryam iti etāvatā eva anumānam iti ced nanu anvitam abhidhānīyam yogyañcā anvīyate anyat icchataḥ ca anyat kartavyam anvaya ayogyam tat katham abhidhīyatām tatas eva tad sādhana tva siddhiḥ iti ced evam tarhi iṣṭa sā adhana tā eka artha samavāyi kartavya tva abhidhānāt anumāna anavakāśaḥ naca anvitā abhidhāne āpi tad sādhana tva siddhiḥ adhikārya vaccheda mātreṇa api anvaya yogyata upapatteḥ 
NKA_5.67^1	 na ca kārya tvam apūrve sambhavati tat hi kṛti vyāpya tā ced vrīhi ādiṣu eva siddha tvāt kṛti phala tvam ced yāgasya eva tatas tasya eva ahatya utpatteḥ kṛtī uddeśya tā ced svargasya eva nisarga sundara tvāt na tu apūrvasya tad viparīta tvāt stana pāna ādi vat aupādhikī iti ced sā api yāgasya eva svargasya sādhya tva sthitau yāgasya eva sādhana tvena anvayāt kāla vyavadhānāt na etat nirvahati iti ced yathā nirvahati śruta anurodhena tathā kalpyatām vyāpāra dvārā kathañcid syāt na tu bhinna kālayoḥ vyāpāra vyāpāribhāvaḥ kāraṇa tvañca vyāpāreṇa yujyate avyavadhānena pūrva kāla niyamḥ ca tattvam anyathā ati prasaṅgāt iti ced na pūrva bhāva niyama mātrasya kāraṇa tvāt kārya anuguṇa avāntara kāryasya eva vyāpāra tvāt 
NKA_5.67^2	 kṛṣi cikitsā ādau bahulam tathā vyavahārāt lākṣaṇikaḥ asau= iti ced na mukhya artha tve virodha abhāvāt astu tarhi putreṇa hate brahmaṇi ciradhvastasya pituḥ tam avāntara vyāpārīkṛtya kartṛ tvam tathā ca lokayātrā viplavaḥ iti ced na sati api sute kadācid tad akaraṇāt tasmin= asati api kadācid kāraṇāt anirvāhaka tayā tasya vyāpāra tva ayogāt yam janayitvā eva hi yam prati yasya pūrva bhāva nirvāhaḥ saḥ eva tam prati tasya vyāpāraḥ na aparaḥ yathā anubhavasya smaraṇam prati saṃskāraḥ tasya hi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāne siddhe tad anyathā anupapatyā saṃskāraḥ kalpyate na tu anyathā tathā iha api na ced evam tava api brahma bhidura śara vimoka sama samaya hatasya hantṛ tvam na syāt syāt ca sva niveśana śayānasya tad pituḥ iti etena ubhayam na iti nirastam 
NKA_5.68	 astu tarhi kriyā dharmaḥ eva kāryatvam vidhiḥ sarvaḥ hi kartavyam etat iti pratyeti tatas kuryām iti saṅkalpya pravartate iti ced na kartavyam mayā iti kṛtī a dhyavasāya arthaḥ vā syāt kartavyam mayā iti ucita arthaḥ vā syāta tatra prathamaḥ saṅkalpāt na bhidyate vyavahita kārya saṅkalpaḥ hi kartavyaḥ mayā iti sannihita kārya saṅkalpaḥ tu kuryām iti sa ca na liṅā arthaḥ sattā mātreṇa pravartanāt iti uktam tat etat kartavyatāyām jātāyām pravartate iti vastu sthitau bhrāntaiḥ jñātāyām iti gṛhītam aucityantu kriyā dharmaḥ prāgabhāvavat tvam tasmin sati śakya tvam vā tasmin sati kartāram pratyupakāraka tvam vā prathame kutaścid api na nivarteta dvitīye duḥkhe api tathāvidhe pravarteta tṛtīye tu vakṣyate 
NKA_5.69	 astu tarhi karaṇa dharmaḥ na karaṇam hi śabdaḥ tad dharmaḥ abhidhā vā syāt tad arthaḥ bhāvanā ādiḥ vā tad dharmaḥ iṣṭa sādhana tā vā na prathamaḥ asattvāt apravṛtteḥ ca na abhidhā api garīyasī bādhakasya samāna tvāt pariśeṣaḥ api durlabhaḥ saṅgati pratisandhāna adhikāyām tasyām pramāṇa abhāvāt anya samavetasya apūrvavat anya vyāpāra tvena api upapatteḥ viṣaya tayā api ca sva vyāpāram pratiliṅga vat hetu bhāva avirodhāta adhikattve api tatas apravṛtteḥ bālānām tad abhāve api tad bhāvāt śabda antareṇa tad śrāviṇām api apravṛtteḥ na ca vilakṣaṇā eva sā liṅaḥ viṣayaḥ tat vailakṣyaṇyam pratītim prati ced artha viśeṣaḥ api syāt pravṛtti mātram prati ced abhidhā samavetam tat iti kutas tad sannidhānāt iti ced naḥ aniyamāt anyasya sarvasya niṣedhāt iti ced na pravṛtti hetuttva niṣedhasya tulya tvāt tad sannidhi niṣeṣasya ca aśakya tvāt śabda eka vedya tve ca avyutpatteḥ pravṛtti anyathā anupapatti siddhe vyutpattiḥ iti api vārtam na hi pravṛtti hetuḥ kaścid asti iti pravartate 
NKA_5.70	 iṣṭa sādhana tā tu syāt sarvaḥ hi mayā kriyamāṇam etat mama samīhitam sādhayiṣyati iti pratisandhatte tatas icchati kuryām iti tatas karoti iti sarva anubhava siddham tat ayam vyutpitsuḥ yat jñānāt prayatna jananīm icchām avāptavān tat jñānam eva liṅśrāviṇaḥ pravṛtti kāraṇam anuminoti tatas ca kartavyatā eka artha samavāyinī iṣṭa sādhana tā āliṅā arthaḥ iti avadhārayati na ca vācyam evañcet varam kartavyatā eva astu avaśya abhyupagamanīya tvāt kṛtam iṣṭa sādhana tayā iti yathā hi na iṣṭa sādhana tā mātram pratītya pravartate asādhyeṣu vyabhicārāt tathā prayatna viṣaya sama vāyinīm iṣṭa sādhana tām adhigamya adhikārī pravartate iti anubhavaḥ tatra viṣayaḥ dhātunā bhāvanā akhyāta mātreṇa śeṣantu tad viśeṣeṇa liṅā iti evam iṣṭa abhyupāyatāyām adhigatāyām anvaya balāt tad viṣayasya iṣṭa sādhana tva avagatiḥ iti kartavyatā eka artha samavāyini iṣṭa abhyupāya tāta liṅāḥ pravṛtti nimittam iti uktam 
NKA_5.71–5.72	 karaṇasya iṣṭa sā adhana tā abhidhāne jyotiṣṭomena iti tṛtīyayā na bhavitavyam iti tu deśyam avaiyākaraṇasya avadhīraṇīyam eva tad saṅkhyā abhidhānam hi tad abhidhānam ākhyātena na ca tat prakṛte na ca yāga iṣṭa sādhana tā abhidhānam liṅā kintu anvaya balāt talābhaḥ iti uktam yat tu siddha apadeśāt api pratīyate iṣṭa sādhana tā na ca atas saṅkalpa ātmā pravṛttiḥ asti iti deśyam tatra samutkaṭa phala abhilāṣasya samarthasya tad sādhana tāvahame api na pravṛttiḥ iti kaḥ pratīyāt sarva pakṣa samānañca etat samāna parīhārañca iti kim tena 
NKA_5.73	 atra abhidhīyate astu prayatna viṣaya samavāyini iṣṭa sādhana tā pravṛtti hetuḥ tathā api na asau liṅa arthaḥ sandehāt sā hi kim sākṣāt eva liṅā avagamyate stana pāna ādau= anumānāt iva bālena kim vā tad pratipāditāt kutaścid arthāt anumīyate ceṣṭā viśeṣa anumita āt iva abhipraya viśeṣāt samayā abhijñena iti sandihyate evañca sati sā na abhidhīyate iti eva nirṇayaḥ hetu tvāt anumānāt ca madhyamādau viyogataḥ anyatra kpta sāmarthyāt niṣedha anupapattitaḥ 
NKA_5.74	 tathā hi agni kāmaḥ dāruṇī mathnīyāt iti śrutvā kutas iti ukte vaktāraḥ vadanti yatas tad manthanāt agniḥ arasya sidhyati iti tarati brahmahatyām yaḥ aśvamedhena yajate iti ādā= iṣṭa abhyupāya tāyām eva avagatāyām anumimate tāntrikāḥ yat aśvamedhena yajeta mṛtyu brahmahatyā taraṇa kāmaḥ ityādi vidhim nindayā ca niṣedham tat yathā andham tamaḥ praviśanti ye ke ca ātma hanaḥ janāḥ iti atas na ātmānam hanyāt iti kuryyāḥ kuryyām iti atra vidhi vihitā eva lij na iṣṭa abhyupāyatām āha kintu vaktṛ saṅkalpam na hi iṣṭa abhyupāyaḥ mama ayam iti kuryām iti padārthaḥ kintu tat pratipatteḥ anantaram yaḥ asya saṅkalpaḥ kuryām iti saḥ eva sarvatra ca anyatra vaktuḥ eva icchā abhidhīyate liṅā iti avadhṛtam tathā hi ājñā adhyeṣaṇa anujñā sampraśna prārthanā āśaṃsāḥ liṅinā an yat cakāsti yām vaktuḥ icchām ananu vidadhānaḥ tad kṣobhāt bibheti sā ājñā yā tu śrotuḥ pūjā saṃmāna vyañjikā sā adhyeṣaṇāḥ vāraṇa abhāva vyañjikā anujñā abhidhāna prayojanā sampraśnaḥ lobha icchā prārthanā śubha āśaṃsanam āśīḥ iti 
NKA_5.75	 na ca vidhi vikalpeṣu niṣedhaḥ upapadyate tathā hi yadā abhidhā vidhiḥ tadā na hanyāt hanana bhāvanā na abhidhīyate iti vākya arthaḥ vyāghātāt nirastaḥ yadā kāla traya aparāmṛṣṭā bhāvanā tadā na iti sambandhe atyanta abhāvaḥ mithyā yadā kāryam tadā na hanyāt na hananam kāryam iti anubhava viruddham kriyate eva yatas na hananena kāryam hanana kāraṇakam kāryam na asti iti arthaḥ iti api na asti duḥkha nivṛtti sukha āptyoḥ anyatarasya tatra sadbhāvāt 
NKA_5.76	 hanana kāraṇakam adṛṣṭam na asti iti arthaḥ iti tu nirātaṅkam dṛṣṭa arthinam pravartayet eva iti sādhu śāstra arthaḥ ahananena apūrvam bhāvayet iti tu aśakyam kāraṇasya anādi tvena kāryasya api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt bhāvanāyāḥ ca tad aviṣaya tvāt ahanana saṅkalpena iti yāvat jīvam avicchinni tad saṅkalpaḥ syāt sakṛt kṛtvā evavā nivṛttiḥ paścāt hanyā t eva avirodhāt sampāditaḥ hi anena niyoga arthaḥ yāvat yāvat dhanana saṅkalpavān tāvat tāvat viparīta saṅkalpena apūrvam bhāvayet iti vākya arthaḥ tathābhūtasya adhikāri tvāt iti api vārtam tad aśruteḥ prasaktam hi pratiṣidhyate na aprasaktam iti ced na vai kiñcid iha pratiṣidhyate tad abhāvaḥ pratipādyate iti niṣedha arthaḥ ahanana saṅkalpa karaṇa kamapūrvam vākya arthaḥ kiñca na hanyāt iti ahananena apūrvasya kartavya tā pratyayaḥ jātaḥ vedāt jātaḥ ca hanana kriyāyām rāgāt niṣphalāt ca kāryāt apekṣita phalaṅgarīyaḥ iti nyāyena hanyāt eva iti ahaḥ veda vyākhyā kauśalam āstikya abhimāninaḥ mīmāṃsaka durdurūṭasya 
NKA_5.77	 iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api na hanyāt na hanana bhāvanāḥ iṣṭa abhyupāyaḥ iti vākya arthaḥ tathā ca aniṣṭa sādhantvam kutas labhyate na hi iṣṭa sādhanam yat na bhavati tat avaśyam aniṣṭa sādhanam dṛṣṭam upekṣaṇīyasya api bhāvāt yat rāga ādi prasaktam pratiṣidhyate tat avaśyam aniṣṭa sādhanam dṛṣṭam yathā saviṣam annam na bhuñjīthāḥ iti tena vede api anumāsyate iti api na sādhīyaḥ pratiṣedha arthasya eva cintyamāna tvāt na hi kartavya tvasya iṣṭa sā adhana tvasya bhāvanāyāḥ vā abhāvaḥ pratipādayitum śakyate laukikānām laukika pramāṇa siddha tvāt tathā api pratipādyate tāvat iti ced na pāṣaṇḍa āgama niṣedhena anekāntāt na asau pramāṇam iti ced na artha viparyaya pratipādana aviśeṣe asya api tathā abhāvāt tātparyyataḥ prāmāṇyam iti ced na vidhi niṣedhayoḥ ananya paratvāt na vidhau paraḥ śabda arthaḥ iti vacanāt tathā api niṣedhe tathā bhaviṣyati iti ced na avinā abhāva tad uddeśa pravṛttyoḥ abhāvāt na api asurā vidyā ādi vadasya nañaḥ virodhi vacana tvam kriyā saṅgata tvāt asamasta tvāt ca tasmāt 
NKA_5.78	 vidhiḥ vaktuḥ abhiprāyaḥ pravṛtti ādau liṅa ādibhiḥ abhidheyaḥ anumeyā tu kartariṣṭa abhyupāya tā tatra svayaṅkartṛka kriyā icchā abhidhānam kuryām iti sambodhya kartṛka kriyā icchā abhidhānam kuryāḥ iti śeṣa kartṛka kriyā icchā abhidhānam kurvīta iti tathā ca agni kāmaḥ dāruṇī mathnīyā ādityasya laukika vākyasi ayam arthaḥ sampadyate agni kāmasya dāru mathane pravṛttiḥ mama iṣṭa iti tatas śrotā anum inoti nūnam kāru mathana yatnaḥ agneḥ upāyaḥ iti yat viṣayaḥ hi prayatnaḥ yasya āptena iṣyate sa tasya apekṣita hetu tathā tena avagataḥ ca yathā mama eva putra ādeḥ bhojana viṣayaḥ iti vyāpteḥ viṣam na bhakṣayet iti asya tu viṣa bhakṣaṇa gocarā pravṛttiḥ mama na iṣṭā iti arthaḥ tatas api śrotā anum inoti nūnam viṣa bhakṣaṇa bhāvanā aniṣṭa sādhanam yat viṣayaḥ hi prayatnaḥ kartuḥ abhimata sādhaka upya āptena na iṣyate sa tatas adhikatara anartha hetuḥ tathā tena avagataḥ ca yathā mama eva putra ādeḥ krīḍā kardama viṣa bhakṣaṇa ādi viṣayaḥ iti vyāpteḥ 
NKA_5.79	 laukikaḥ eva vākye ayam prakāraḥ kadācid buddhim adhirohati na tu vedikeṣu teṣu puruṣasya nirasta tvāt iti ced na nirāsa hetoḥ abhāvāt tad astitve api pramāṇam na asti iti ced mā bhūt anyat vidhiḥ eva tāvat garbhaḥ iva puṃyoge pramāṇam śruti kumāryāḥ kim atra kriyatām liṅaḥ vā laukika artha atikrame yaḥ eva laukikāḥ te eva vaidikāḥ te eva ca eṣām arthāḥ iti viplaveta tathā ca jabagaḍa daśa ādi vat anarthaka tva prasaṅgaḥ iti bhava susthaḥ syāt etat tathā api vaktṝṇām upādhyāyānām eva abhiprāyaḥ vede vidhiḥ astu kṛtam svatantreṇa vaktrā parameśvareṇa iti ced na teṣām anuvaktṛtayā abhyāsa abhiprāya mātreṇa pravṛtteḥ śuka ādi vat tathāvidha abhiprāya abhāvāt bhāve vā na rāja śāsana anuvādinaḥ abhiprāyaḥ ājñā kim nāma rājñaḥ eva iti laukikaḥ anubhavaḥ 
NKA_5.80	 śruteḥ khalu api kṛtsnaḥ eva hi vedaḥ ayam parameśvara gocaraḥ sva artha dvārā evatāt paryyam tasya svarga ādi vat vidhau na santi eva hi veda bhāgāḥ yatra parameśvaraḥ na gīyate tathā hi sraṣṭṛ tvena puruṣasūkteṣu vibhūtyā rudreṣu śabdabrahma tvena maṇḍala brāhmaṇeṣu pravañcam puraskṛtya niṣprapañca tayā upaniṣatsu yajñapuruṣa tvena mantra vidhiṣu deha āviḥ bhāvaiḥ upākhyāneṣu upāsya tvena ca sarvatra iti siddhārtha tayā na te pramāṇam iti ced na tad hetu kāraṇa doṣa śaṅkā nirāsasya bhāvya bhūta artha sādhāraṇa tvāt 
NKA_5.81–5.82	 anyatra amīṣām tātparyam iti ced sva artha pratipādana dvārā śabda mātra tayā vā prathame sva arthe api pramāṇyameṣitavyam tasya arthasya ananya pramāṇaka tvāt atas eva tatra tasya smāraka tvam iti api mithyā tad pratipādaka tve api na tatra tātparyam iti ced sva artha aparityāge jyotiḥśāstra vat anyatra api tātparye kaḥ doṣaḥ anyathā svarga naraka vrātya śrotriya ādi svarūpa pratipādakānām aprāmāṇye bahu viplaveta tatra ābādhanāt tathā iti ced tulyam na tādṛśaḥ athaḥ kvacid dṛṣṭaḥ iti ced svarga ādayaḥ api tathā tat mithyātvetad arthi nām apravṛttau vidhāna anarthakya prasaṅgaḥ iti ced iha api tad upāsana avidhāna ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ tat mithyā tve hi sālokya sāyujya ādi phala mithyā tve kaḥ prekṣāvān= tam upāsīta iti tulyam iti vākyāt api saṃsarga bheda pratipādaka tvam hi atra vākya tvam abhipretam tathā ca yat pada kadambakam yat saṃsarga bheda pratipādakam tat tad anapekṣa saṃsarga jñāna pūrvakam yathā laukikam tathā ca vaidikam iti prayogaḥ vipakṣe ca bādhakam uktam 
NKA_5.83	 saṅkhyā viśeṣāt api syām abhūvam bhaviṣyāmi ityādi saṅkhyā ca vaktṛ gā samākhyā api na śākhānām ādya pravacanāt ṛte kārya tayā hi prāk saṅkhyā uktā samprati tu pratipādyatayā ucyate tathā hi uttama puruṣa abhihitā saṅkhyā vaktāram anveti iti su prasiddham asti ca tad prayogaḥ prāyaśas vede tatas tad abhihitayā tayā api saḥ eva anugantavyaḥ anyathā ananvaya prasaṅgāt athavā samākhyā viśeṣaḥ saṅkhyā viśeṣaḥ ucyate kāṭhakam kālāpakam ityādayaḥ hi samākhyā viśeṣāḥ śākhā viśeṣāṇām anusmaryante te ca na pravacana mātra nibandhanāḥ pravaktṝṇām ananta tvāt na api prakṛṣṭa vacana nimittāḥ upādhyāyebhyaḥ api prakarṣe pratyutānyathā karaṇa doṣāt tad pāṭhā anukaraṇe ca prakarṣa abhāvāt kati ca anādau saṃsāre prakṛṣṭāḥ pravaktāraḥ iti kaḥ niyāmakaḥ iti na api ādyasya vaktuḥ samākhyā iti yuktam bhavadbhiḥ tad anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā saḥ eva asmākam vedakāraḥ iti vṛthā vipratipattiḥ 
NKA_5.84	 syāt etat brāhmaṇa tve satyavāntara jāti bhedāḥ eva kaṭha tva ādayaḥ tad adhyeyā tad anuṣṭheya arthā ca śākhā tad samākhyayā vpapadiśyate iti kim anupapannam na kṣatriya ādeḥ api tatra eva adhikārāt na ca yaḥ brāhmaṇasya viśeṣaḥ sa kṣatriya ādau sambhavati na ca kṣatriya ādeḥ anyaḥ vedaḥ iti asti na ca kaṭhāḥ kāṭhakam eva ādhīyate tad artham eva anutiṣṭhanti iti niyamaḥ śākhā sañcārasya api prāyaśas darśanāt prāk evam niyamaḥ āsīt idānīm ayam viplavate iti ced viplavaḥ eva tarhi sarvadā kaṭhādi avāntara jāti viplava āditya gatiḥ eva iyam tasmāt ādya pravaktṛ vacana nimittaḥ eva ayam samākhyā viśeṣa sambandhaḥ iti eva sādhyiti śrīḥ 
NKA_5.85	 saḥ evam bhagavān śrutaḥ anumitaḥ ca kaiścid sākṣāt api dṛścate prameya tva ādeḥ ghaṭa vat nanu tad sāmagrī rahitaḥ katham draṣṭavyaḥ sā hi bahis indriya garbha manaḥ garbhāḥ vā tatra na sambhavati cakṣuḥ ādeḥ niyata viṣaya tvāt manasaḥ bahis asvātantryāt tat uktam hetu abhāve phala abhāvāt ityādi na kāryā eka vyaṅgyāyāḥ sāmagryāḥ niṣeddhum aśakyatvāt 
NKA_5.86	 api ca dṛśyate tāvat bahis indriya uparame api asat nihita deśa kāla artha sākṣātkāraḥ na ca smṛtiḥ eva asau paṭīyasī smarāmi smṛtam vā iti svapna anusandhāna abhāvāt paśyāmi dṛṣṭa miti anuvyavasāyāt naca āropitam tatra anubhava tvam abādhanāt ananubhūtasya api sva śira= chedana ādeḥ avabhāsanāt ca smṛti viparyāsaḥ asau= iti ced yadi smṛti viṣaye viparyāsaḥ iti arthaḥ tadā anumanyāmahe atha smṛtau= eva anubhavatu a viparyāsaḥ iti tadā prāk eva nirastaḥ na ca sambhavati api na hi anyena ākāreṇa adhyavasitaḥ anyena jñāna avacchedaka tayā adhyavasīyate tathā ca sa ghaṭaḥ iti utpannāyām smṛtau bhrāmyataḥ tam ghaṭam anubhavāmi iti syāt na tu imam ghaṭam iti na hi ayam ghaṭaḥ iti smṛteḥ ākāraḥ tasmāt anubhavaḥ eva asau svīkartavyaḥ 
NKA_5.87–5.88	 asti ca svapna anubhavasya api kasyacid satya tvam saṃvādāt tat ca kākatālīyam api na nirnimittam sarva svapna jñānānām api tathā tva prasaṅgāt hetuḥ ca atra dharmaḥ eva sa ca karma ja vat yoga jaḥ api yoga vidheḥ avaseyaḥ karma yoga vidhyoḥ tulya yogakṣema tvāt tasmāt yoginām anubhavaḥ dharmaja tvāt pramā sākṣātkāri tvāt pratyakṣa phalam dharmān anugṛhīta bhāvanā mātra prabhavaḥ tu na pramā iti vibhāgaḥ iti atas tad sāmagrī virahaḥ asiddhaḥ tathā api vipakṣe kim bādhakam iti ced dve brahmaṇī veditavye ityādi yoga vidhi vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ aśakya anuṣṭhāna upāya upadeśaka tvāt na ca asākṣātkāri jñāna vidhānam etat artha jñāna avadhinā adhyayana vidhinā eva tasya gata artha tvāt iti etena paramāṇu ādayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ iti 
NKA_5.89	 tat enam evam bhūtam adhikṛtya śrūyate na draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ vidyate iti ekam eva advitīyam iti paśyati acakṣuḥ sa śṛṇoti akarṇaḥ iti dve brahmaṇī veditavye parañca aparam eva ca iti yajñena yajñam ayajanta devāḥ iti yajñaḥ vai viṣṇuḥ ityādi smaryate ca sarva dharmān parityajya mām ekam śaraṇam vrajaḥ iti mad artham karma kaunteya mukta saṅgaḥ samācaraḥ iti yajña arthāt karmaṇaḥ anyatra lokaḥ ayam karma bandhanaḥ iti yajñāya ācarataḥ karma samagram pravilīyate ityādi anuśiṣyate ca sāṅkhya pravacane īśvara praṇidhānam tam imam jyotiṣṭoma ādibhiḥ iṣṭaiḥ prāsāda ādinā pūrtena śīta ātapa sahana ādinā tapasā ahiṃsā ādibhiḥ yamaiḥ śauca santoṣa ādibhiḥ niyamaiḥ āsana prāṇāyāma ādinā yogena mahā ṛṣayaḥ api vividiṣanti tasmin jñāte sarvam idam jñātam bhavati iti evam vijñāya śrutvā ekatānaḥ tad paraḥ bhavet yat ta idam gīyate mad manāḥ bhava mad bhaktaḥ mad yājī mām namaskuru mām eva eṣyasi yuktvā evam ātmānam mad parāyaṇaḥ bhoktāram yajña tapasām sarva loka maheśvaram suhṛdam sarva bhūtānām jñātvā mām śāntim ṛcchati iti 
NKA_5.90	 iti evam śruti nīti samplava jalaiḥ bhūyobhiḥ ākṣālite yeṣām na āspadam ādadhā asi hṛdaye te śaula sāra āśayāḥ kintu prastuta vipratīpa vidhayaḥ api uccais bhavat cintakāḥ kāle kāruṇika! tvayā eva kṛpayā te bhāvanīyāḥ narāḥ asmākam tu nisarga sundara! cirāt cetaḥ nimagnam tvayī tyaddhā ananda nidhe! tathā api taralam na adya api santṛpyate tad nātha! tvaritam vidhehi karuṇām yena tvad ekāgra tām yāte cetasi na āpnuvāma śataśas yāmyāḥ punar yātanāḥ iti eṣa nīti kusuma añjaliḥ ujjvala śrīḥ yat vāsayet api ca dakṣiṇa vāmakau dvau no vā tatas kim amara īśa guroḥ guruḥ tu prītaḥ astu anena pada pīṭha samarpitenar
